/ /amr-itomahadhenuyanAmarutsitryAdaramanasyasindhuMspr-ishanaiH/ napurohitaMsukhollayabr-iddhakapAlatubinAyabidhutenAsmAna?/ / /gang mtshan bdud rtsi'i dga' ston 'jo ba'i
'od/ /dad gsum yid kyi chu gter la reg pas/ /sngon med phan bde'i rlabs phreng 'phel bgyid pa/ /rnam 'dren ri bong can des bdag skyongs shig /

gzod nas thabs dang shes rab rnal 'byor gyis/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i rgyal sar 'dzegs zin kyang / /'jam dpal dbyangs dang kun tu bzang po ltar/ /'gro ba sgrol slad rnam 'phrul
bsam mi khyab/ /de las dam pa'i grib bsil dang ldan zhing / /bsngags 'os me tog rab tu mdzes 'bar bas/ /'gro la 'dod rgu ster ba'i dpag bsam shing / /gangs ljongs bsod
nams bye ba'i mgron du khug /gang de'i rnam par dkar ba'i phrin las kyi/ /cha shas rer yang ngo mtshar 'bum g.yo ba/ /de kun srid zhi'i smra ba ji snyed pa/ /gcig tu tshogs
te brjod kyang bri ba med/ /'on te rgya mtsho che las dag byed rgyun/ /cung zad blangs pas dri ma 'khrud pa ltar/ /de bzhin dam pa'i yon tan srid pa na/ /rnyed par dka'
'di cha tsam gleng bar bgyi/ /spyi don gsum pa bdag cag rnams kyi 'dren pa dam pa khams gsum gyi mgon po/ nyan rang thams cad kyi bla ma/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
gtso bo/ dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho spro ba dang sdud pa'i byed po/ rigs thams cad kyi khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje 'chang chen po dang dbyer ma mchis pa mtshan brjod par dka'
ba don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na dpal e waM chos ldan gyi mkhan rabs lnga bcu pa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po bkra shis grags pa'i
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes yongs su grags pa'i snyan grags kyi dri bzhon nam mkha'i mtha' dang mngon par 'grogs pa 'di nyid kyi sku gsung thugs kyi rnam par thar pa
yongs su rdzogs pa ni/ dus gsum gyi rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa rnams kyis kyang ji bzhin du bsnyad par dka' na/ bdag cag so so skye bo 'ching ba kun dang ldan pa rnams kyis
ni smra ba lta ga la zhig /de lta na'ang sems can drang

pa'i thabs kyi khyad par la gzigs te re zhig bdag cag mi rnams kyi skal ba dang bstun te thun mong pa'i mdzad pa ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul mdo tsam zhig gleng bar bya ste/ de
la bdun/ thog mar shing sA la chen po lta bu'i rigs su sku'i skye ba bzhes nas gzhon nu rol rtsed mdzad pa'i tshul/ gzhan dag bstan pa la 'jug pa'i go rim bstan pa'i ched
du bslab pa rin po che'i sgor zhugs te thos bsam sgom gsum ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ bstan pa'i bdag po chen por mnga' gsol nas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don ji ltar
mdzad pa'i tshul/ slar yang gnam bskos gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang pa chen pos chen por 'os pa'i mtshan dang yo byad kyis chen po'i go sar mnga' gsol nas rnam par dkar
ba'i phrin las ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ gsung las skyes pa'i bstan 'dzin gyi slob ma ji tsam byon pa'i tshul/ sdom pa gsum la gces spras su mdzad cing nyams su bzhes pa
la brten nas nyams rtogs ji ltar 'khrungs pa'i tshul/ mthar rtag 'dzin can dang le lo can rnams chos la bskul ba'i slad du gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos dbyings su bsdus kyang
sems can gyi don rgyun mi 'chad pa'i tshul lo/ /de'i dang po ni/ mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam par 'phrul pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang po'i zhal snga nas
mdzad pa'i rje 'di'i rnam thar dang bstun pa'i gsol 'debs byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i chu gter zhes bya ba las/ dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang dbang gdul bya rnams/ /rnal 'byor zab
mo'i lam gyis rjes gzung phyir/ /'jam dpal ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i skur ston pa/ /rnam 'dren bzang po'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /zab gsal gnyis med chos sku'i ngang nyid las/
yan lag bdun ldan longs sku'i rnam rol ni/ /gang 'dul sprul pa'i sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i gar/ /dam pa'i

rigs su 'khrungs la gsol ba 'debs/ /gzhon nu nyid nas nges 'byung snying rje sogs/ /theg chen rigs kyi nus pa yongs rdzogs pas/ /bsngags 'os yon tan bye ba'i snang ba yis/
/grags pa'i utpal rgyas der gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar te/ de'ang ji skad du 'phags pa chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dbyer med pa bstan pa'i mdo las/ khams gsum
du mtshams sbyor ba mi byed pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i shes pa ma yin gyi/ sems can rnams yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir bsam bzhin du skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa ni byang
chub sems dpa'i shes pa yin no/ /zhes dang / gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan pa las/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus brtsams pa rnams ni 'khor
ba la yongs su skyo ba'i blo skye bar mi 'gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sems can yongs su smin par bgyi ba'i slad du 'khor ba la phan yon du blta
ba lags kyi/ mya ngan las 'das pa la ni de lta ma yin no/ /bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sems can gyi don la brtson pa lags so/ /zhes bka' stsal pa ltar/ bdag
nyid chen po rnams ni zhi ba mya ngan las 'das pa'i bde ba la gzhar yang mi chags par/ ji ltar padmo'i tshal du bung ba 'jug pa bzhin du sems can rnams la rjes su brtse
ba'i sgo nas srid pa yongs su gzung ba la rtse gcig tu gzhol ba chos nyid yin pa ltar/ bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa yon tan rin po che'i phung por gyur pa 'dis
kyang gdul bya 'dul ba'i thabs la gzigs te chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa'i pho brang nas/ sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ngor longs
spyod rdzogs pa'i sku dang / gdul bya thun mong ba rnams kyi snang ngor

mchog dang mchog ma yin pa'i sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgo nas sems can gyi don mdzad pa las/ 'dir skabs su bab pa bdag cag skal ba dman pa rnams kyi don du so so skye
bo'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi rnam par rol par bzhed de/ de'ang 'di'i 'khrungs pa'i yul ni/ byang chub kyi snying po 'phags yul rdo rje gdan las byang phyogs su dpag tshad
brgya bgrod pa'i gnas/ gtsang la stod gram pa dpal ldan sa skya zhes yongs su grags pa dang ha cang mi ring ba'i yul/ yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e waM
chos ldan dang khad nye ba'i sa'i thig le rtse na rgya mtsho gling zhes par/ yab mkhan chen nam mkha' bsam 'grub kyi rus dbon padma don grub ces bya ba bya ba dang bya ba
ma yin pa'i blang dor la mkhas pa/ pho rtsal sna dgu la sogs pa'i stobs kyi pha rol tu son zhing / rigs gzugs longs spyod kyis mngon par sgeg pa de dang / yum kha na ma
tho ba med pa'i rigs su 'khrungs shing ngo tsha dang khrel yod kyis brgyan pa/ dad pa dang snying rje dang gtong ba la sogs pa ya rabs kyi yon tan mang pos mdzes pa padma
bu khrid ces bya ba ste/ yab yum de gnyis la sras drug tsam yod pa las/ phu bo gnyis kyi 'og mar gyur pa de ni bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa yon tan ma lus pa'i gter
mdzod du gyur pa 'di nyid yin te/ de'ang yum gyi lhums su zhugs pa'i dus su yab yum la rmi ltas bzang ba la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas mang du byung zhing / de nas ji
srid phyir ma btsas kyi bar du'ang yum gyi lus yang zhing zo mdog bde ba dang / rang bzhin gyis dge ba la spro zhing ting nge 'dzin ngang gis skye ba la sogs pa dge mtshan
mtha' dag mngon du gyur bzhin pa'i ngang nas/ rab byung bcu gsum pa'i nang gses legs sbyar gyi skad du sa mya zhes pa zhi ba ste rgya rtsis

pa'i lugs kyis mo bya'i lor yum la gnod pa med cing bde ba dang / 'byor pa dang / lo legs pa la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dang mthun par bltams so/ /de
ltar bltams pa'i khye'u de ni gzugs bzang zhing lta bas chog mi shes pa/ skyes bu chen po'i mtshan dang ldan pa zhig ste/ yab yum rnams kyis mtshan padma phrin las zhes
bya bar gsol to/ /de nas na tshod dang mthun pa'i kha zas kyi khyad par bzang ngo cog gis rdzing bu'i nang gi padmo bzhin du rim gyis bskyed bsrings te cung zad mno shes
pa na'ang / gzhon nu de ni sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams la lhag par bya ba byas shing dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i stobs kyis rigs kyi yon tan khyad par can sad de/ yab yum dang
rgan pa rnams la gus shing / dman pa rnams la rjes su brtse ba dang / bzhin 'dzum pa dang / gsong por smra ba dang / khro ba mi mnga' ba dang / gtsang sbra che ba la
sogs pa 'gro ba rnams kyi yid kyi brtan pa cig car du 'phrog par nus pa zhig yod ces thos la/ khyad par du'ang khyim na gnas pa ni dug can gyi zas bzhin du sdug bsngal thams
cad kyi 'byung gnas su gzigs te/ rab tu byung ba la skom pa chu 'dod pa lta bu'i sgo nas zhal nas kyang / nga btsun pa byed pa yin kho na gsungs shing / dgun grang ba'i
skabs su'ang yab yum rnams kyis pags pa'i na bza' zhig bzo bar mdzad kyang / de la thugs skrag pa'i snang bas gtan nas mi bzhes pa dang / des mtshon pa'i rgyun gyi na
bza' rnams kyang dmar po 'ba' zhig las dkar po dang khra bo'i rigs mi gsol ba dang / gzhan yang tha mal pa'i rtsed mo dang 'du 'dzi'i rigs la mi dgyes shing / de'i stobs
kyis byis pa gzhan dang lhan cig byon pa'i tshe'ang / thog mar rtse mo'i rnam pa cung zad re mdzad nas/ slar rang nyid su'ang med pa'i sa phyogs dben pa dag tu

phebs nas bzhugs pa dang / rgyun par chos zhig byed pa'i dus nam 'ong snyam pa'i dgongs pa kho na rgyun chags su 'khrungs pa la brten nas dgung lo drug pa shing pho stag gi
lor/ yab yum gyi skyel ma la sogs pa'i bdag po'i rkyen la brten te sa la spyod pa'i 'og min gnyis pa dpal e waM chos ldan gyi bla brang thar pa rtser phebs/ rang nyid kyi
gcen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi zhal snga nas ye ge'i phyi mo nas brtsams te/ klog la sogs pa bka' khrid zhus pa tsam gyis tshegs med du mkhyen/ de
nas bzung ste e waM rang du bzhugs/ skabs skabs su yab yum rnams kyi rtsar yang lan kha shas phebs/ khyad par dgung lo bcu pa sa rta lor mdo khams nas khu bo mkhan chen
rdo rje 'chang chen pos dbus gtsang gi ljongs su bsnyen bkur stob par phyag mdzod yon tan rgya mtsho dpon 'khor rnams gtong gnang mdzad pa bzhin bar chad med par 'dir 'byor/
khong la khu bo mkhan chen gyis rje 'di dge rgan zhig gi rtsar bzhag na legs tshul gyi zhal mngags stsal 'dug pa ltar/ dgung grangs bcu gcig pa don grub kyi lo'i hor
zla lnga pa'i nang / drung khang du mkhan sangs rgyas grags pa'i mchod dpon bsod nams lhun grub kyi rtsar byon/ der lo gcig dang zla ba brgyad bzhugs/ de'i bar la e waM
pa'i chos spyod phyi nang yongs su rdzogs pa dang / ngan song sbyong rgyud nas bshad pa'i kun rig gi cho ga dang / dze tA ri'i lugs kyi tshe dpag med lha dgu dang / mi 'khrugs
pa lha dgu dang / rnam rgyal ma lha dgu dang / birWa pa'i lugs kyi gshed dmar lha lnga dang / kye rdo rje man ngag lugs lha dgu rnams kyi cho ga cha lag dang bcas pa
dang / dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i rgyud bshad kyi sngon 'gro tshul gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan dang / rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs

pa ljon shing mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan bcas dang / kye rdo rje'i rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa rnams thugs 'dzin mthar phyin par mdzad de e waM bla brang gzhung du rgyugs
'bul bar mdzad pa yin no/ /srid pa'i 'byor pa ring spangs kyang / /brtse bas gzhan don nyid la 'jug /yid can rnams kyi khur 'di yis/ /rgyal rnams thog ma nyid nas lci/
/de slad rnam par 'phrul pa yi/ /thabs ni gang dang gang zhig gis/ /'gro 'di ji ltar dbugs dbyung zhing / /snying rje'i bsam gtan kho nar g.yengs/ /smra ba'i nyin byed
phal che ba/ /nub ring ngal bso brten pa'i tshe/ /rgyal kun ye shes zla ba'i gzugs/ /ljongs 'dir 'char ba'i sbyor ba brtsams/ /rgyal ba rnams kyi ye shes kyang / /gang du
chags par gyur pa'i yul/ /'dod rgu'i ri mo rnam bkra ba/ /su yis bris pa yong mi shes/ /de lta'i yul du smin legs ma'i/ /lang tsho'i me tog 'bar ba'i dbus/ /dge mtshan snang
ba brgya phrag dang / /lhan cig srid pa yongs su bzung / /thabs kyi ngo bo 'jam dpal dang / /shes rab rang bzhin dbyangs lha mo/ /rgyal ba'i gzugs sku bskyed pa'i phyir/
/yab yum zol gyis 'ong min nam/ /de nas mdzes sdug 'khyil pa yi/ /yid 'ong lha mo'i chu gter las/ /gzugs sku'i padmo 'khrungs pa ni/ /gser gyi mchod sdong 'bar ba bzhin/
/de mthong mi yi yul du ci/ /mtho ris na yang rnyed dka' ba'i/ /dpal 'di gang nas 'ong ba zhes/ /'gro ba'i mig ni zum ma gyur/ /shin tu dag pa'i mtshan dpe ni/ /nyin
las nyin bzhin gsal gyur pa/ /de tshe lus can ngo mtshar bas/ /gzhon nu'i gsang sngags 'ba' zhig bzla/ /zhi zhing dul ba'i dri bzang po / /thog ma med nas gang sbyar ba/
/mtshan dpe'i me tog dgod tsam nas/ /yid can brtan pa 'phrog la chas/ /khyod kyi nges par 'byung ba'i

spyan/ /'jig rten gsum na gsal ba yis/ /yul gyi dug dang rab ldan pa'i/ /khyim 'di sbrul nag khros par gzigs/ /de tshe srid pa'i sman pa yis/ /chos kyi sman chen sbyar ba'i
zhing / /e wa~M byang chub dga' tshal du/ /zhabs zung gser gyi padma bkod/ /skye med yi ge dam pa'i mchog /gzod ma nyid nas brnyes zin kyang / /da dung slob pa'i zol sbyor
gyi/ /sgyu 'dis bdag cag rmongs par byas// //spyi don gnyis pa gzhan dag bstan pa la 'jug pa'i go rim bstan pa'i ched du bslab pa rin po che'i sgor zhugs te thos bsam
sgom gsum ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rje 'di'i rnam thar gsol 'debs byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i
chu gter las/ mkhas grub chen po bsod nams dpal 'byor mdun/ /thun bstan yongs su rdzogs pa'i sgor zhugs nas/ /rdo rje 'chang dngos nam mkha'i mtshan can gyi/ /thugs kyi
sras su gyur la gsol ba 'debs/ /gzhan yang ris med bshes gnyen mchog rnams las/ /mang du gsan dang bsam pa'i mthar son nas/ /rtse gcig lam bzang bsgoms pa'i bdud rtsi yis/
/grub gnyis pad dkar bzhad der gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi don zhib tu bshad pa la gnyis te/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che'i sgor zhugs pa'i tshul dang /
zhugs pa'i rten des thos bsam sgom gsum ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul lo/ /de'i dang po ni/ ji skad du mdo las/ tshul khrims la brten tshul khrims la gnas na/ /rim gyis 'phags
pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag /yang dag ji lta ba bzhin rtogs par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam du bgrod pa la them skas kyi dang po lta
bu med du mi rung ba'i gzhi chen po ni lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa nyid yin zhing /

der ma zad dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyang tshul khrims kyi bslab pa 'di kho na la brten nas byang chub kyi bdud rtsi mngon du bzhes pa yin la/ rgyu mtshan de'i phyir
na rab tu byung ba'i brtul zhugs myur du len par bya'o snyam pa'i rgyu'i kun slong zla ba 'bum phrag 'char pa'i gzi brjid kyis kyang mtshon par mi nus pa thugs kyi dbus
su shar te/ dgung grangs bcu gsum pa lcags bya hor zla gnyis pa'i gza' skar mchog tu dge ba'i nyin/ brtan mkhas kyi yon tan gnyis dang ldan pa'i mtshungs med chos kyi
rje mkhas grub ngag dbang dam chos pa'i zhal snga nas kyi mkhan po dang / mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan mang pos mngon par mdzes pa byams pa bsod nams dpal 'byor pas
las kyi slob dpon la sogs pa mdor na dad pa'i dge 'dun bcu'i dbus su rje 'di dang / dung 'bud sprul sku dpal ldan bkra shis dang / khang gsar rje drung bstan 'dzin bzang
po gsum gyis dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa len pa sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas khyim pa'i rtags dang cha lugs mtha' dag bdud rtsis bkrus pa'i dri ma bzhin du bsal ba dang / rab tu
byung ba'i rtags dang cha lugs thams cad ngang pas chu las 'o ma len pa bzhin du yang dag par blangs te tshigs snga ma dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa legs par bzhes
par mdzad do/ /dus de nyid nas bzung ste dge tshul gyi bslab pa'i gzhi bcu char gtogs dang bcas pa thams cad kyang srung sdom gyi ra ba las nam yang mi 'da' bar mdzad
pa yin no/ /de skabs rje 'di dang / rje 'di'i sku mched chung ba tshe dbang rdo rje gnyis ka bla ma mdzad rtsis yin pa la/ de rjes khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen
po de nyid mdo khams nas e wa~M du byon pa'i skabs/ rje 'di la byis pa che ba 'di btsun 'dog pa zhig 'dug pas bla ma byas/ chung ba 'di grwa pa zhig byas te

phyag mdzod lta bu byas na legs pa 'dra gsungs pa dang / khyad par khu bo mkhan chen de nyid kyi drung du rje 'di sku mched gnyis char gyi mtshan zhig zhu bar mdzad pa'i tshe'ang
/ nged kyis bla ma la bla ma'i ming dang / grwa pa la grwa pa'i ming gdags kyi gsungs nas/ rje 'di la rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po dang / gcung tshe dbang rdo rje
la nor ldan shes rab bzang po zhes 'dogs par mdzad do/ /de lta bu'i rdo rje'i bka' de ni dus gsum thams cad thogs med du mkhyen pa'i gsung khyad par can 'jig rten na tshad
mar gyur pa yin na'ang / slar yang 'gro ba rnams yid ches bskyed pa'i slad du/ de skabs su rgyal khams bskor ba'i rnal 'byor pa ston chen zer ba me long la bltas te de'i
nang du ji ltar shar ba bzhin lung ston par byed pa zhig sleb par/ de la byis pa 'di gnyis sus bla ma byas na legs me long nang du ltos shig ces bka' stsal pa na/ des
kyang de bzhin du bltas te ji ltar bka' stsal pa ltar rje 'di chos kyi bag chags shin tu mthug pas bla ma dang / chung ba 'di las byed cig byed par 'os so zhes gsol pa na/
des kyang ji lta ba bzhin mthong bar gzigs te bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'di gzod ma nyid nas srid pa dang zhi ba'i bla mar gyur zin na'ang / slar yang bdag sogs
skal ba dman pa rnams kyi 'dren pa dam par yongs su gzengs bstod par mdzad do/ /da ni 'dir sde tshan gcig pa'i phyir tshigs phyi ma bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i bdud rtsi bzhes
pa'i tshul brjod na/ de'ang thams cad mkhyen pa'i grong khyer du 'jug par 'dod pa'i skyes bu blo gros dang ldan pa rnams kyis ni 'khor ba dngos kyi gnyen po rnam par
mi rtog pa'i shes rab bskyed pa'i thabs la 'bad dgos pa yin la/ de lta bu'i shes rab de'ang dmigs pa rtse gcig pa'i ting nge 'dzin la ltos la/ de'ang tshul khrims rnam par
dag

pa la rag las shing / de la'ang nang gses su so sor thar pa rigs brgyad yod pa'i nang nas mchog tu gyur pa ni dge slong gi sdom pa nyid yin par gsungs te/ lung las/ sangs rgyas
bstan pa rin chen sgron/ /'bar ba'i snod ni dka' thub can/ /ngur smrig 'dzin pa shAkya'i sras/ /dge slong rnams ni yin phyir ro/ /zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /rgyu mtshan
de bas na rang nyid kyang yongs su rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos por bsgrub par bzhed nas dgung grangs nyer gcig pa sa mo sbrul gyi lor/ e waM bla brang gzhung du mkhan
po bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag mtshungs med chos kyi rje mtshan brjod par dka' ba/ don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te 'phags pa nye bar 'khor gnyis pa byams pa bsod
nams dpal 'byor bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / dgag sgrub gnang gsum gyi bslab bya mtha' dag tshul bzhin du ston pa la bsnyengs
pa mi mnga' ba'i las kyi slob dpon dpal ldan chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa dang / gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon dpal ldan chos 'phel ba dang / dus go ba dpal 'byor rgya mtsho
ba dang / grogs dan pa kun dga' dpal 'byor la sogs pa mdor na gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa bcu phrag gcig gi dbus su rje 'di dang / khang gsar zhabs drung rin po che blo
gros rgyal mtshan pa dang / zhe'u zhing skyong gi bla ma dang gsum gyis mngon du gyur pa bcus sdom pa skye ba'i rgyu tshogs thams cad tshang ba'i sgo nas gzhan la gnod pa
gzhi dang bcas pa spong ba'i sems pa mtshungs ldan dang bcas pa so so thar pa'i sdom pa mngon du gyur par mdzad do/ /dus de nyid nas brtsams te ltung ba sde lnga char gtogs
dang bcas pa tshul bzhin du bsrungs pas nyes byas kyi dri ma phra zhing phra bas kyang

ma gos shing / bslab bya'i gtso bo gyur pa bsten bya 'tsho ba dang / bsrung bya tshul khrims dang / nyams len spyod pa dang / rtogs don lta ba ste rnam dag rnam pa bzhi la
gus pa dang bag yod pa'i thabs kyis tshul bzhin du bslabs pa sngon gyi 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po u pa li la sogs pa dang tshul mtshungs par bzhugs pa yin no/ /gang gi tshe
skyes bu dam pa 'di rgyal ba'i bstan pa la zhugs shing bslab pa rin po che rnams zhal gyis bzhes pa de'i tshe/ nag po'i phyogs su gyur pa'i bdud kyi rigs ni ngo zum gnag
cing shin tu 'grib par gyur la/ gang dag dkar po'i phyogs la dga' ba'i lha rnams ni/ snga na med pa'i spro ba'i chu gter chen po snying gi dbus nas 'phyur ba la brten nas
'jig rten na 'di lta bu'i bde legs 'byung ba'i rgyu'i gtso bo ci zhig snyam du legs par brtags pas/ ji zhig tsam na dam pa 'di rab tu byung bas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa
dang lha'i ris thams cad yongs su rgyas par gyur pa'i ltas su shes nas/ phan tshun gcig gis gcig la sbran te dga' ba dang ca co'i sgra chen po 'og min gyi bar du grag par
gyur pa ni yid ches pa'i lung dang / rjes su dpag pa'i rig pas kyang rtogs par nus pa yin no/ /byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa bzhes pa'i tshul ni/ 'di ltar mtha' yas pa'i
sems can thams cad ma rig pa'i ling thog gis bsgribs te/ dge ba'i lam stegs mtha' dag nyams par byas pa la brten nas 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho chen por rang dbang med par 'khor
zhing sdug bsngal gyis gzir bar gzigs te/ 'di lta bu'i sems can thams cad kyi khur ni bdag nyid gcig pus khyer te srid pa'i 'jigs pa thams cad zhi bar bgyid pa ma gtogs
'di dag gi bde ba'i rgyu gzhan med do snyam pa'i nye bar len pa'i rgyu'i gtso bo lhag pa'i

bsam pa rnam par dag pa thugs la 'khrungs nas/ lhan cig byed pa'i rkyen du gyur pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen khu bo mkhan chen byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'
'chi med dang / gcen byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gnyis char gyi drung nas/ brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis las 'ongs pa'i sems bskyed
kyi sdom pa bzhes te/ de phyin chad nam mkha'i snying po'i mdo las gsungs pa'i rtsa ba'i ltung ba bcu bzhi dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang / sdom pa nyi shu pa sogs
las gsungs pa'i pham 'dra'i nyes byas bzhi dang / yan lag gi nyes byas zhe drug la sogs pa mdor na bslab bya'i gnas mtha' dag la srung sdom tshul bzhin du mdzad pas nyes
pa phra zhing phra bas kyang ma gos pa yin no/ /der ma zad pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi sgo nas dge ba'i chos thams cad yongs su sdud pa dang bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi'i sgo
nas sems can rnams yongs su smin par mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ bdag nyid chen po kun tu bzang po dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs la sogs pa'i rnam thar la co 'dri ba bzhin mdzad do/
/rig pa 'dzin pa sngags kyi sdom pa'i dbang du byas na/ 'og nas 'byung ba ltar gyi rgyud ma smin pa smin par byed pa'i dbang bskur ba legs par gsan te/ snang ba'i dngos
po thams cad lha dang ye shes kyi ngo bor byin gyis brlabs pa la brten nas dbang las byung ba'i ye shes brjod bral lhan cig skyes pa don gyi sdom pa thob par mdzad cing
/ de las byung ba'i rtsa ba dang yan lag gis bsdus pa'i dam tshig thams cad srog gi dbang po las kyang gces par bsrungs pas nyes pa'i dri ma shin tu phra bas kyang reg pa'i
gnas skabs mi srid pa yin no/ /thams cad mkhyen pa brnyes zin kyang / /thams cad sgrol ba'i ded dpon du/ /thams cad

gzigs pa'i bka' lung gis/ /thams cad mgon du mnga' rab gsol/ /e ma rgyal rnams tshul khrims kyi/ /nor bu'i rkang stegs la brten nas/ /thar pa dam pa'i khang bzang du/ /gshegs
pa'i shul lam mtshon pa'i phyir/ /rang nyid so sor thar pa'i sgor/ /zhugs pa'i mi smra brtul zhugs kyis/ /skal bzang mtho ris chas pa la/ /lam de 'di nyid yin par ston/
/mchog rnams rang gi spyod yul du/ /zhugs la gdung ba skyed byed pa'i/ /'khrul pa'i gdon 'di yid srubs la/ /bsod nams min pas nye bar gnas/ /bzhin la 'dzum pa'i zla ris
kyi/ /dog pa mu tig 'od bkod pas/ /lha rnams gang gi grags pa yi/ /spring yig srid rtse'i bar du sgrogs/ /gzhan gyi bde ba bsgrub pa la/ /bdud rtsi bzhin du don gnyer ba/
/sman mdzad rnams kyi bsam pa gang / /tshangs pa yis kyang rnyed par dka'/ /de slad byang chub sems gnyis kyi/ /gser gyi khri 'phang la 'dzegs te/ /thar pa mchog gi rgyal
srid la/ /'gro 'di ji ltar dgod ces dgongs/ /gang zhig rig pa'i sngags kyis ni/ /dngos kun lha dang ye shes su/ /sgyur byed gsang ba'i mig 'phrul la/ /mngon 'dod spyan
gyi zur mda' lhung / /de tshe rig 'dzin sdom pa ni/ /rlung gi gshog can la zhon nas/ /rdo rje 'dzin sar bgrod la yang / /thogs med glog gi rnam 'phrul bzhin/ /nyes kun bcom
pa'i bdag nyid la/ /slar yang glags lta rtsom byed pa'i/ /bdag gi rmongs pa 'di ci zhes/ /sdom pa'i mi mthun phyogs rnams song // //gnyis pa zhugs pa'i rten des thos
bsam sgom gsum ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul la gsum ste/ thog mar e wa~M rang du bzhugs nas gsan bsam sgom gsum ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ de rjes mdo khams su byon nas bstan
'gro'i don dang thos bsam ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ slar yang

mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i slad du dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du bsnyen bkur rgya cher bstabs pa dang nyan bshad sgom gsum ji ltar
mdzad pa'i tshul lo/ /de'i dang po ni/ 'jig rten na blang dor gyi gnas phyin ci ma log par rtogs par byed pa'i thabs ni/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen la brten te thos pa byed pa
nyid yin la/ gang dag thos bsam gyi rgyu sngon du ma song bar bsam gtan la mnyam par bzhag pa tsam gyis ni thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang thob par ma gsungs
te/ 'phags pa dkon mchog brtsegs pa las/ gang dge ba'i bshes gnyen la brten par byed pa de ni thos par 'gyur ro/ /thos nas rab tu shes so/ /shes nas nan tan byed do/ /zhes
dang / ji ltar mun pas khyab bsgribs pa/ /khyim du zhugs par gyur na ni/ yod par gyur pa'i gzugs rnams kyang / /mig gis mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du ni 'di la
yang / /la la'i mig dag skyes gyur kyang / /dge ba dang ni sdig pa'i chos/ /ma thos par ni shes mi 'gyur/ /zhes sogs dang / gang dag byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi chos
kyi rnam grangs 'di ma thos/ 'phags pa'i chos 'dul ba ma thos par ting nge 'dzin tsam gyis dga' ba rnyed pas nga rgyal gyi dbang gis che ba'i nga rgyal du lhung ba de
dag ni skye ba dang rga ba sogs nas/ sdug bsngal gyi phung po las yongs su mi thar te/ zhes sogs kyi bar du gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /de bas na rgyal ba'i bstan pa la zhugs
pa rnams kyi mngon par rtogs pa ni thos bsam sgom gsum rim pa can du nyams su len pa nyid yin no zhes gdul bya rnams la gdams pa'i slad du rang nyid kyang de'i rjes su slob
par bzhed de/ de'ang dge tshul gyi sdom pa gsan ma thag pa nas bzung ste/ gcen byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi zhabs pad bsten te thar rtse

rang gi lha khang khag rnams la yon chab 'bul ba dang / phyag dar bya ba dang / gcen byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin par gsol ja 'dren pa dang / gzhan yang phar sprod tshur len
la sogs pa thar rtse rang gi bya ba che phra mtha' dag mdzad bzhin pa'i ngang nas sa paNDi ta chen pos mdzad pa'i bstan bcos sdom gsum rab dbye dang / dkon mchog lhun
grub kyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras kyi khrid yig snang gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan dang / rgyud gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan rnams dgung grangs bcu dgu tshun chad du thugs
la bzung nas e waM bla brang gzhung du rgyugs 'bul ba sogs grub par mdzad pa dang / de'ang tha mal pa'i byis pa ltar gzhan gyis dbang med du bskul ba la ma ltos par/ rje
'di ni sku na chung ngu'i skabs kyang phyag dpe cung zad re gzigs rgyu byung tshe thugs dgyes pa'i zhal ras padmo 'dzum pa lta bu'i sgo nas rgyun par dpe cha 'di rkyang
pa zhig bltas nas sdod rgyu byung na ci ma rung snyam pa kho na thugs rgyud la 'khrungs pa zhig yod ces bka' stsal pa dang / gzhan yang 'du 'dzi la mi dges pa'i stobs kyis
thugs brel med pa'i skabs kyang dben pa kho nar zhugs pa zhig yod pa yin no/ /de skabs shig tu phyag g.yas pa rtsa dkar gyis shin tu snyun gzer che bar gyur te/ nub mo
gzims kyang cher mi 'ong ba zhig byung rung / snyun zug la mi 'dzems par lha khang khag rnams la phyag dar dang / sku 'dra'i rdul phyis sogs la shin tu brtson par mdzad
pas nub gcig mnal lam du/ phyag g.yas pa'i sor mo'i gseb nas sbrul lta bu'i sems can mtho gang tsam zhig phyir 'thon pa'i snang ba byung ba dang lhan cig snyun gzhi'ang
legs par dwangs pa yin no zhes thos so/ /khyad par dgung lo bcu gsum pa'i nang nyams dang rtogs pa'i dbang phyug phan khang zhabs drung rin po che dpal ldan rin chen chos
mdzod kyi drung

nas ma ti lugs kyi 'jam dpal dkar po'i rjes su gnang ba dang / dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje dam
can chos kyi rgyal po lha bcu gsum gyi rjes su gnang ba rnams gsan pa dang / gsang sngags snga 'gyur 'dzin pa snying ri khri chen rin po che padma bdud 'dul mthu stobs
rgyal mtshan pa'i drung nas las 'brel lugs kyi gza' bdud kyi srog dbang dang / de dang 'brel bar gza'i byad 'grol dug dbyung dang bcas pa dang / byad 'grol gser lde sogs
chos 'brel tsam gsan pa dang / chos kyi spyan ras bkra ba 'dam thog bla ma rin chen grags pa las grub chen a bha yas phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs shing yar lung lo tsA ba grags
pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'i sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang brgya dang zhe gcig yongs su rdzogs pa dang / de'i rjes gnang bya tshul thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i yig
cha'i lung bcas gsan pa dang / dgung lo bcu gnyis chu khyi lor sa skya nas 'jam mgon dbang sdud snying po dbus phebs bskyangs pa'i mar lam ngor du phebs/ bla khag thams
cad kyis kyang 'bul bsnyen gya nom pa bstabs shing / rje 'dis kyang bya rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo thub pa gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba dang
/ mnga' bdag nyang nyi ma 'od zer gyis zab gter nas spyan drangs pa'i gu ru drag dmar gyi dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa bcas gsan pa dang / khyad par dgung grangs bcu bdun
pa shing glang hor zla dgu pa'i nang mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med kyang mdo khams nas yar byon/ rje 'di'ang gzhis rtse bar phebs bsur byon
pa dang / gzhan yang bla khag khang tshan dang bcas pa'i phebs bsu'i tshogs dang bcas te e wa~M du phebs/ dus de nyid nas bzung ste khu bo mkhan chen

rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid mdo khams su ma byon gyi bar du zhabs pad 'bral ba med par gtsug gi rgyan du bsten cing / ci gsungs dang du len pa'i kun spyod kyis mnyes par
byas te chos kyi bdud rtsi ji ltar gsol ba'i tshul yang / dgung grangs bco brgyad pa me stag lo'i hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i yar tshes nas bzung ste bka' chos kyi dbu 'dzugs
par mdzad de/ de'ang chos kyi rnam grangs mtha' dag mdo sngags gnyis su 'dus pa'i nang nas ches mchog tu gyur pa gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i skor la/ rgyud sde rin po
che rnam pa bzhir bzhugs pa'i nang tshan dang po bya ba'i rgyud la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo sman bla mched bdun gyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha thar
paN gyis mdzad pa'i lung / sangs rgyas klu dbang rgyal po lha lnga'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub skor 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs bcom ldan ral
gris mdzad pa/ bstod pa rong ston gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub rjes ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa/ char 'bebs dpal ldan chos skyong gis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / jo
bo rje nas brgyud pa'i thub pa gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung / gsang ba spyi rgyud nas
gsungs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi bdag po rigs gsum spyi'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i yig cha thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i
lung / 'jam dpal dkar po ma ti lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i bstod pa paNDi ta ma tis mdzad pa/ sgrub skor rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus kyis mdzad pa/ sgrub
thabs dang rjes gnang gi yi ge thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ smon lam paNDi ta rig pa'i khu byug gis mdzad par grags pa dang / sbyin sreg sangs rgyas phun tshogs

kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / 'jam dbyangs dang sa paN sbags te sgrub pa'i byin rlabs dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang chos grags dang / tshogs gsog pa kun dga' tshul khrims
kyis mdzad pa'i lung / 'jam dbyangs la bstod pa gang blo ma la brten pa'i 'jam dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po'i rig gtad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi yum 'phags ma
rig pa chen mo'am gza' rnams kyi yum du grags pa gtso 'khor rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bstod pa bstan 'dzin
rdo rje mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma lha dgu'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i bstod pa ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad
pa/ sgrub rjes dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ brgyud 'debs mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa kha skong dang bcas pa/ sbyin sreg dpal ldan don grub kyis
mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / gtsug tor gdugs dkar gyi byad 'grol rmor chen pa'i yig cha'i steng nas lung dang bcas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi khro bo gtsug tor 'bar
ba'i rjes gnang byad 'grol dang bcas pa dang / de'i yig cha zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung / khro rgyal mi g.yo ba dkar po'i rjes su gnang ba dang /
de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung / bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil
dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa/ thar rtse paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor dang / rab gnas bya tshul/ sbyin sreg sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa/
/tshe sgrub kyi gdams pa zab mo thun mong

ma yin pa sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN
gyis mdzad pa/ de'i lhan thabs sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / grub chen mi tra dzo ki'i lugs kyi tshe dpag med dkar po'i rjes su gnang ba dang
/ de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub dang zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ khro phu lo tsA bas mdzad pa'i 'chi ba slu ba'i man ngag /zhu chen gyis mdzad pa'i
kha 'bar ma dkar mo'i 'chi slu dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung dang / padma'i rigs kyi bdag po 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal gtso rkyang gi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha dkon
mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ smyung gnas kyi cho ga zhu chen gyis mdzad pa bcas kyi lung dang / skyer sgang lugs kyi thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum pa'i rjes su gnang
ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ las kha tshar sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa/ thugs rje chen po dang phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug tu nyams su len
tshul dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung dang / 'phags pa seng ge sgra'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ gdon 'grol
gyi cho ga thar paN dang / sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa/ seng ge sgra'i char 'bebs 'dam thog bstan 'dzin rdo rjes mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / padma'i
rigs kyi yum sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i tshe khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun dang / de'i
lhan thabs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i yig cha bcas kyi steng nas nyams khrid zab mo yongs su rdzogs pa dang / sgrol dkar sgrub thabs slob dpon
ngag gi dbang

phyug grags pas mdzad pa'i 'chi bdag slu ba'i rtog pa nas phyung ba paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba ba ri'i 'gyur/ sgrol dkar sgrub thabs/ gtor ma/ bum chog/ srung
'khor bcas kyi yi ge /bris pa'i srung 'khor gyi yi ge /bar chad zhi bar byed pa/ ltas ngan g.yang du blang ba'i man ngag /ngag gi byad 'grol gyi yi ge slob dpon padma nag
pos mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i sprul pa ce spyang sngon mo'i srung ba/ ce spyang sngon mo'i lam srung gi gsal byed/ rjes gnang gi skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i lo rgyus mdzad byang
med pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang bstod pa dang bcas pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i sgrol dkar rjes
gnang dang / de'i dmigs rim skyabs yul zhing khams ma/ sbyin sreg bklags chog tu bkod pa/ dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang / sgrol dkar sbyin sreg
mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung / jo bo nas brgyud pa'i sgrol ma nyi shu rtsa gcig gi rjes su gnang ba dang / sgrol ma'i phyag
'tshal nyer gcig gi sgrub thabs yig rnying dang / de'i rjes gnang gi chings mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i sgrol
ma maNDal bzhi chog dang bcas pa'i lung / bla med du gtogs kyang 'dir mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad kyi lung blang dgos pa dang sde tshan gcig pa'i phyir bya rgyud du bzhag pa
gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i man ngag rmi lam brtag thabs shin tu zab pa lha mo shra
ma Na'i sgrub thabs kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal dang / sa chen kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / padma'i rigs kyi khro bo rta mgrin lcags ral can zla
rgyal

lugs su grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub thabs zla ba rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ nad gso ba/ steng gdon gzir ba/ lus srung ba/ ser ba srung ba/ phyir zlog pa/
rjes gnang gi yi ge rnying pa/ thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub rjes rnams kyi lung / padma'i rigs kyi pho nya mo dbyangs can ma dkar mo'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub
rjes thar paN gyis mdzad pa kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung / rdo rje'i rigs kyi gtso bo slob dpon dze tA ris bkral ba'i mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur
ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ de'i zur 'debs zhu chen gyis mdzad pa/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa rnams kyi
lung / rdo rje'i rigs kyi bdag po phyag rdor gos sngon can 'gro bzang lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba/ rnam 'joms ba ri lugs lha gcig bum gcig gi rjes gnang khrus dang bcas pa
dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung / rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nyar gtogs pa khro bo dme brtsegs sa lugs su grags pa dud ka'i rjes gnang khrus dang
bcas pa/ de'i zhal gdams zab mo sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ rmor chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub rjes khrus chog dang bcas pa/ bsod nams lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i grib mdos bcas kyi
lung / jo bo'i lugs kyi dme brtsegs ljang nag gi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ las tshogs la grib srung ba/ ser ba srung ba/ rims nad srung
ba/ phyugs nad srung ba/ mi lo nad can srung ba/ ra lug la spyang ki srung ba/ 'bras phol lhog pa gso ba/ nad pa'i sngas srung ba/ zhing gi 'bu srung ba/ bang mdzod srung
ba/ 'gong po sreg pa/ dme grib srung thabs dang bcas pa'i lung / rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho

nya mo khro mo dme brtsegs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha 'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i lung / bya rgyud nor can gyi rigs dzaM dkar 'brug zhon lha lnga
jo bo lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags dang / 'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i lung / phyag rdor gos sngon

med byams ldan ma'i bar dang / mkhas

gyi zab

gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lung / gter kha 'og ma gu ru chos dbang gi gter byon phyag rdor gtum po khyung lnga'i rjes su gnang ba dang

gling gter chen gyis mdzad pa 'dod bum las byung ba'i lung / rdo rje nam mkha' lding khyung dmar gyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig rnying gi lung / grwa mngon dbang
phyug 'bar gyi gter byon dzambha la dmar po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i rjes gnang chu sbyin dang bcas pa dang / de'i yig cha sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa/
dge ba'i bshes gnyen nyang ston sgrub pa po'i gter byon thugs rje chen po'i mig 'byed kyi gdams pa dang / de'i gsal byed sngags 'chang bkra shis stobs rgyal gyis mdzad
pa/ gter ston bzang po grags pa'i gter byon gsol 'debs le'u bdun ma dang / ba mkhal smug po'i gter byon gsol 'debs bar chad lam sel rnams kyi lung / gnubs lugs kyi srung
ma legs ldan stag gzhon nag po 'khor bcas kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i gtor chog dang rjes gnang thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ skong ba sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa
bcas dang / gzhan yang sa paNDi ta chen pos mdzad pa'i sdom gsum rab dbye/ lam 'bras kyi phyi nang gsang gsum gyi maNDal dang / snang ba mtha' yas kyi bsgom don/ 'chi kha
ma'i gdams ngag /yan lag bdun pa rnams dang / paN chen shAkya shrIs mdzad par grags pa'i gnas brtan phyag mchod/ byang pa rigs ldan pas mdzad pa'i cho 'phrul smon lam/
dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i yas

gtam dang bsngo ba/ de la dgos pa'i tshigs bcad sangs phun pas bsgrigs pa/ bar do ngo sprod shar khang pas mdzad pa/ 'od dpag med la brten pa'i 'pho ba dkon mchog dpal ldan
pas mdzad pa/ bum gter gyi lag len dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa/ de'i zur 'debs sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa/ 'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i dam
tshig rdo rje'i sgom bzlas dang / bka' bsgo bya tshul thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ brgya bzhi'i cho ga rnams dang / slob dpon padmas mdzad par grags pa'i gser skyems
dang / bdag chen rgya gar bas mdzad pa'i bsang gzhung sogs bsang yig gi skor dang bcas pa'i lung rnams legs par gsan cing / de thams cad kyi phyag len phra mo tshun
chad kyang shin tu mthar phyin par thugs su chud par mdzad pa yin no/ /rje 'di dgung grangs nyi shur son pa rnam byung gi lor khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de
nyid kyang mdo khams kyi bstan 'gro'i don du chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ rje 'dis kyang bde mchog lU nag gi cho ga thugs 'dzin bskyangs te e waM pa'i sgrub mchod du lo bzhi tsam
phebs pa dang / gzhan yang cho ga'i phyag len dang / gzhung gi go don rnams la gzigs rtog rgya cher bskyangs pa dang / ji ltar thos pa'i chos rnams kyang bsam byung gi
rig pas yang dang yang du dpyad cing gtan la phab pas ma rtogs pa dang / log par rtog pa'i the tshom gyi dri ma mtha' dag rgyang ring du bsal ba dang / bsam pas sgro 'dogs
chod pa rnams kyang snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa khyad par can dang sbyar te sgom pas nyams su bzhes par mdzad do/ /dgung grangs nye bzhir son pa chu sprel lo'i hor zla
lnga pa'i nang mkhan chen rdo rje

'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin sa skyar khri mjal la phebs pa dang lhan cig bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por phebs/ dus gsum gyi rgyal ba rnams
kyi ye shes kyi sku 'chi med lha'i rigs su mngon par bzhengs pa'i gong ma sku ngo thams cad dang / srid pa'i 'jigs pa thams cad yongs su gzhil ba la rgyal byed kyi tshal
dang tshul mtshungs pa'i gtsug lag khang lta bas chog mi shes pa dang / de dag gi nang du bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i sku brnyan byin rlabs kyi
gzi 'od 'bar ba srid pa gsum na 'gran zla dang bral ba rnams legs par mjal zhing thugs smon rnam par dag pa'i rgyas 'debs pa dang / 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che ngag
dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po'i drung nas gu ru drag dmar nyang lugs kyi dbang chen zhig kyang gsan te hor zla drug pa'i nang e wa~M du phebs/
lo de'i mjug tu khro rgyal 'byung po 'dul byed kyi ljags bsnyen zla gcig lhag tsam dang / de'i bcu cha'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa mthar phyin par mdzad/ dgung grangs nyer
lnga pa dpal gdong gi lo'i hor zla gnyis pa'i dmar phyogs nas bzung ste zla ba bdun gyi bar du kye rdo rje gzhi'i bsnyen pa gdan thog gcig tu mthar phyin pa dang / de'i bcu
cha'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa mdzad cing / de rjes mkhan rin po che khri thog pa byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi drung nas/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa nas 'byung ba'i lo
gyon ma'i rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i grub chen birWa pa'i bzhed gzhung gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras tshogs bshad du grags pa'i lam gyi sngon 'gro snang ba gsum gyis
rgyud sbyangs te/ brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sgo nas sems bskyed pa dang / de rjes

dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i sgo nas kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur ba dang / lam gyi dngos gzhi rgyud gsum gyi khrid yongs su
rdzogs pa dang / de dag gi skabs su slob dpon gyi zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / gzhan yang e wa~M pa'i chos spyod dum bu gsum kha skong dang bcas pa
dang / rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i mngon rtogs/ lus dkyil/ dbang chu/ gtor chog /zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg gi sdom rnams dang
/ thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg gi lhan thabs/ dbang dang drag po'i sbyin sreg gi sdom dang lhan thabs rnams dang / padma badzra gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa
nyi shu pa dang / grags pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa daNDa ka /des mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi bkra shis dang / rgyud nas phyung ba'i mdzad bcu'i bkra shis rnams kyi lung / ba
ri lugs kyi sgrub thabs brgya rtsar grags pa'i rjes gnang don brgyad dang / mchims nam mkha' grags kyis bsgrigs pa'i mngon rtogs brgya rtsa las byung ba'i rjes gnang sum
cu so bzhi rnams legs par gsan par mdzad do/ /'ga' zhig thos dang bsam bor nas/ /rmongs sgom byis pa'i gom stabs kyis/ /kun mkhyen rgyal sar 'dzegs 'dod pa/ smig rgyu'i
chu la snyegs pa bzhin/ /la la mang du thos gyur kyang / /sgom pa'i bdud rtsi mi bsten pa/ /de kun rgya mtsho'i klong nyid du/ /skom pas gzir te 'chi dang mtshungs/ /mtha'
de gnyis ka bsal ba'i slad/ /zab yangs mkhyen brtse nus pa'i mtha'/ /mkha' dang yang dag mtshungs gyur pa'i/ /rnam par 'dren pa mang bsten zhing / /khyad par byams brtse'i
'jug pa yis/ /chos dbyings nam mkha'i thig le las/ /legs 'ongs

'chi med rdo rje'i sku/ /gtsug gi rgyan du gus bsten nas/ /zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsi'i zer/ /thugs kyi sa mos la 'phos pas/ /gzod nas rtogs pa'i shes rab kyi/ 'dab stong
slar yang bzhad par byas/ /de lta'i mang thos dga' tshal las/ /bsams byung rig pa'i bung ba yis/ /ma nor don gyi bcud myangs pas/ /shes rab lang tsho ci yang rgyas/ /rnam
rtog rdul gyis ma gos pa'i/ /rim gnyis sgom pa'i chu klung gis/ /spang bya'i dri ma kun bkrus pas/ /mya ngan 'das pa'i ri mo gsal// //gnyis pa mdo khams su byon nas bstan
'gro'i don dang thos bsam ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ de'ang kye rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen bzhugs pa'i skabs sogs mnal lam phal cher zhig tu/ spang gshong shin tu rgya che
ba skabs skabs su 'brog pa'i sbra yang yod pa zhig nas zhal shar du gzigs te phebs pa'i snang ba kho na byung ba dang / yang skabs 'gar rje rang gis dbu zhwa sa zhu zhig
mnabs te phebs pa'i mnal lam byung ba dang / yang skabs 'gar sde dge'i mgon khang shar du bzhugs pa'i chos skyong gi zhal 'bags rnams mnal lam du byung zhing / gnas tshul
de bzhin phyis su khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen por snyan sbron phul ba na/ nged kyang thog mar mdo khams su 'ong khar chos skyong gi zhal 'bags lta bu'i snang
ba yang yang 'char ba zhig yod ces gsungs shing / de ni chos srung rnams kyis bstan 'gro'i don la 'byon par bskul ba dang / phebs bsu'i rnam pa lta bu yin par sems la/ gang
ltar yang kye rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen grol mtshams su sde dge'i gnyer chen kun dga' dbang rgyal dpon mkhor rnams e wa~M du 'byor/ de gdong du khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje
'chang chen po dang / sde dge chos rgyal

mchog nas phyag bris re stsal 'dug par/ khu bo mkhan chen sku na mtho bar brten dbang lung gi 'phro rnams gsan pa'i phyir mdo khams su phebs rgyu mdzad tshe/ shing khyi lor
byon na mar lam gyi zhabs 'bring sogs ci dgos kun dga' dbang rgyal nas zhus chog tshul phebs rung / 'phral du phebs chas sogs gang ci nas 'grig dka' bar brten lo phyi ma
shing phag lor phebs rgyu mdzad/ de lo don gnyer rnams kyi ngor chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang ci rigs pa stsal/ khyad par hor zla bcu gcig pa'i mjug tu yon tan rin po che du ma'i
'byung gnas dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por phebs/ der bzhugs pa'i bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku ngo khag rnams su skyabs 'jug zhu mtshon gyi 'bul ba dang / lha
khang khag rnams su mchod 'bul dang thugs smon sogs zhib par mdzad/ khri chen grub pa'i dbang phyug ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po'i drung
nas gu ru drag dmar nyang lugs kyi dbang dang / sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi drung nas rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi rjes su gnang
ba dang / rje btsun ma 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma'i drung nas thang stong pa nas brgyud pa'i tshe rta zung 'brel gyi dbang bcas gsan nas e wa~M du phebs/ mdo khams su
phebs rgyu'i nyer bsdogs rnams kyang ji ltar 'os pa brtsams te/ dgung grangs nyer bdun pa shing phag lor e wa~M nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur nye ba na khu bo mkhan chen rdo
rje 'chang chen po'i phyag bris zhig 'byor te/ de snga e wa~M nas thon tshar med tshe/ 'di lo grwa pa gnyis 'bul skyel du gtong rgyu yin pas de dang lhan cig gis lo phyi
ma me byi lor 'byon rgyu byas na legs tshul phebs par brten de lo e wa~M rang du bzhugs/ lo de'i

mjug tu mdo khams nas khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i grwa tshang gras kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa dang / kun dga' ye shes 'khor bcas kyang e wa~M du 'byor/ bla ma
so sor 'bul ba dang dgon par mang 'gyed sogs gtos che bar bsgrubs/ rje 'dis kyang lha khang khag rnams su mchod 'bul dang / chos srung la skong phrin dang / yul lhar bsang
mchod la sogs pa skabs su bab pa'i rim gro'i rigs rnams kyang bsgrubs te/ dgung grangs nyer brgyad du son pa 'dzin byed kyi lo'i sa ga zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi rgyal ba
dang po'i nyin rje btsun dam pa sku 'khor chibs skyel gyi tshogs dang bcas te e wa~M nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ rim bzhin byang brgyud de shin tu mtho zhing brjid pa'i
snyems pas 'chi ba med pa'i grong khyer du snyoms pa lta bu'i la lung du ma dang / nyi 'od kyis bzhus pa'i gnam sngon gyi zhun ma sa la 'khyil pa la/ rgyu skar gyi phreng
ba 'thor ba dang 'dra ba'i chu bo dang chu phran du ma dang / kun gsal bu mo'i bzhin ras kyi mtha'ang mtshon par nus pa'i mi zad pa'i thang chen po rnams rim gyis brgal
te/ gro zhun zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes bzhi'i nyin phebs bsu ring thung gi tshogs sa chen po'i rdul la 'gran pa dang bcas te dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi rgyal
khab chen por nye zho'i dri mas ma gos par bde bar phebs/ zla ba de'i tshes bcu gsum nyin khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po yang bkra shis chos rdzong nas lhun grub
steng gi rgyal khab tu phebs te khu dbon gser zhal lhan rgyas par zhag bdun tsam bzhugs/ de'i bar la gtang rag gi skong gso la sogs pa mdzad/ slar khu bo mkhan chen mchog
bkra shis chos rdzong du lha sras rin po che rnams kyi sku'i rkyen sel sgrub par phebs/ rje 'dis stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba

sde dge chos rgyal chen po 'khor dang bcas par la rong 'bul ba sogs zab par 'bul bar mdzad pa dang / tshur yang de dag so so nas dbu thon legs 'bul gyi rigs shin tu rgya che
bar phul/ de lo lhun grub steng rang du bzhugs shing chos rgyal chen pos ji ltar bzhed pa'i rkyen sel rnams bsgrub pa dang / khyad par rgyu skar rgyal gyis nya ba'i dmar
phyogs kyi rdzogs pa gnyis pa nas bzung ste/ cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes bcu drug gi bar du 'du ba chen mo zhes pa chos grwa chen po de nyid na gnyug mar gnas pa'i dge slong
gi dge 'dun ji snyed bzhugs pa rnams dang / gzhan yang lcags ra/ sga len steng / 'khor lo mdo/ rdzong chen mgo /ye na/ rab brtan bcas kyi dgon pa so so'i dge 'dun thams
cad stabs gcig tu tshogs te 'jigs byed drug cu dang / ngor lugs dkyil 'khor bdun gyi sgrub mchod rnams gsungs pa'i tshogs dbur phebs pa dang / de rjes hor zla gsum pa'i
nang chu nag mar char 'bebs su phebs te cho ga gsungs ma thag pa nas char chen po babs/ thams cad kyis phyis su chu nag mar bla ma su phebs kyang char che rigs mi 'babs
pa la da lan babs pa ngo mtshar che zer ba byung / gang ltar yang / de phyin chad lo re bzhin char 'bebs su rtag par phebs shing char mi 'babs pa mi srid/ khyad par de sngon
bkra shis chos rdzong du lha sras rin po che rnams kyi sku'i rkyen sel sgrub par dbyar gyi ring khu bo mkhan chen dang / dgun gyi ring rong pa chos rje bzhugs pa yin
kyang / 'di lo chos rgyal mchog nas rje 'di phebs dgos tshul gyi bka' nan stsal pa ltar/ me glang sa ga zla ba'i nang bkra shis chos rdzong du phebs/ lha sras rin po che
sku mched rnams su nyin re bzhin tshe dpag med lha dgu'i

dbang dang / rta mgrin dang / phyag rdor dang / so 'brang bcas kyi rjes gnang dang / rnam dme gang rung gi khrus re bcas chag med du 'bul dgos pa dang / de'i steng du'ang sku
rim gsar 'phar gyi dbang rjes gnang khrus la sogs pa dang / chos srung rnams la skong ba phrin bcol la sogs pa ji dgos bsgrub par mdzad/ 'di lo chos rgyal chen po tshe
dbang rdo rje rig 'dzin pa'ang dbus gtsang ljongs kyi rten gsum rnams mjal ba dang / mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur stob pa'i phyir du chibs bteg /khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang
chen po'ang sga stod phyogs su chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur/ rje 'di hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nang bkra shis chos rdzong nas lhun grub steng du phebs/ hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i
tshes nyer lnga nas bzung drug 'du'i dbu bzhugs sogs mdzad pas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dbu bzhugs mdzad dus dang khyad med pa'i dge mtshan che bar kun gyis gleng / slar
yang dgung grangs sum cu pa sa pho stag gi lo'i hor zla gsum pa'i mjug tu bkra shis chos rdzong du phebs/ lha sras rin po che sku mched rnams su chag med kyi dbang rjes
gnang khrus rnams 'bul ba dang / gsar 'phar gyi sku rim rnams kyang bsgrub par mdzad/ de lo sde dge chos rgyal chen po dpon 'khor rnams kyang dbu thon gang legs kyis bod
nas mar phebs/ de dag la'ang dbu thon legs 'bul sogs skabs su bab pa rnams zab par mdzad/ de lo hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nang rje 'di'i mnal lam du sde dge chos rgyal nyid
yin snyam pa'i byis pa zhig chu nang du mchongs pa sogs mi dge ba'i ltas 'ga' zhig byung ba ltar/ rje 'di bkra shis chos rdzong nas lhun grub steng du phebs khar sras sku
mched kyi zhabs 'bring ba sku tshab tshe ring phun tshogs par/ deng skabs sras mo chung ba tshe dbang dpal

mo 'di sku khams dwangs min yod par ma zad/ rmi ltas kyang 'khrugs pa zhig 'dug pas/ bla ma rnams su thugs brtag dang mo rtsis zhib par byas te rim gro gang zab bsgrubs na
legs tshul gsungs pa bzhin sku tshab pas de bzhin bgyis kyang / sems can rang rang gi las kyi bsgo skal chu bo'i rgyun dang 'dra ba bzlog tu med pas thams cad kyis sku gegs
ci yang med tshul bshad rung / zla ba de'i nang du sras mo tshe dbang dpal mo dus kyi chos nyid du gyur/ rje 'dis lhun grub steng du phebs nas drug 'du'i dbu bzhugs rnams
mdzad/ de rjes lha sras rin po che rnams kyi sku'i rkyen sel sgrub par phur pa bla ma chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa bsko bzhag stsal/ rje 'di dgung grangs so gcig pa sa yos
hor zla gnyis pa'i yar tshes nas brtsams te/ stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba sde dge chos rgyal chen pos gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos
gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras slob bshad kyi chos 'khor bskor ba rnams rje 'dis kyang gsan par mdzad de/ de'ang lam gyi sngon 'gro snang ba gsum gyi khrid sngon du 'gro
ba'i brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi cho ga'i sgo nas byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa dang / de nas slob ma rjes su 'dzin pa sogs dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad
dang ldan pa'i sgo nas dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba aShta'i bzlas lung dang bcas pa dang / lam gyi dngos gzhi rgyud gsum yongs su rdzogs
pa'i nyams khrid shin tu zhib pa/ de dag gi nang gses phyi bskyed rim gyi mgor bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dbang dang / nang bskyed rim gyi mgor slob dpon gyi zab mo
lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba yig brgya'i bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ rdzogs rim gyi mgor

bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i byin gyis brlabs pa dang / gzhan yang de dag gi bar skabs rnams su sbyor ba don yod pa bzhis bla ma mnyes par byed pa'i khrid sngon du 'gro ba'i
lam zab phyi ma'i byin rlabs dang / de las 'phros pa bla ma rin 'byung gi byin rlabs/ lam zab nang ma'i byin gyis brlabs pa dang / bir srung phyi ma'i byin rlabs sgom lung
dang bcas pa/ bir srung nang ma'i byin rlabs sgom lung dang bcas pa/ lam sbas bshad kyi byin rlabs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs/ tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/
rten 'brel snying pos bsrung ba'i byin rlabs/ brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs/ a mes zhabs kyi yig steng nas brda chig brgyud thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs dang / sgrub
pa lung sbyin pa dang / gsang ba bcu'i rgyas gdab pa'i byin rlabs/ mthar mgon rkyang gi rjes su gnang ba rnams dang / lung gi skor la/ rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i sdom
pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa dang / ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i bir srung phyi nang gi byin rlabs dang / tshogs 'khor gsang ba kun rgyan/ bdag chen rdo rje
'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med dang / brda' don gsal ba'i khrid yig /lus dkyil dbang chog /lam zab phyi ma'i nyams len/ lam sbas bshad kyi zin
bris/ bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub thabs rnams dang / rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi mngon rtogs dang byin rlabs bya tshul nub pa rig 'dzin grags dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges
mdzad pa/ dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i mngon rtogs/ lus dkyil/ dbang chu/ gtor chog /rdul mtshon chu bor spyan drang tshul/ zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /rgyas
pa'i sbyin sreg gi sdom rnams

dang / thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg gi lhan thabs dang / drag po'i sbyin sreg dang dbang gi sbyin sreg gi sdom dang lhan thabs/ dus tha ma'i cho ga /'thor
nas bsgrub tshul rnams dang / dkon mchog dpal ldan gyis mdzad pa'i rab gnas dpal 'byor rgya mtsho/ tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i phyi nang gi bskyed rim rnam bshad nyi ma'i
'od zer dang / bla ma rin 'byung gi nyams len/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i kye rdor bsnyen thabs/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad
pa'i sems bskyed cho ga /slob ma rjes 'dzin/ bdag med ma/ lam zab phyi nang / bla ma rin 'byung rnams kyi byin rlabs/ bir srung phyi ma'i byin rlabs ngor chen gyis mdzad
pa'i zur 'debs dang / bir srung nang ma'i byin rlabs/ brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs gnyis las gsum byung gi go don dang bcas pa/ lam sbas bshad dang / brda chig brgyud kyi
byin rlabs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi zur 'debs/ sgrub pa lung sbyin dang gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab kyi phyag len/ slob bshad gnad kyi gsal byed rnams dang / 'jam mgon a mes
zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i lam zab nang ma'i nyams len dang / brda chig brgyud kyi byin rlabs/ rdor dril dgang gzar bum pa rnams kyi rnam bshad bcas dang / sangs phun gyis mdzad
pa'i kye rdo rje'i dus tha ma'i cho ga /slob dpon padma badzra gyis mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i bstod pa nyi shu pa/ grags pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa daNDa ka dang / dkyil
'khor gyi bkra shis/ rgyud nas phyung ba'i mdzad bcu'i bkra shis rnams kyi lung bcas legs par gsan pa yin no/ /mdor na bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'di dang / khu
bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po gnyis ni/ sngon

gyi dus su jo bo rje dang / 'brom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyi rnam thar dang tshul mtshungs par yang srid snga ma rnams su'ang bla slob kyi 'brel ba zam ma chad pa zhig
yin par gor ma chag ste/ de'ang sku tshe 'dir thog mar zhal mjal ba tsam gyis bcos ma ma yin pa'i mos gus chen po 'khrungs shing / nges par rdo rje 'chang dngos yin pa la
the tshom cung zad kyang mi mnga'/ dus rtag tu thugs mnyes pa kho na las mi mnyes pa skad cig kyang mi mdzad/ khyad par mdo khams su dmigs bsal dbang lung gsan pa dang
/ sku yon gzigs par phebs pa yin rung / chos rgyal mchog gis lha sras rin po che rnams kyi sku'i rkyen sel sgrub par phebs dgos tshul bka' stsal ba sogs kyis bshad ma thag
pa'i gsung ngag slob bshad tsam las/ bka' chos gsan pa dang sku yon gzigs long ma byung rung / bla ma'i byin rlabs thugs rgyud la zhugs pa lta bus khams su phebs ma thag
pa nas mnal lam du'ang / me tog mang po thag sgra dang bcas te shar ba'i snang ba byung zhing / gnas tshul de bzhin khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen por snyan sgron
phul ba na shes rab rgyas pa'i ltas yin nam gsungs shing / don la'ang snga na med pa'i thugs rab kyi klong chen po rdol ba dang / khu bo mkhan chen mchog gis kyang / khyed
de snga bod du chos skad chags pa ci'ang byung mi 'dug pas da lan 'dir slebs pa legs gsungs shing thugs dgyes tshor mdzad pa dang / nged chung ngu'i dus ji ltar byed
pa bzhin/ khyed kyis kyang de ltar byed 'dug gsungs shing sku'i mdzad spyod mthun pa dang / sku shin tu btsun pa sogs kyis thugs kyi sras dam par gyur cing shin tu thugs
rtsis su mdzad pa yin no/ /hor zla bzhi pa'i nang khu dbon gnyis char gyis kye rdo rje'i sgrub mchod zhag bdun tsam gsungs shing / de

rjes hor zla drug pa'i nang rma rong chu tshan du khu dbon gnyis ka phebs te zhag bdun tsam bzhugs pa dang / de nas khu bo mkhan chen sde dge dbyar gzigs su phebs pa'i sku'i
rkyen sel sgrub par phebs shing / rje 'di la khyod kyis sgra rig pa 'di rab mthar phyin pa zhig dang / de ltar ma byung na'ang bag chags zhig nges par zhog cig ces bka'
stsal ba ltar lhun grub steng du phebs te/ lnga rig smra ba zhu slob kun dga' don grub pa'i drung nas gzhon nu kArti kas dbang phyug go cha la stsal ba'i sgra'i bstan bcos
ka lA pa dang / de'i 'grel pa sa bzang paNDi ta blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa dang / mtshams sbyor dang ming le'i lag len zhe drung padma rnam dag gis mdzad pa sogs
kyi steng nas mtshams sbyor lnga dang / ming le drug dang / kun bshad brgyad dang / kr-ita rkang drug ste le'u nyer lnga'i ri mo yongs su rdzogs pa bslab sbyangs mthar
phyin par mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang mkhas pa'i dbang po de nyid kyi drung nas rje btsun sa skya pa dang dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa rnams las brgyud pa gtso bor
gyur pa'i zab chos 'ga' zhig phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa man ngag be bum mam gser pod du grags pa'i lung gsan pa'i skor la/ thog mar bya rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi
gtso bo klu dbang rgyal po'i sgrub thabs klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa lo chen rin bzang gi 'gyur/ de'i sgrub thabs bcom ldan ral gris mdzad pa/ bstod pa rong ston gyis mdzad
pa/ rjes gnang gi tho yig mdzad byang mi gsal ba rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'irigs kyi bdag po ma ti'i lugs kyi 'jam dpal dkar po dpa' bo gcig grub kyi skor la sgrub
thabs paNDi ta ma ti'am gsang mtshan sgeg pa'i rdo rjer grags pas

mdzad pa khro lo'i 'gyur/ des mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal gyi bstod pa/ rjes gnang gi phyag len khro los mdzad pa/ 'jam dkar gyi lo rgyus dang / rtsa ba'i sgrub thabs las kha tshar
bzhi dang bcas pa rnams rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus kyis mdzad pa bcas dang / dam pa rgya gar nas brgyud pa'i 'jam dpal smra ba'i seng ge'i skor la sgrub thabs dam
pa sangs rgyas kyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal gyi sgrub pa'i rim pa tshig lhug pa/ bstod pa mdzad byang med pa/ shes rab 'phel ba'i dmigs pa 'jam dpal dmar po'i
gsung gi rdzogs rim/ 'jam dpal gyi zhal blta ba'i thabs/ shes rab 'phel ba dang dbang du bya ba'i thabs/ mu drA dbang du bya ba mdzes ma rgyan 'khor/ gzhan gyi ngag rku ba/
pha rol gyi shes rab 'phrog pa/ mngon shes sgrub pa/ rkang mgyogs sgrub pa/ mig rno ba sman rnams kyi thun tshad/ ral gri'i rgyu dang ril bu'i dbyibs dang kha dog gza'
skar dang bcas pa bstan pa/ ril bu'i gdan gyi 'khor lo'i rnam gzhag /rjes gnang gi cho ga /sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang gi maNDal gyi rnam gzhag /sgrub pa'i tshad dang blang
dor bstan pa/ sAtstsha dkar nag gi las sbyor/ dbang sdud 'khor lo 'bri tshul gyi gsal byed mdzad byang med pa rnams dang / gshegs rigs kyi khro bo mi g.yo ba dkar po'i
skor rmor chen gyis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa la/ mi g.yo ba dkar po'i sgrub thabs dA na shI las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa/ mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa'i mi g.yo ba dkar
po shes rab blo 'phel gyi sgrub thabs bcud kyi snying po/ mi g.yo ba dkar po'i zhal gdams gsum gyi snyan brgyud yi ger bkod pa/ lta ba bka' rtags kyi phyag rgya'i nyams
len gyi gnad dang bcas

pa/ mi g.yo ba dkar po'i bstod pa rnams yon tan khris mdzad pa bcas dang / padma'i rigs kyi yum du gtogs pa sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i skor 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug gis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs par mdzad pa la/ sgrol dkar sgrub thabs slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa ba ri'i 'gyur/ sgrol dkar gyi bum chog gtor
ma srung 'khor rnams kyi yi ge /bris pa'i srung 'khor gyi yi ge /bar chad zhi bar byed pa'i yi ge /sgrol ma'i byad 'grol gyi yi ge slob dpon padma nag pos mdzad pa ba
ri'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i sprul pa ce spyang sngon mo'i lam srung / de'i gsal byed/ dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrol dkar bum chog rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ sgrol dkar
gyi mngon rtogs dang / de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ sgrol dkar bla brgyud kyi lo rgyus mdzad byang med pa/ sgrol dkar gyi rjes
gnang dang / de'i zab khrid kyi dmigs rim dang / sbyin sreg gi cho ga rnams 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ sgrol dkar sgrub thabs nyung ngu dbang
rab pas mdzad pa bcas dang / padma'i rigs kyi khro bo rta mgrin zla rgyal lugs sam lcags ral can du grags pa'i skor la/ rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ thun mong gi las tshogs
nad pa gso ba/ steng gdon gzir ba/ nad gdon srung ba/ ser ba srung ba/ phyir zlog dang bcas byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ rjes gnang gi cho ga mdzad byang
med pa rnams dang / rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nya dme brtsegs dud ka sa lugs su grags pa'i skor la/ sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa sa paNDi tas mdzad pa la/ nang gses
kyi las tshogs smyo 'bogs 'dul ba/

ser ba zlog pa/ rims nad gso ba/ phyugs god srung ba/ mi lo nad can gso ba/ ra lug la spyang ki srung ba/ nad pa'i sngas srung / zhing gi 'bu srung ba/ sris rme ba'i thabs/
'gong po sreg pa dang bcas pa rnams dang / jo lugs dme brtsegs ljang nag gi las tshogs skor la/ nad pa grib kyis phog pa srung ba/ lam gyi grib srung ba/ smyon pa 'dul ba/
ser ba srung ba/ rims nad gso ba/ phyugs god srung ba/ mi lo nad can gso ba/ ra lugs la spyang ki srung ba/ 'bras phol lhog pa gso ba/ nad pa'i sngas srung / zhing la
'bu srin srung ba/ bang mdzod du 'gong po zhugs pa srung ba/ nor phyugs la 'gong po rjes su 'brang ba sreg pa/ dme grib srung ba'i thabs lo rgyus dang bcas pa rnams dang
/ bya rgyud nor can gyi rigs jo bo lugs kyi dzaM dkar 'brug zhon lha lnga'i skor la/ dzaM dkar lha lnga'i sgrub thabs jo bos mdzad pa la nang gses su phyi chu sbyin la brten
nas sgrub pa/ nang gtor ma la brten nas sgrub pa/ gsang ba gwa'u la brten nas sgrub pa rnams dang / thugs rje chen po'i spyan chab las sprul pa'i dzambha las jo bo la
gdams pa gnang ba'i lo rgyus/ rjes gnang gi tho yig a ti sha'i man ngag las byung ba/ bstod pa jo bos mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa she'u lo tsA ba kun dga'
chos grags kyis mdzad pa rnams dang / sa skya'i gser chos ba ri lugs kyi seng gdong sngon mo'i skor la/ byad ma 'bum rdugs kyi 'khor lor grags pa'i man ngag la nang gses

zhing gi 'bu srung ba/ g.yag nad gcod pa/ sad srung

ba/ ser srung / thog srung / lug nad srung ba/ tse ge gcod pa/ lhog pa srung ba/ rims srung / 'brum srung / 'khrug gcod/ mtshon srung / gre 'gag srung ba/ 'go yor srung ba/
gza' nad srung ba/ jag chings te las tshogs nyer lnga rnams dang / mkha' 'gro stong gi srog snying nang nas phyir zlog pa'i thabs/ seng gdong ma'i man ngag yi ge bcu bzhi'i
las tshogs/ tshigs bcad ma phyir zlog lugs gcig /tshar chen dang mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rnams dang / gser chos 'jam dpal nag po'i skor la/ 'jam dpal nag

yi ger yar klung pas zhu dag byas pa/ tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs kyi ngag 'don dang / rmor chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs nyung ngu bcas dang / gser chos rdo

ba/ srung skud gdags pa/ sman la brten nas mdze gso ba'i ril bu sogs rgyas par bstan pa/ rje btsun rin po che grags pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ bzlas lung ster ba'i man ngag

bya mdos/ ngan song sgo 'gegs bya ba khyi dug bcos pa'i man ngag rnams gzungs pas mdzad pa/ gdon rnam 'grol bya ba gza' bcos pa'i man ngag bzang po'i mtshan can gyis mdzad
pa/ dkar phra men brtag pa'i zhal shes/ gza' bcos pa'i lag len shog dril khyung rgya ma/ khyung gi las mtha' gshed skor zab mo bcas gzungs pas mdzad pa/ klu dang gza' rigs

skya pa rnams shin tu thugs gtsigs che ba'i nor gyi lha mo dbyu gu mched gsum gyi skor la/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis gnod sbyin mo kun 'khyil gyi rtog pa nas phyung ba'i sgrub

de'i snying po sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ ba ri ba bod du byon khar rdo rje gdan pas skyel thung mdzad nas gnang ba'i thugs dam mkha' 'gro ma'i dngos grub lag bcang / dbyu gu

li ya'i sgrub

pa bya tshul bklags chog ma 'jam mgon kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa/ rmor chen gyis mdzad pa'i mkha' spyod ma'i zhing bkod dang mthun pa'i bstod pa dang / mchod phreng rgyas

zhun rnams kyi lung dang / rje btsun sa skya pa rnams la chos srung gi gdams pa rgya mtsho tsam bzhugs pa'i nang nas mchog tu gyur pa rdo rjai nag po chen po'i skor gyi
rtsa ba'i yi ge rnams bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i glegs bam me 'bar mar grags pa dang / de'i yan lag gi yi ge rnams tshar chen chos kyi

yig sna rnams tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i snyan brgyud glegs bam/ rmor chen gyis bsgrigs pa'i snyan brgyud dang rjes su 'brel ba'i yang skong
glegs bam rnams dang / zhing skyong stobs 'phrog dbang po gdong bzhi pa'i chos skor rnams rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i zhal pod nor bu'i
do shal dang / de'i snying thig ha la nag po'i dpe bum bcas dang / zhal bzhi pa'i bka' sdod gnod sbyin bektse'i chos skor phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i dpe bum rnams kyi
lung bcas legs par gsan cing khong du chud par mdzad do/ /yang mkhas btsun bzang po'i gter gyur gdong dgon bla ma bstan 'dzin phun tshogs kyi drung nas ngor chen bstan pa'i

rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgrigs pa'i lam 'bras glegs bam pod ser mar grags pa dang / ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos bsgrigs pa'i gsung ngag glegs bam pod dmar
du grags pa rnams kyi lung bcas legs par gsan cing tshig don rnams kyang bsams byung gi shes rab zab mos mngon sum du mdzad pa yin no/ /gzhan yang de skabs kyi lo snga

pa rnams kyi rgyud smin cing grol bar mdzad de/ mdor na bshad sgrub kyis bsdus pa'i bstan pa rin po che nyi 'od kyis phyes pa'i padmo bzhin du rgyas par mdzad pa yin no/
/gang du son pa tsam gyis kyang / /srid pa'i 'jigs pa zil gnon pa'i/ /dpal ldan sa skya zhes grags pa/ /dad pa'i spyan gyis legs par mjal/ /de na brtan pa'i 'khor lo nyid/
