te/ /rdo rje'i sngags kyi cho ga yis/ /mngon 'dod re ba'i shing rta bkang / /las kyi 'byung 'gyur mkhyen pa ni/ /tshems dkar 'od kyis 'grems pa bzhin/ /'gro ba'i blo mun
kun bsal bas/ /mkhas dang rmongs pa'i khyad par bye/ /zab gsang sngags kyi smin grol dang / /tha snyad sgra yi bstan bcos sogs/ /rnam dpyod blo yi bang mdzod du/ /bcug pas
shes rab nor gyis phyug /mos pa'i rdzing bu dang 'tshams par/ /chos kyi zla snang 'bum spros pas/ /'khor ba'i rab rib kun bsal te/ /rnam grol ku mud rgyas par mdzad// //gsum
pa mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i slad du dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du bsnyen bkur rgya cher bstabs pa dang nyan bshad sgom gsum
ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni 'di ltar rjes su thos te/ rje 'di dgung grangs so gcig pa sa yos hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nang khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid
dbon po stod du bad kan skya rbab kyis bsnyun tshul bzhes shing / slar hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i nang cung zad sku khams dwangs tshul bstan nas lhun grub steng du phebs/ sku
rim sman dpyad sogs la thugs 'dun mi mdzad par 'dug na'ang rje 'dis gong du khu bo mkhan chen de nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar gyi zhabs brtan gyi rigs shin tu rgya
che bar bsgrubs/ gzhan yang de skabs su rje 'dis drug 'du'i dbu bzhugs rnams kyang mdzad/ slar yang rim gyis sku khams je nyog tu song zhing yun ring mi bzhugs par zhal
gyis bzhes par brten/ rje 'di'i

thugs la'ang da ni 'jig rten na smra ba'i nyi ma nub par 'gyur ro snyam pa'i thugs 'gyod shin tu che bar gyur na'ang khu bo mkhan chen de nyid kyi zhal snga nas/ yang dag par
rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan na/ gzhan la mi rtag par byung ba lta ci smos zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i bka' stsal phebs pa dang /
bla ma'i byin rlabs kyis thugs kyi mya ngan kyang rim gyis bsal bar gyur la/ de skabs kun tu nyin mtshan bar ma chad par bla ma'i zhabs tog 'ba' zhig mdzad pas/ sdig pa dag
pa'i rtags nam mkha' la 'phur ba la sogs pa'i rmi ltas kyang mang du byung gsungs / de nas rje 'di dgung grangs so gnyis su phebs pa lcags 'brug hor zla dang po'i tshes
bcu dgu'i nyin/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dam pa tog dkar po dga' ldan gyi yul nas dzambu'i gling du 'pho bar brtsams pa na/ rang gi cod pan rje btsun
ma pham pa'i dbur bcings te theg pa chen po'i chos kyi rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol ba dang / 'jam mgon sa paNDi ta chen po zhi bar gshegs pa'i tshe'ang / chos kyi dung
dang lhung bzed la sogs pa 'phags pa rin po che la stsal te da ni khyod kyis bstan pa'i bya ba dang / sems can dpag tu med pa'i don bya ba'i dus la bab pas sngon gyi dam
bcas pa dran par gyis shig /ces bka' stsal te chos kyi rgyal srid chen por mnga' gsol ba sogs dang tshul mtshungs par/ khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyi sku
srung rwa lo'i mgul phur du grags pa dang / rten sgam dang / phyag phreng dang / dam tshig gi rdor dril rnams rje 'di la stsal te/ 'di nged kyi dam tshig rdor dril yin
kyang / da khyed rang gi 'bral spangs dam tshig rdor dril gyis/ spyir khyed rang spun rnams kyi tshe la thar rtse yang dar zhing rgyas par 'byung / sgos khyed rang 'di

nas yar byon nas lo shas zhig nas ngor gyi mkhan po byed dgos par 'dug /de nas kyang khams phyogs 'dir da dung lan cig 'byon dgos par 'dug /de thams cad la bar chad med cing
bstan 'gror phan thogs par 'ong gsungs pa dang / rje 'dis bdag la spangs rtogs kyi yon tan ci'ang med bzhin du mkhan po byas pas ga la 'ong zhes gsol ba na/ khyed rang
kun spyod thams cad da lta'i 'di bzhin du gyis dang / mkhan po mi yong ba ci'ang med/ da lta'i ngor pa'i zhabs drung thams cad kyi nang nas khyed rang drag shos su 'dug gsungs
pa dang / nged kyi yi dam gyi lha bcu gnyis po de rab gser zangs las grub pa/ 'bring sman 'dam las grub pa/ tha ma bris sku re nges par bzhengs dgos/ gzhan nga la 'dra
sku dang gdung rten bzhengs mi dgos/ nga yi rus pa rnams sa gtsang sa zhig tu bskyal bas chog gsungs pa sogs zhal ta mthil phyin par gnang / de'i phyi nyin yang lhag
tu sku khams ngan du song ba ma mchis mod/ gdul bya rtag 'dzin can rnams chos la bskul ba'i phyir du de nub zla ba dang po 'char ba dang mnyam du gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos
kyi dbyings su bsdus par gyur to/ /de nas zhag brgyad bar thugs dam la bzhugs shing / zla ba de'i tshes nyer brgyad kyi nub mo rje 'di'i mnal lam du/ khu bo mkhan chen rdo
rje 'chang chen po de nyid byon nas da nged thugs dam las grol ba yin no gsungs par brten/ de'i phyi nyin sku gdung rin po cher cho ga rnam par dag pa'i sgo nas bsgrubs
pa'i bum chus sku khrus yang yang gsol zhing / dri bzang po dang / sman sna tshogs kyi lde gus byugs pa dang / ras ser pos legs par dkris shing dbu rgyan dang / lha rdzas
kyi na bzas mdzes par bklubs te/ gdung sgrom gyi khri'i steng du mchod pa'i bye brag dpag tu

med pa dang bcas bzhugs su gsol zhing / de nas mkhas dbang kun dga' don grub ba dang / gdong dgon bla ma bstan 'dzin phun tshogs pa la sogs pa'i dge slong bcu phrag gcig gis
dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub cing mchod pa dang / yang dge slong nyi shu tsam gyis bcom ldan 'das kun rig rnam par snang mdzad kyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs
te sgrub cing mchod pa sogs mdzad pa dang / khyad par hor zla gnyis pa'i yar ngo'i tshes drug gi nyin klu ldings zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan
gyi gtsos pa'i dge slong bcu phrag gcig gis dpal kye rdo rje la brten pa'i dus tha ma'i cho ga'i sgo nas zhugs phul ba dang / grub mchog ngag dbang rin chen gyi gtsos
pa'i dge 'dun mang rab cig gis kun rig la brten pa'i sbyin sreg gi mchod pa phul bar mdzad cing / de nas kyang yun ring po'i bar du dge slong bcu phrag gcig gis dpal kye
rdo rje'i sgrub mchod dang / dge slong nyi shu skor gyis kun rig gi sgrub mchod zhag zhe dgu'i bar ma chag pa dang / bdun re re'i steng du'ang lhun grub steng gi shar nub
kyi bla ma gnyis dang / zhu dag sprul sku dang / rong po bla ma dang / rdo rje 'dzin pa ngag dbang chos 'byor dang / gling mgo zi dgon du bzhugs pa'i khang sar zhabs drung
rin po che ngag dbang blo gros rgyal mtshan pa rnams spyan drangs te dge slong sum cu skor gyis kun rig gi sgrub mchod rgyas par mdzad pa dang / lhun grub steng du bzhugs
pa'i bla ma yod rigs thams cad la'ang bsngo smon gyi rten shin tu zab pa dang / dgon par kun rig gi cho ga nyin grangs kha shas dang / gzhan yang sde dge'i mnga' zhabs
kyi sa dgon yod do cog la bsnyen bkur dang / gral 'gyed la sogs pa shin tu gya nom pa dang / dpal spungs/ rdzogs chen/ bye chen/ kaHthog /dpal yul la sogs pa'i ris su med
pa'i bla ma che gras rnams su rgya dngul srang lnga bcu re'i mgo

byas pa'i 'bul ba dang / bla ma chung ba rnams su rgya dngul srang nyer lnga re'i gtso byas pa'i 'bul ba dang / dgon khag rnams su bsnyen bkur gya nom par mdzad de/ 'di dag
zhib par gong du mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar ro/ /'dra sku dang gdung rten bzhengs mi dgos zhes gsungs na'ang / dad pa'i rten
du rin chen gnyis pa thur srang dgu bcu las grub pa'i mchod rten bkra shis sgo mang dang / gser zangs las grub pa'i 'dra sku khru gang lhag tsam dang / zhal chems su yod
pa'i yi dam gyi lha bcu gnyis kyi sku brnyan gser zangs las grub pa khru gang cung med tsam re bzhengs par mdzad do/ /de'i tshe slob ma'i tshogs thams cad kyang chos kyi
rje de zhi bar gshegs par gyur na'ang / de'i sku yi bkod pa gnyis pa lta bu'i bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'di bzhugs so snyam pas mya ngan dang yid mi bde ba ci'ang
med cing / zhabs 'bring pa rnams kyis kyang rje 'di'i sku'i mdzad tshul legs pa dang kun spyod btsun pa rnams mthong ba'i tshe mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de 'di
rang yin snyam pa kho na byung zhes gleng bar byed do/ /slar yang mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i phyir dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du
bsnyen bkur rgya cher bstab pa'i slad du 'byon par brtsams te/ de skor gyi nyer bsdogs rnams kyang ji ltar 'os pa bsgrigs pa'i tshe sde dge chos rgyal mchog gi gtsos mchog
dman rnams kyis mgrin gcig tu/ chos kyi rgyal po chen po mkhan chen smra ba'i nyi ma de nyid ni bdag cag rnams kyi bsod nams kyir bar ma tshud par nges par skal ba dman
pa'i nub ri'i phag tu gshegs par gyur na'ang / srid pa gsum gyi sdug bsngal gyi me chen rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i

mi zad pa'i bdud rtsi'i gter chen po khyod lta bu ni bdag sogs rnams kyi dbang po'i dngas ma dang / spyi bo'i gtsug rgyan du thob pa lags na mkhan chen mchog gi dgongs rdzogs
sgrub pa'i 'os su gyur pa gang rung zhig ched du mngags ste/ rje rang nyid khams phyogs 'dir yun ring du bzhugs par zhu ba'i gsol ba lan grangs mang du btab kyang / ji
skad du/ dam pa mang po khas 'che mi byed cing / gal te dka' ba'i gnas ni khas blangs na/ /rdo la ri mo bris pa ji bzhin du/ /shi yang gzhan du 'dor bar mi byed do/ /zhes
pa ltar/ dang po ji ltar dam bcas pa'i mtshams las nam yang mi 'da' ba dam pa rnams kyi chos nyid yin pa ltar zhal gyis ma bzhes par bod du 'byon par thag bcad/ slar yang
lhun grub steng gi gtsug lag khang du chos grwa der bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun gang yod kyis tshe chog dang / bla ma mchod pa nyin gsum mdzad pa'i nyin re bzhin bsnyen bkur
dang gral 'gyed shin tu zab pa'i steng / gtsug lag khang der bzang gos 'phan sogs sbyor 'jags stsal ba dang / lhun grub steng gi phan gling bla brang rang du'ang sa skyong
mchog gi dbu'i mchod gnas rim byon gyi nyer mkho'i thebs su/ khu bo mkhan chen de nyid kyi 'bral spangs sa chen kun blo'i snang brnyan sman 'dam las grub pa dang / gser
zangs las grub pa'i sku 'dra che chung thams cad bsdoms pas bzhi bcu zhe drug dang / 'khar rag sogs las grub pa'i sku 'dra che chung bsdoms pas sum cu so dgu dang / zhal
thang skor la/ lam 'bras bla ma brgyud pa'i gser thang gras 'grig spus legs drug /kye rdo rje gdan gsum tshang ba'i bris thang gcig bcas dang / mchod cha'i rigs la sil snyan
bzang 'bring gnyis/ rol mo bzang 'bring bzhi/ 'kha' rnga gcig /dung chen cha

gcig /zangs kyi ka To ra che chung lnga/ rkang gling ha mgo ma zangs rag gi shan ma cha gcig /mchod kong gras 'grig brgya/ spos rta gras 'grig brgya/ lhung bzed gcig /bzang
gos 'brug ris ma'i bla bre gcig /glang po che'i mche ba che chung gnyis la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang gdan/ lcog rtse/ thab cha'i skor sna tshogs pa dang bcas gsar sbyor
stsal ba dang / nye skor gyi dgon khag rnams su'ang bsnyen bkur zab par bstabs pa dang / don du gnyer ba so so'i mos pa dang bstun pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang c-i rigs par
stsal ba dang / sbyin bdag dad pa can 'ga' zhig gis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor rang rang gi khyim du byon te 'gal rkyen bsal zhing / 'phral yun gyi mthun rkyen mtha' dag lhun
gyis grub par mdzad pa dang / chos rgyal chen po 'khor dang bcas pa rnams nas kyang phebs brdzong dang 'bul ba sogs zab par phul ba dang / phar yang de dag la skabs su
bab pa'i chos dang zang zing gis tshim par mdzad de lcags 'brug snron gyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes lnga'i nyin phebs skyel gyi tshogs shin tu rgya che ba dang
bcas te dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi rgyal khab nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ sde dge chos rgyal mchog nas kyang / ye na bar gyi phebs skyel du gnyer kun dga' dbang rgyal
'khor dang bcas pa rnams dang / khyad par e wa~M rang du ma phebs bar gyi zhabs 'bring bar 'dun 'khor nis mda' bu kun dga' bstan 'dzin pas gtso byas pa'i sku tshab gsum 'khor
dang bcas pa gtong gnang mdzad pa bzhin/ de rnams dang bcas te rim gyis chibs bteg /lam bar du 'khod pa'i 'gro ba rnams la'ang chos kyi bdud rtsi ci rigs par stsol ba
dang / dgon khag rnams su'ang bsnyen bkur ji ltar rigs pa stob bzhin pa'i sgo nas hor zla brgyad

pa'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes bco lnga'i nyin bod gangs can gyi lte ba lugs gnyis kyi dpal 'byor zad mi shes pa 'byung ba'i gnas lha ldan du phebs/ de skabs rgyal dbang thams
cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims rgya mtsho li thang du sku 'khrungs zin na'ang / yar gdan 'dren zhu ma tshar bar brten/ rgyal ba'i bzhugs khri rin po che'i mdun du/ maNDal
sku gsung thugs rten/ bzang ja 'khor drug lnga bcu/ rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu/ bod dngul Tam srang lnga bcu/ rta drel drug /mdzo g.yag bcu/ gzhan yang dar/ ras/ ling
/ gos chen/ spu shun gyi rigs shin tu mang po dang / mchod cha dang thab cha'i skor sna tshogs pa dang bcas phul ba dang / stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba rgyal tshab chen
po tshe smon gling par yang maNDal sku gsung thugs rten dang gsol ja bzhes 'bras kyi dod dngul Tam srang brgyad dang / bzang ja 'khor drug nyer lnga/ bod dngul Tam srang
lnga bcu/ rta drel gsum/ mdzo g.yag lnga/ dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen/ spu shun la sogs pa'i tshan grangs mang po dang / mchod cha dang / thab cha'i rigs sna tshogs pa dang
bcas 'bul lam zhus par/ phyir slog tu na bza' sku chas kyi rigs dang / lam yig /dos rta/ rtsa shing sogs phon che ba dang / ja khral rtsa chag bcas bka' drin stsal ba
dang / bstan rgyas gling dang / kun bde gling / tshe chog gling / dga' ldan khri chen rin po che gsar rnying rnams su'ang so sor ljon 'dab 'khor drug lnga dang / rta re'i
gtsos pa'i tshan grangs gang mang dang / gzhan yang bka' shag dang / rtse shod kyi gsol gzim mgron gnyer la sogs par ja gsar skabs su gang bab re dang / khyad par lha dang
bcas pa'i 'jig rten kun gyi mchod sdong bla na med pa ston mchog nyi ma'i gnyen gyi sku brnyan rnam pa gnyis kyi gtso byas pa'i rten gsum yongs la gser gsol

dang / snyan dar dang / jo shAka rnam gnyis kyi mdun du stong mchod shin tu rgyas pa dang / lha khang gzhan rnams su'ang mchod 'bul rgyas bsdus ci rigs pa dang / rtse rnam
rgyal grwa tshang / gling khag gsum gyi grwa tshang / tshe chog gling / 'bras spungs 'dus spyi/ de'i nang tshan gling khang tshan/ se ra 'dus spyi/ de'i nang gses tre bo
khang tshan/ dga' ldan/ rgyud stod smad/ rme ru/ bzhi sde rnams su mang jas bsnyen bkur ba dang / smon lam chen mo'i skabs kyi 'dus tshogs rin po cher mang ja gnyis kyis
bsnyen bkur ba'i dod du bzang ja 'khor drug bdun cu skor lha sa bla brang gi phyag mdzod par 'bul lam zhus pa dang / gzhan yang rje 'dis jo khang la zhabs skor shin tu mang
po dang / lha ldan gyi phyi skor lnga bcu nga brgyad bcas mdzad nas/ hor zla dgu pa'i dmar phyogs kyi dga' ba gnyis pa'i nyin lha ldan nas chibs bteg ste/ yar lam ra bstod
dang / snye thang dang / lcags zam chu bo ri'i dgon pa dang / rong byams chen dang / rong ngur smrig bcas kyi rten gsum rnams mjal te/ mchod 'bul dang / so so'i bla
ma rnams su bsngo smon gyi rten dang / dgon khag so sor mang jas bsnyen bkur ba rnams mdzad de/ hor zla bcu pa'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes drug gi nyin gzhis ka rtser phebs/
der zhag gnyis bzhugs/ chos grwa chen po bkra shis lhun por phebs te paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa rje btsun blo bzang dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi ma'i mtshan dpe'i dkyil
'khor mjal ba dang chabs cig 'bul bar/ maNDal sku gsung thugs rten gsol ja bzhes 'bras kyi dod dngul Tam srang brgyad dang / bzang ja 'khor drug nyi shu/ bod dngul Tam
srang lnga bcu/ rta drel bzhi/ mdzo g.yag bdun/ dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen/ spu shun gyi rigs mang po dang / mchod cha dang / thab cha'i rigs

sna tshogs pa dang bcas phul ba dang / zhabs pad mdun du'ang ljon 'dab 'khor drug lnga dang / rta gcig bcas dang / gzhan yang rtse'i gsol gzim mgron gnyer phyag mdzod sogs
la'ang 'dris zab che chung dang bstun pa'i ja sar skabs su gang bab re stsal ba dang / khyad par dgon de'i rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul dang / 'dus tshogs spyir mang jas
bsnyen bkur ba dang / de'i nang gses rgya khang tshan par mang ja dang ja gsar sogs zab par mdzad de/ tshes brgyad kyi nyin e wa~M pa'i bla khag khang tshan rnams kyis phebs
bsu'i tshogs rgya che ba dang bcas te/ dpal ldan stobs bcu mnga' ba'i lung rtogs kyi bstan pa'i chu klung mtha' dag phyogs gcig tu 'khyil zhing / slar yang bshad pa
dang sgrub pa'i phrin las kyi rgyun chen po phyogs kyi khor yug kun tu 'bebs par byed pa'i gnas yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas shrI e wa~M chos ldan du bde bar phebs/
de nas kyang thog mar gza' skar phun sum tshogs pa'i nyin e wa~M bla brang gzhung du/ rigs dang dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i khyab bdag mkhan chen khri thog pa gcen byams
pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi drung du/ maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ bzang ja 'khor drug bzhi bcu dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu/ rta drel spus ldan drug /pho mdzo
spus ldan gsum/ dar ras ling gos chen spu shun gyi rigs mang po/ mchod cha/ dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs pa dang bcas phul ba dang / bla brang phun tshogs khang gsar
du/ mkhas dang grub pa'i gtsug rgyan ngag dbang blo gros bzang po dang / de'i dbon ngag dbang blo gros bstan 'dzin lhan rgyas pa'i mdun dang / klu ldings bla brang du zhabs

mdun du'ang / sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / bzang ja 'khor drug bco lnga re/ rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu re/ rta drel bzhi re/ mdzo g.yag spus ldan gsum re/ gzhan yang
dar ras ling gos chen spu shun gyi rigs mang po dang / mchod cha dang / dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs pa dang bcas phul ba dang / thar rtse rang du'ang rnam dkar mchod
thebs kyi rten du 'bul ba shin tu stobs che ba dang / gzim khang 'og mkhan rin po che byams pa bsod nams dpal 'byor pa dang / dpon slob rin po che dpal ldan chos kyi rgyal
mtshan pa bcas su'ang 'bul ba gang zab dang / e wa~M pa'i lha khang khag thams cad du'ang mchod 'bul shin tu rgya che ba dang / khyad par gtsug lag khang du nyin re bzhin
brgya mchod re dang bcas te/ dge slong phyed bdun brgya skor bzhugs pa thams cad tshogs te bla ma mchod pa dang / kun rig dang / tshe chog sogs nyin grangs nyi shu rtsa
bdun gyi bar du 'dzugs par mdzad de/ de'ang thog mar nyin bcu gsum la nyin re bzhin grwa pa nyi shu re la phyag 'gyed bzang ja sbag re phul ba dang / de 'phros nyin bcu
bzhi la nyin re bzhin grwa pa re la phyag 'gyed dngul Tam phyed re dang / dngul zho re spel mar stsal ba dang / gtsug lag khang du gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi phye phur
cha dang / rgya mthongs khor yug tu gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi phur ma dang / gos yug gi 'phan bcas gsar sbyor mdzad pa dang / khang tshan bcu gcig po thams cad la'ang so
sor thob khungs dang / khang tshan che chung la dpags pa'i ja sar dang / khyad par rang rang gi skong brgya tshogs pa'i skabs 'phar ja'i bsnyen bkur dang 'brel bar gtan
gzhag zab pa re stsal ba dang / dgon pa'i chos khrims dang / bla khag so so'i phyag gnyer las tshan gyi rigs dang / thar rtse

rang gi las tshan dang / grwa tshang dang / lto zan gyi rigs dang / ngor pa'i chos gzhis mi ser sogs la'ang ja gsar dang gnang sbyin skabs su gang bab re stsal ba dang / gzhan
yang rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sder mang jas bsnyen bkur ba dang / de'i nang gses gur pa grwa tshang par mang 'gyed dang / zhwa lu dang / snar thang dang / srad rgyud
pa dang / srad dgon khra sogs nye skor gyi dgon khag rnams su mang jas bsnyen bkur ba bcas mdzad nas/ hor zla bcu gcig pa'i dmar phyogs kyi dga' ba gnyis pa'i nyin e wa~M
nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur te/ 'phags pa rigs gsum mgon po'i rnam 'phrul rgyun chad med par 'khrungs pa'i yul/ mkhas pa dang grub pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'byung ba'i
gnas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs/ gangs ljongs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun gong ma yab sras rnams kyi gser zhal rin po che mjal ba dang lhan cig sa skya
gzhung gi 'bul bar maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ bzang ja 'khor drug lnga bcu/ rgya dngul 'degs srang brgya tham pa/ rta drel bdun/ gzhan yang dngul las grub pa'i mchod cha'i
rigs dang / dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs pa/ dar ras ling gos chen spu shun gyi rigs mang po dang bcas phul ba dang / khri chen grub pa'i dbang phyug ngag dbang kun
dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po sku sger gyi 'bul bar sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / bzang ja 'khor drug lnga/ dre'u a mdo gcig /dngos chas kyi rigs sna
tshogs pa dang / rje btsun ma 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma'i drung sku sger gyi 'bul bar sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / bzang ja 'khor drug bcu/ rta gcig gi gtsos pa'i tshan
grangs kha shas/ 'jam mgon kun

dga' rin chen gyi drung du sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / ljon 'dab 'khor drug lnga/ dre'u a mdo gcig /dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs pa dang / 'jam mgon dngos grub dpal 'bar
dang / gdung sras rin po che bkra shis rin chen bcas kyi sku sger so sor bzang ja 'khor drug gsum re dang / rta re'i gtsos pa'i tshan grangs dang / dngos chas kyi rigs
sna tshogs pa dang / gzhan yang btsun mo pho brang gi rje btsun ma gsum dang / phun tshogs pho brang gi rje btsun ma dang / khro khang rje btsun ma dang / zhabs brtan lha
khang gi rje btsun ma gnyis dang / rgyal yum dang / bdag mo sogs kyi sku sger so sor ljon ja 'khor drug gnyis re'i gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas re dang / lha khang
mkhan rin po che'i mdun du ljon ja 'khor gnyis kyi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs dang / zhabs pad mdun du'ang bzang ja 'khor drug gnyis dang / gzhan yang gsol gzim dang / mgron
gnyer dang / drung yig dang / lde phyung ba dang / rtswa gnyer dang / shing gnyer sogs la'ang 'dris zab dang bstun pa'i ja sar skabs su gang bab re dang / khyad par chos
sde lho byang gi rten gsum ngo mtshar can rnams kyi drung du mchod 'bul dang / gser gsol dang / snyan dar shin tu zab pa dang / sprul pa'i lha khang chen mor dge 'dun 'dus
pa rgya mtshor mang ja gnyis kyi steng phyag 'gyed grwa pa bco lnga re la bzang ja sbag re phul ba sogs bsod nams kyi tshogs rgya chen po 'du mdzad do/ /hor zla bcu gnyis
pa'i yar ngo'i nang e wa~M du phebs/ don du gnyer ba'i gdul bya 'ga' zhig gis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor dbang rjes gnang lung la sogs pa'i bka' chos ci rigs kyang stsal
ba dang / mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi 'dra sku dang / mchod

rten sogs la'ang rgyud nas bshad pa ltar dang / bla ma gong ma'i phyag len dang mthun par gzungs gzhug rnams tshad dang ldan par phul te/ dgung grangs so gsum pa khyu mchog
gi lo'i cho 'phrul zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi nang / mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po gcen byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin pas rdo rje slob dpon mdzad de rje 'di dang / dge
slong mang pos dpal kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas par mdzad pa dang / zla ba de'i tshes nyi shu'i nyin lam 'bras lha khang du brgya mchod rnam lnga dang bcas
te dge slong bzang gras phal che ba tshogs te bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa'i sgo nas bla ma mchod pa gsung ba dang lhan cig 'dra sku rin po che'ang lam 'bras lha khang
du bzhugs su gsol zhing / de'ang gos chen las grub pa'i bzhugs 'bol dang / gos chen gyi snam sbyar dang / gos chen gyi sku ber dang bcas pa dang / sku mdun du'ang rdo dril
gser mgo ma spus legs dang / dngul srang so bdun las grub pa'i bum pa cha gcig kha rgyan bum gos dang bcas pa dang / dngul srang brgyad dang zho gsum las grub pa'i 'bru
spar dang / dngul srang bcu gnyis dang zho lnga las grub pa'i spyi blugs dang / ting shags spus legs dngul thag dang bcas pa dang / dngul las grub pa'i nang mchod thod pa
dang / zhal dkar yu ring dang / de'i stegs dngul srang bco lnga las grub pa dang / dngul srang bdun dang zho brgyad las grub pa'i phud kong dang / Da ma ru dngul gyi shan
can dang / dngul srang brgyad dang zho gsum las grub pa'i dngul ting bdun tshar dang / dngul srang nyer drug dang zho brgyad las grub pa'i gtor theb lnga tshar 'gu tshe
dang bcas pa dang / dngul srang bcu gsum dang zho lnga las grub pa'i bzed zhal rnams sbyor 'jags mdzad pa dang / hor zla bzhi pa'i nang ngor lugs dkyil 'khor lnga'i sgrub
mchod chen mo tshogs pa'i skabs

kyang / mang ja dang gral 'gyed la sogs pa'i bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs par stsal ba dang / lo de'i hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i nang gnas skor du e wa~M nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/
mar lam rong chen brgyud de lha ldan du phebs/ der zhag nyi shu skor bzhugs/ phyogs de'i rten gsum byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba zhib mjal thog gser gsol dang / mchod
'bul dang / phyag dang skor ba mang du mdzad de rim gyis chibs bteg /yer pa dang / dga' ldan dang / bsam yas skor dang / gdan sa mthil dang / zangs ri mkhar dmar dang
/ rtse thang dang / yar klung bkra shis chos sde dang / shel brag sogs dang / tsandan g.yu'i lha khang dang / ras chung phug dang / khra 'brug dang / gung thang 'bum pa la
sogs pa dang / de nas 'phyong rgyas ri bo bde chen sogs brgyud/ yar 'brog mtsho skor mdzad de de skor gyi dgon sde rnams kyang mjal/ rim gyis rgyal rtse dang zhwa lu brgyud
de/ dgung grangs so bzhi pa chu rta lo'i hor zla gnyis pa'i dkar phyogs kyi dga' ba dang po'i nyin e wa~M du phebs pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i gnas de rnams su'ang gser
gsol dang / mchod 'bul dang / phyag dang skor ba sogs zab par mdzad de bsod nams kyi chu gter dbyar mtsho bzhin du 'phel bar mdzad do/ /mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po
gcen byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin pas kyang lo snga ma lcags sbrul lor e wa~M pa'i mkhan sa bla brang phun tshogs khang gsar par rtsis phul te/ 'di lo hor zla bzhi pa'i
nang mdo khams su chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur/ rje 'di de nas brtsams te/ dgung grangs zhe bdun pa shing mo lug gi lo'i bar du sku'i 'phrod bzhes kyi chu tshan khag rnams su
tshar kha shas phebs pa ma gtogs e wa~M rang du bzhugs/ kun rig gi bsnyen pa zla ba gsum dang / brag rdzong ma'i sku

mtshams zla ba bzhi tsam dang / mkha' spyod ma'i sku mtshams zla ba bzhi tsam dang / 'jam dbyangs dkar po'i sku mtshams zla ba bzhi tsam dang / tshe sgrub zla shas bcas bzhugs
pa dang / der ma zad dus rgyun du'ang sku mtshams kyi ming dmigs bsal ma btags rung / mtshams par rlom pa mang pos kyang 'gran du med pa'i thugs dam kho na la rtse gcig
tu gzhol ba dang / rgyud nas bshad pa ltar gyi bdud rtsi ril bu'i sman rnams 'dzom pa dang bstun lo gnyis gsum re'i mtshams nas bdud rtsi ril bu chig sgrub re chag med
lta bur mdzad pa dang / skabs skabs su bla ma mchod pa dang / yi dam gyi lha 'ga' zhig gi sgrub mchod dang / chos srung rnams la skong gso sogs nyin grangs kha shas re gsung
ba dang / dgung grangs zhe bzhir son pa chu 'brug gi lor/ mkhan chen rdo rjai 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin dang / sde dge chos rgyal chen po byams pa kun dga'
sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan ston 'khor rnams mdo khams nas e wa~M du phebs/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang gcen byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi drung nas dpal kye
rdo rje'i rgyud lam gyi dbang dang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas de'i sngon 'gro thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa dang / bskyed rim rnal
'byor bcu gcig /rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma/ bde ba dang 'ja' lus sgrub pa/ mkha' spyod yab yum gyi 'pho ba/ nang gi mkha' spyod sgrub pa sogs nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i nyams khrid
yongs su rdzogs pa dang / chos nyid dngos su ston pa'i byin rlabs bcas gsan pa dang / sde dge chos rgyal chen po'i drung nas kyang zhal rnam 'gyur bcu bdun gyi rjes su
gnang ba rnams gsan par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang de skabs kyi lo snga phyi kun tu gdul bya so so'i mos pa dang bstun

te zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang ci rigs par stsal ba'i sgo nas 'gro ba rnams rnam par grol ba'i lam la bkod pa dang / lo re gnyis tsam ma gtogs phal che
bar cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes nyi shu'i nyin/ e wa~M pa'i gtsug lag khang du dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor mang ja dang gral 'gyed la sogs pa'i bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs
pa'i sgo nas bla ma mchod pa gsung ba sogs mdor na rnam dkar gyi phrin las kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad do/ /skye 'jig spros pa kun bcad pa'i/ /rgyal rnams 'gro ba sgrol
ba'i slad/ /sna tshogs spro dang bsdu ba yi/ /rnam 'phrul sgyu ma'i rol rtsed bzhin/ /de slad nam mkha'i mtshan can gyi/ /mtshan dpe'i ri bong 'dzin pa yang / /'gro 'di skal
ba dman pa yis/ /bsnyun tshul sprin gyis bsgribs par gyur/ /khyad par rtag par 'dzin pa'i blos/ 'dir snang la chags yid can kun/ /sgrol phyir gzugs sku'i bkod pa yang
/ /dbyings su bstim la chas pa na/ /dus gsum gzigs pa'i ye shes kyi/ /ston ka'i zla shel dag pa las/ /'byung 'gyur ston pa'i bdud rtsi'i zer/ /'gro 'di'i blo mun sel phyir
spros/ /srid na rnyed par dka' ba'i nor/ /dam tshig rdzas rnams rab stsal te/ /chos kyi rgyal por dbang bskur ba/ /thub pas ma pham mgon por bzhin/ /de nas bstan dang
'gro ba'i mig /nyin mo'i dpal de nub gyur kyang / /bdud rtsi'i 'byung gnas 'di'i bzhugs pas/ /thar 'dod yid kyi gdung ba bsal/ /bla gos dmar po'i 'od rdul gyis/ /thun mtshams
chu 'dzin pham bgyid pa/ /khams phyogs ngur smrig 'dzin pa kun/ /rnyed dang bkur stis mnyes par byas/ /khyad par lhag pa'i lha mang po/ /sgrub cing mchod pa'i chu rgyun
gyis/ /bsod nams myu gu skyed

bsrings shing / /thugs kyi rgyal mtsho yongs su bkang / /slar yang sgyu ma'i nor rdzas kun/ /bsod nams phung por bsgyur ba'i slad/ /dbus gtsang ljongs su zhabs bkod de/ /mchod
dang bsnyen bkur ci yang bstabs/ /byin rlabs zil dngar rab g.yo ba'i/ /gangs can ljongs kyi gnas chen rnams/ /gang gi dad dang gus pa yi/ /'dren byed snyim pas legs par
bzung / /mang du thos kyang thos pa btsal/ /grub par gyur kyang sgrub la brtson/ /rang nyid srid zhi'i rtser 'phags kyang / /bstan la gus pa'i sri zhu mdzad// //spyi don
gsum pa bstan pa'i bdag po chen por mnga' gsol nas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul la gsum ste/ thog mar kun mkhyen e wa~M pa chen po'i chos kyi
rgyal srid chen por mnga' gsol nas bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ de nas mi bdag sa'i tshangs pa chen pos spyan drangs te mdo khams su bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar
mdzad pa'i tshul/ slar yang dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du bsnyen bkur rgya cher bstabs te rang gnas gdan sa chen por zhabs bkod de bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i
tshul lo/ /de'i dang po ni/ snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rnam thar gsol 'debs las/ khyab bdag
bla ma'i lung gis dbugs dbyung bzhin/ /rgyal ba gnyis pa'i chos kyi rgyal thabs la/ /bgrang bya bdun gyi bar du dbang bsgyur nas/ /rnam dag lam srol bstan la gsol ba 'debs/
/zhes bka' stsal pa ltar te/ de'ang spyir dam pa 'di nyid ni nang du lung dang rtogs pa'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa la dbang 'byor yang / phyi rol gyi rnam par g.yeng
ba'i spros

pa mtha' dag rmi lam gyi rang bzhin lta bur mngon sum du gzigs pa la brten nas/ sku na chung ngu'i dus nas gcen byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi drung du bdag grwa rkyang
zhig byas te zur du bzhugs chog pa'i snyan sbron yang yang 'bul bar mdzad na'ang / de bzhin mdzad pa zhig ma byung la/ de rjes gong du bshad pa ltar rje 'di mdo khams nas
yar e wa~M du phebs pa'i skabs kyang / sde dge chos rgyal chen pos gcen mkhan chen khri thog pa byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin mdo khams su gdan 'dren zhu mi ched du mngags
par brten/ sa skya nas kyang bla brang rtsis sprod 'phral du bgyis te mdo khams su phebs dgos tshul dang / gal srid rtsis sprod 'grig min yod tshe rje 'di mkhan por bsko
bzhag bgyis chog tshul bka' phebs na'ang / de dag la thugs 'dun gtan nas ma mdzad rung / dgung grangs zhe bdun tu phebs pa myos byed ces pa shing mo lug gi lor phan khang
mkhan rin po che byams pa dpal ldan bzang po e wa~M pa'i mkhan sa dgongs khrol nan tan chen pos zhus par brten/ e wa~M pa'i bla khag khang tshan dang bcas pa thams cad
kyis mgrin gcig tu/ da ni rje 'di kho na kun mkhyen e wa~M pa chen po'i chos kyi rgyal srid chen por mnga' gsol bar 'os so zhes gleng zhing / rje 'di la'ang gsol ba phur
tshugs su btab pa na/ spyir dgon pa'i 'dzin skyong gi khur 'di shes 'khos kyis lcogs dka' bar ma zad/ gal srid bstan pa'i khur blangs kyang chags sdang 'phel ba'i rgyu
kho na las ma 'das pas e wa~M pa'i mkhan sa 'dzin mi dgos pa'i dgongs khrol dgos tshul nan tan gyis bka' stsal rung / e wa~M pa'i bla khag khang tshan thams cad kyis mkhan
por 'os pa rje 'di kho na las gzhan su yang med do zhes dpal ldan sa skya'i 'jam mgon khri

chen rin po che ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po'i gser snyan rin po cher gsol ba na/ des kyang stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba gzhung sa dga' ldan
pho brang ba chen por snyan spron phul te/ de dag nas kyang khyod kyis bstan pa dang sems can gyi don du snying stobs ches cher bskyed de/ kun mkhyen e wa~M pa chen po'i
bstan pa'i khur chen po khyed la spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa rin po che dbyar gyi mtsho bzhin du spel ba dang / 'os su gyur pa'i gdul bya rnams kyang smin grol la bkod
cig ces pa'i bka' stsal gser gyi phreng ba dbyar gyi gru char bzhin du bsnyil ba dang / der ma zad khang sar zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros bstan 'dzin ni
de skabs gling mgo zi dgon du bzhugs pa dang / klu ldings zhabs drung rin po che'ang sde dger phebs par brten/ gzhan mkhan por 'os pa su'ang med gshis re zhig mkhan po zhal
bzhes mi mdzad thabs med du gyur te/ snyigs ma'i sems can mi srun pa'i spyod pa rlung dmar ltar 'tshubs pa'i nang 'dir bstan pa dang sems can la ci nus kyis phan gdags
par bzhed de/ lo de'i hor zla bcu gcig pa mgo zla'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes bco lnga'i nyin yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi gtsug lag
khang chen por bsu ba'i bkod pa lta bas chog mi shes pa'i tshogs dang bcas pas byon te/ lha dang mi dang lha ma yin dang / gnod sbyin dang dri za dang grul bum la sogs pa
thams cad kyi ral pa'i thor tshugs anda rnyil gyi mdog lta bus lan cig ma yin par btud pa'i mi 'jigs gdong lngas bteg pa'i chos kyi khri 'phang 'thon po ga la bar/ zhabs
kyi chu skyes dmar po rnam par bkod de ji ltar gser gyi lhun po gur gum gyi char pas lan brgya stong du bkrus pa la/ slar yang 'char ka'i nyi

'od kyi thigs pas yongs su dran pa bzhin du lham mer bzhugs pa na/ sngon bcom ldan 'das la lha'i dbang po tshangs pa dang / brgya byin gyis bkra shis pa'i rdzas kyis mngon
par mchod de/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba btab pa dang tshul mtshungs par chos kyi dung dang / lam 'bras glegs bam dang / bkra shis pa'i rdzas brgyad la sogs pa sngon
du 'gro ba'i dpal ldan sa skya'i legs 'bul dang / e wa~M pa'i bla brang khag rnams dang / khang tshan bcu gcig dang / gzhan yang grwa rigs sbyin bdag dang bcas pa rnams
nas rang rang gi 'byor pa dang bstun pa'i legs 'bul gyi dngos po ri ltar spungs te/ rgyal bas lung gis bsngags pa'i ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i chos kyi rgyal
srid chen por yongs su mnga' gsol bas skal ba bzang po'i dus kyi chu gter dbyar gyi mtsho bzhin du rgyas par gyur to/ /gzhan yang ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid
kyi dbang bskur ba'i gnas dbang khang du grags pa dang / de'i thog g.yabs chen du grags pa bcas kyi bzhugs khri so so'i steng du'ang khri 'bul zab rgyas dang bcas pas mnga'
gsol zhing / de ltar bgyis pa'i dge tshogs rnams kyang 'khor gsum rnam par mi rtog pa'i bsngo ba'i rgyas 'debs par mdzad pa dang / de lta bu'i dus kyi tshe nam mkha'i
dbyings thams cad kyang 'ja' sprin gyis gang ba la sogs pa bkra shis pa'i ltas mang po'ang / ji ltar padmo rnam par rgyas pa'i tshal du sprang rtsi 'thung ba'i bung ba gzhon
nu'i tshogs rnams ma bsdus par yang ngang gis 'du ba bzhin du mngon sum du lhags par gyur to/ /de ltar chos kyi khri la zhabs sen bkod ma thag pa nas dpal gyi mgur las/
dung gi tshems bar nas 'phrul gyi ljags brkyangs te/ dus gsum

gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i dbu btsugs pa nas bzung ste/ dgung
grangs nga bzhir son pa chu stag lo'i bar mkhan po lo bdun mdzad/ lo re bzhin dgun gyi dus stod smad bar gsum nas 'dus pa'i don du gnyer ba mang dus nyis brgya lhag tsam
dang / nyung dus phyed nyis brgya bskor la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras tshogs bshad kyi smin byed kyi dbang dang / grol byed kyi khrid dang / rgyab rten lung dang bcas
pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i tshar bdun dang / dpyid kyi dus de dag thams cad la dge bsnyen dang / dge tshul dang / dge slong gi sdom pa rnams legs par 'bogs par mdzad cing
/ 'on kyang dgung grangs lnga bcur son pa sa khyi lor lam 'bras grub mtshams su mgul cham lta bus cung zad snyun tshul bzhes pa la brten nas/ de lo'i grwa gsar rnams la
rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa rnams gcen mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyis stsal bar mdzad do/ /gzhan yang de dag gi bar skabs rnams su'ang
gdul bya so so'i mos pa dang bstun te dbang dang / rjes gnang dang / lung la sogs pa chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang ci rigs pa stsal te gdul bya rnams kyi rnam par grol ba'i
lo tog mtha' dag ches cher rgyas par mdzad do/ /chos kyi bdud rtsi stsal ba de dag kyang bstan pa dang sems can gyi don 'ba' zhig la dgongs te/ phyag len phra mo tshun chad
kyang sla chos su ma song bar dgag sgrub kyi bca' ba dam po mdzad pa ni mkhas pa rnams kyis bsngags pa'i gnas su gyur pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar ba zhig go /dgung grangs
zhe dgur son pa me bya lo'i hor zla lnga pa'i nang bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal

ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por khri mjal la phebs te/ sa skya gzhung du maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ tshan grangs dang mchod cha'i rigs sna tshogs pa/ ma hA tsi na'i yul
gyi ljon 'dab 'khor drug bcu gsum/ rgya dngul 'degs srang nyer lnga/ rta gnyis bcas dang / 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan
'dzin bzang po sku sger gyi 'bul bar tshan grangs sna tshogs pa dang / ljon ja 'khor drug lnga/ bod dngul Tam srang bco lnga bcas dang / sngags 'chang grub pa'i dbang phyug
ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen pa dang / bstan dang 'gro ba'i dpal gyur mgon po dngos grub dpal 'bar ba dang / 'jam mgon thams can mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' rgyal mtshan
bcas kyi sku sger so sor tshan grangs rigs sna tshogs pa dang / ljon ja 'khor drug bzhi re bcas dang / gdung sras rin po che ngag dbang rdo rje rin chen pa dang / ngag
dbang bkra shis rin chen bcas kyi sku sger so sor ljon 'dab 'khor drug gnyis re'i gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas re dang / rje btsun ma khag rnams dang / lha khang mkhan
rin po che dang / sa skya zhabs pad bcas su'ang ljon ja 'khor drug re re'i gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas dang / gzhan yang gsol gzim mchod gsum dang / mgron gnyer
dang / drung yig dang / lde phyung ba dang / rtswa gnyer dang / shing gnyer sogs la'ang rang rang gi go babs dang bstun pa'i gnang sbyin gang la gang 'os dang / khyad par
chos sde lho byang gi lha khang khag rnams su bzhugs pa'i rten gsum ngo mtshar ba rnams kyi mdun du mchod pa'i khyad par shin tu rgya che ba dang / sprul pa'i lha khang
chen mor dge 'dun 'dus pa brgya mtsho'i tshogs la mang ja gral 'gyed dang bcas pa'i bsnyen bkur

phun sum tshogs pa stob par mdzad cing / de skabs 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che nas/ sngon gyi dus su ngor pa zhes thams cad kyis sgrig lam dam pa'i tshad bzhag sa lta bu
yin na'ang / dus phyis dge 'dun gyi sgrig je lhod je yang du song bar brten/ da cha sngar gyi rtsis nas sgrig lam med pa lta bur song yod tshod du 'dug gshis/ 'di nas kyang
mkhan po snga ma rim can la sgrig lam bsdam dgos tshul gleng ba yin na'ang / 'di byas zhes ston rgyu yod pa zhig ma byung bas/ da cha khyed kyis dge 'dun gyi sgrig lam
mtha' dag sngar bzhin sor chud pa zhig bya dgos so zhes bka' stsal rin po che gser gyi cod pan lta bu shin tu lci ba phebs rung / spyir dge 'dun gyi sgrig lam sngar ltar
sor chud pa zhig byung na legs pa bzhir bcas kyang / de bzhin bgyis tshe dus dbang gis ci 'gyur ma rtogs pas/ de ltar mi dgos pa'i dgongs khrol nan tan gyis zhu bar mdzad
na'ang / sgrig lam ma bsdams thabs med yin tshul dang / 'di nas kyang bla grwa tshang mar bka' shog cig stsal chog tshul gsungs pa bzhin bka' shog cig kyang stsal bar brten/
rjes nas rim gyis snyan sbron phul chog par gsol nas e wa~M du phebs te/ ji skad du legs par bshad pa rin po che'i gter las/ rang gis legs par shes na yang / /bya ba
thams cad gros kyis bsgrub/ /mi gang gros la mi dga' ba/ /'gyod pa rin gyis nyo ba yin/ /zhes 'byung ba ltar lo de'i hor zla bcu pa'i nang mdo khams nas gcen mkhan chen
rdo rje 'chang dpon 'khor rnams e wa~M du ma phebs kyi bar la bka' shog su la'ang bstan par ma mdzad cing / de rjes gcen mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dang / gcung mdzod pa
nor ldan shes rab bzang po bcas bka' bgros te/ bstan pa'i don kho na

las rang gi don ni ci yang med gshis bzang ngan ci 'gyur yang sgrig lam bsdam par thugs thag bcad de/ sa skya nas stsal ba'i bka' shog thams cad la bstan zhing / gtso cher
sems dpa' chen po'i bca' yig ltar dang / de'i rgyab skyor du bca' yig gsar pa zhig kyang bzos te/ mchog dman kun gyis de bzhin byed dgos tshul gsungs pas/ thams cad kyis
de bzhin byed par khas blangs te thil tshe 'dzugs pa'i skabs/ yid srubs kyis rgyud bslad pa'i skye bo ngan pa ngan 'gro'i g.yang sar mngon sum du rgyug par rtsom pa kha cig
gis dkrugs pa'i rkyen gyis ji skad du/ shes rab med pa'i blun po rnams/ /mang yang dgra yi dbang du 'gro/ /zhes pa ltar mi nyag khang tshan pas thil tshe ma btsugs par
brten rim gyis zlos gzhi je cher gyur te e wa~M pa'i bla khag lnga dang / khang tshan bcu phyogs gcig dang mi nyag khang tshan phyogs gcig tu byas te thog mar sa skya dang
/ de nas gzhis rtse rdzong dang / de rjes mda' dpon lcang lo can pa rnams su rim gyis gtugs te 'khrugs long je cher 'phel bar gyur rung / rje 'di'i mnal lam gyi gsal snang
du/ gzim chung gi thog tu rgyal mtshan gyi srog shing zhig brtan par btsugs te/ de la rgyal mtshan gsar du bskon pa dang / yang bsang dar chen po zhig btsugs par phyogs
gzhan zhig nas me chen po zhig 'bar te bsreg par brtsams kyang bsreg par ma nus pa la sogs pa'i mtshan ltas 'ga' zhig byung bar brten/ rang re rnams kyis sangs rgyas
kyi bstan pa kho na bsams te dge 'dun gyi sgrig lam bsdams pa la/ bdud kyi ris kyis glags ltas par gyur na'ang / da ni mi ring bar yid srubs kyi dpung las rnam par rgyal
bar 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan pa bzhin/ de kho na ltar mi ring bar pha rol po'i

gtso bor gyur pa rnams kyis da ni rang re rnams yul 'dir mi chags pas 'gro bar 'os so zhes smras te/ mi 'dod bzhin du pha rol gyi grwa mang thams cad khrid de song ba na/ de'i
rjes su mda' dpon lcang lo can pa 'khor bcas kyang byon te/ pa rnam du 'phrad pa na pha rol po de dag nang 'khrugs kyi rnam pas grwa mang rnams kyis gtso bo rnams 'di
dang 'di yin no zhes dngos su smos pa la brten nas/ mda' dpon pas kyang gtso bo de rnams tshar bcad cing / de 'phros kyi grwa mang rnams kyang tshur 'ongs te sgrig lam mtha'
dag tshul bzhin du bsrung bar khas blangs par gyur to/ /'di lta bu ni chos skyong ba'i srung ma rnams kyis phrin las bsgrubs pa yin par gor ma chag go /mdor na de sngon
du dgon pa'i sgrig lam phal cher zhig ste mgo med 'jug med lta bur song yang / deng skabs sgrig lam skyon med lta bu yod pa 'di ni rje 'di dang / de'i phrin las pa gcung
mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang po bcas kyi bka' drin las byung ba yin no/ /gzhan yang dgon pa'i gtong sgo dang / dus dang khyad par gyi mchod pa rnams kyang sngar las
gong 'phel du mdzad pa dang / sa mchod chen mo'i skabs khyer rgyu'i gos chen gyi yo byad rnying song phal cher kyang gsar du bzos pa dang / gong du mkhan chen rdo rje
'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar gyi rje 'di sku mched rnams nas gtsug lag gi tshogs 'bol yongs su rdzogs pa gsar bzos dang / de'i steng
gi grum rtse'i gral gdan rnams gsar sbyor mdzad pa bcas la'ang rin chen gnyis pa rdo tshad mang du song ba dang / rab byung bsnyen rdzogs stsal ba'i skabs kyi mkhan slob
las grwa dang bcas pa'i snam sbyar rnams kyang gsar bzos mdzad pa sogs mdor na lha khang steng shod thams

cad du nyams gso dgos rigs yongs su rdzogs pa nyams gsos phul du phyin par mdzad pa dang / khyad par e wa~M pa'i mgon khang shar du sngon zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes nyer
drug nas nyer dgu'i bar la bstod gsar rnying gi dbyangs shes rigs rnams tshogs te/ mgon po che chung gi skong ba dang 'brel bar nyin bzhi la bstod gsar rnying gi dbyangs
yongs su rdzogs pa tshar re 'gro bar byed pa'i rgyun mchis pa la/ bar skabs zhig nas dpon slob tshogs la ma byon pa'i rkyen gyis chad song bar brten/ dus phyis ngor pa'i
dbyangs chen bco brgyad kyi rgyun chad la khad du gyur na'ang / bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'dis zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes nyer drug nas nyer dgu'i bar la skong
ba rnams sngar bzhin 'dzugs par mdzad pa la brten nas deng skabs dbyangs chen bco brgyad kyi rgyun ma nub par gnas pa 'di'ang rje bla ma dam pa 'di'i bka' drin las byung
ba yin la/ de skabs su bod dang sing gi rgyal khab 'khrugs pa'i rkyen gyis dbus gtsang thams cad du zings cha che bar byung na'ang / e wa~M pa'i chos gzhis mi ser thams
cad sngar rgyun las nyams chag tu ma song bar mgo 'don dpyis phyin par mdzad pa sogs lugs gnyis char gyi sgo nas bka' drin phul du byung ba yin no/ /gzhan yang snga phyir
bdud rtsi ril bu chig sgrub tshar kha shas mdzad pa dang / rang nyid mang du thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son kyang / ji skad du/ mkhas pa yon tan mdzod 'dzin pa/
/de dag legs bshad rin chen sdud/ /rgya mtsho chen po chu bo'i gter/ /yin phyir chu bo thams cad 'bab/ /ces pa ltar chu stag lor rtsod pa'i dus kyi kun mkhyen bu ston gnyis
pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong e wa~M du phebs pa na

de'i drung nas dpal phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i bya rgyud nor can gyi rigs su gtogs pa'i rgyal chen rnam thos sras bka' mi 'dra ba bcu
drug dang / rnam sras snyan grags sgrub pa bcas kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / bya rgyud gshegs rigs kyi bdag po 'phags pa 'od zer dri ma med pa thub dbang lha bdun ma'i
dbang bskur ba bcas gsan pa dang / yang zhwa ser gyi cod pan 'dzin pa'i bstan 'dzin rnams kyi gtsug rgyan bcu phrag rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta a mdo bkra shis 'khyil gyi brag
dgon zhabs drung rin po che dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas e wa~M du phebs pa na/ de'i drung nas kyang theg pa chen po'i gso sbyong gi sdom pa dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang
chos grags kyi yig cha'i steng nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa'i thugs dam lha bzhir grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba rnams dang / bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi pho nya
mo dbyangs can ma dkar mo sa manta shrI nas brgyud pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i rjes gnang tshig lhug pa dang / de'i sgrub thabs las sbyor tshigs bcad ma bcas thugs
sras rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa dang / bo dong paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa rgyan gyis phreng ba bcas kyi lung / rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i pha rgyud mi bskyod
pa'i rigs kyi khro bo phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po lha bco brgyad kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil 'dul 'dzin grags pa rgyal
mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i lung bcas/ dkon mchog lhun grub yig steng nas dpal phyag na rdo rje u tsarYa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / pha rgyud rnam snang gi rigs su gtogs pa grub
chen dpal 'dzin gyis legs par bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das gshin rje'i gshed dmar po lha bcu gsum

ma'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ bu ston rin po che'i sgrub dkyil gnyis kyi lung dang bcas pa/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub kyi yig cha'i steng nas dgra nag
gi rgyud nas bstan pa'i 'phags ma dbyangs can ma dmar mo gsang sgrub kyi rjes su gnang ba/ de'i sgrub rjes 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang pos mdzad pa'i
lung bcas/ paN chen dpal ldan ye shes kyi nag 'gros steng nas dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi phyag mtshan mda' gzhu la brten nas bi Sha bsad pa'i las tshogs dug dbang rma
bya rgyas pa dang / ma rgyud he ru ka'i rigs su gtogs pa grub chen dril bu lugs kyi bde mchog phyi dkyil lha lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i
sgrub dkyil thugs sras lo tsA bas mdzad pa'i lung dang bcas pa/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa rnal 'byor gsang mtha' ltar bkral ba zab don dril bu pa'i lugs kyi bde mchog lus dkyil
gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ de'i sgrub thabs dang / bdag 'jug gi sdom dang / bdag nyid 'jug pa dang bcas pa 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i lung bcas/ ngag dbang
mchog legs rdo rje yig cha'i steng nas ma rgyud padma gar dbang gi rigs su gtogs pa rje ras pa badzra kIrti nas brgyud pa'i rta mgrin pad dbyug can gyi rjes su gnang
ba dang / ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje'i yig steng nas dpal kye rdo rje'i bshad rgyud gur nas gsungs pa'i 'byung 'dul sems dpa' sum brtsegs kyi rjes gnang me dbang gsum
dang bcas pa/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams kyi yig cha'i steng nas tshogs bdag dmar chen khyad par can gyi rjes su gnang ba dang / dmar chen thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes
gnang bdag chen blo gros rgyal

mtshan gyi yig cha la bla ma brgyud pa'i phyag bzhes 'khrul med kyis brgyan te legs par gsan par mdzad do/ /dgung grangs nga gsum pa lcags mo glang gi lor sa skya'i 'jam mgon
khri chen rin po che ngag dbang rdo rje rin chen par e wa~M pa'i mkhan po dgongs khrol zhu bar mdzad na'ang deng skabs e wa~M pa'i bstan pa'i nyams la phan pa thar rtse
kho nar 'dug gshis/ re zhig dgongs khrol mi 'ong tshul bka' phebs par brten/ de lo'i bka' chos stsal ba sogs mdzad de/ slar yang dgung grangs nga bzhir son pa dge byed
ces pa chu pho stag gi lor/ yang bskyar gyis dgongs khrol nan cher zhu bar mdzad pa la brten nas rim gyis mchog dman thams cad nas dgongs pa khrol te/ lo de'i hor zla bcu
gcig pa'i gza' skar legs 'dzom gyi nyin bstan dang 'gro ba'i dpal mgon khang sar ngag dbang blo gros bstan 'dzin pa nyid kun mkhyen e wa~M pa chen po'i chos kyi rgyal srid
chen por yongs su mnga' gsol zhing / rtsis sprod kyi skor yang sngar rtsis ji ltar blangs pa ltar las nyams chag spu tsam yang ma song ba'i khar nyams gsos dang / gsar
gzos la sogs pa'i sgo nas shin tu dngos gtsang par mdzad de rtsis phul ba dang / gsar du sbyong 'jags stsal ba'i skor la'ang / gtsug lag khang gi bzhugs khri'i steng du
bzhugs 'bol gsum dang sku bsnyes dang / khri khebs rnams gos chen bzang gos sha stag las grub pa dang / bzhugs khri'i g.yas g.yon gyi ka ba gnyis su gos chen bzang bsgrigs
kyi 'phan chung cha gcig dang / gsol lcog rtsi ldan gos chen gyi khebs dang bcas pa dang / dbu chos kyi bzhugs 'bol dang / tshogs 'bol lwa ba dmar po'i g.yogs dang rgyab
sha re da las byas pa ring thung bzhi bcu zhe gnyis dang / de'i

steng du gding rgyu'i grum rtse spus ldan grangs de dang mtshungs pa/ rgyun gyi sgrub mchod rnams kyi dkyil 'khor bsham sa'i gzhi lcog cha gcig dang / de'i steng du gos chen
las grub pa'i gzhi khebs dang / shing la bris pa'i kun rig gi dkyil 'khor zhabs khebs shubs dang bcas pa dang / 'khar li las grub pa'i spos 'dzin brgya tham pa snod dang
bcas pa dang / rgya rag gi ting phor 'gags gzugs ma bdun tshar dang / zangs thebs bco lnga dang / zangs kyi pad sder dngul shan can cha gcig dang / yang 'khar rag gi spos
'dzin bzhi dang / gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi rten khebs nyer lnga dang / sgrub mchod skabs kyi phyi rol gtor ma'i stegs dang / ting phor chung ngu bdun tshar dang / zangs
theb gcig bcas dang / gtsug lag gi rgya mthongs khor yug tu gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi phur ma dang / gos chen gyi phye phur che legs cha gcig bcas dang / g.yabs chen
du gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi snam sbyar dgu dang / ther ma'i chos gos gnyis dang / sa mchod skabs khyer rgyu'i bsang dar dang / rgyal mtshan dang / sbyin bdag hwa shang
gi gos la sogs pa gsar bzos rnam grangs mang ba dang / 'khar rnga che legs gcig dang / sa ga zla ba'i sgrub mchod chen mo'i skabs bsham rgyu'i kye rdor dkyil 'khor gyi yol
ba gos chen dpyad ldan ljang gu las grub pa shin tu spus legs pa dang / lam 'bras lha khang du ras kyi snam sbyar kha gsar drug dang / ther ma'i gding ba drug bcas dang
/ mgon khang nub tu chos srung rnams kyi spyan gzigs su rgya dngul rdo tshad gnyis las grub pa'i dngul dam che legs cha gcig dang / mgon khang shar du zla ba byung ngo
cog

gi tshes nyer drug nas nyer dgu'i bar la skong ba tshogs rgyu'i rgyun 'dzugs par mdzad pa la/ sngon gyi dus gsol chas rkyang pa las yon 'bul med kyang / dge 'dun zhal grangs
rim 'phar yong res rab gsal du Tam srang bdun cu don lnga sbyor 'jags stsal ba bed gang byung gis dge slong re la nyin bzhi bsdoms phyag 'gyed Tam re phul rgyu mdzad pa
dang / gzhan yang gzim chung nub tu rkang gling gri rkang zangs dkris rag shan can dang / deng skabs g.yabs chen du bzhugs pa'i rten gtso thub chen la gos chen bzang bsgrigs
kyi snam sbyar dang / ka drug steng gi 'bol dang grum rtse rnams gsar brjes stsal ba sogs mdor na gsar sbyor rgya che ba dang bcas rtsis phul te bstan pa rin po che
gong 'phel du gyur par mdzad pa yin no/ /phan bde'i ri bong can bskyed pas/ /bdud rtsi'i chu gter nyid do zhes/ /rgyal bas lung gis mnga' gsol ba'i/ /mi mchog kun dga' bzang
po des/ /zab rgyas chos kyi nyin byed kyis/ /'khor ba'i mun pa skrod pa'i gnas/ /mi 'jigs gdong lngas bteg pa'i khri/ /srid zhi'i gtsug na 'phags pa der/ /shis pa'i mtshan
ris ngoms pa yi/ /zhabs kyi chu skyes rnam bkod pas/ /bskal ba bzang po'i dga' ston ni/ /rdzogs ldan dus kyi dpal la 'dzegs/ /rab brjid gser gyi lhun po'i spor/ /'char
ka'i nyi gzhon gyis 'khyud cing / /chos kyi bdud rtsi sbyin byed na/ /mgon po khyod dang mtshungs par 'gyur/ /de tshe ngo mtshar phung po kun/ /gcig tu tshogs pa'i ya
mtshan gyis/ /srid gsum byed por rlom rnams kyi/ /khengs pa'i ngal ba 'phrogs kyis dogs/ /zab rgyas chos kyi gru char gyis/ /rnam grol lo tog skyed bsrings pa/ /thub dbang
kho na'i rjes 'gro ste/ /gzhan pa'i dper 'os

srid ma yin/ /zla ba'i zer gyis mi 'phrog cing / /nyi ma'i 'od kyis mi bzlog pa'i/ /'gro 'di'i ma rig mun pa kun/ /khyod kyi thugs rjes bsal bar byas/ /khyad par legs gsungs
'dul ba'i khrims/ /sa bzhin bstan pa'i gzhi ma ste/ /de slad nyes par spyod pa'i chu/ /sdom pa'i chu lon gyis bzlog tshe/ /bdud kyis bslad pa'i skye bo 'ga'/ /bsod nams
zad pa'i sta gon du/ /bstan la sdang ba'i bsam sbyor gyis/ /log pa'i lam du bkri bar brtsams/ /ji ltar ngan pa'i lam zhugs pa'i/ /bu la ma ni brtse ba ltar/ /de dag ngan
'gror lhung dogs pas/ /mgon khyod thugs rje lhag par 'phel/ /'on te bstan srung che rnams kyis/ /las ni 'di nyid yin pa'i phyir/ /me la lceb pa'i 'bu bzhin tu/ /phas rgol
nus pa nyams par byas/ /'dam skyes 'dam gyis ma gos bzhin/ /'khor bar gnas kyang srid pa yi/ /skyon gyis gzhar yang mi gos pa'i/ /thar pa'i rgyal mtshan bstan par btsugs/
/ngo mtshar byin rlabs 'bum g.yo ba'i/ /sngon byon mkhas pa'i phyag bzhes rgyun/ /deng dus pad rtsa ltar phra ba/ /khyod kyis yar ngo'i zla bzhin spel/ /mdor na chos dang
srid gnyis ka'i/ /'byor pa bla na med pa yis/ /bstan dang 'gro ba'i bde skyid ni/ /nyi mas padmo bzhin du byas// //gnyis pa mi bdag sa'i tshangs pa chen pos spyan drangs
te mdo khams su bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ kun gzigs 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rnam thar gsol 'debs las/
slar yang sde bzhi dge bcu'i nor 'dzin ljongs/ /gang zhabs bsod nams mgron du thob pa'i mod/ /bsdu ba'i dngos po rnam

bzhis bstan dang 'gror/ /phan bde'i dga' ston spel la gsol ba 'debs/ /chos brgyad snang ba rmi lam ltar gzigs pas/ /dgos med tshe 'di'i bya ba ring btang nas/ /rtag tu chos
bzhin spyod pa lhur mdzad phyir/ /kun gyis dam par bsngags la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes bka' stsal pa ltar te/ de'ang dgung grangs nga bzhi pa chu stag lo'i mgor/ skabs shig
mnal lam du mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang nam mkha' mtshan can de nyid 'khor zhabs 'bring ba gcig dang bcas byon te/ gsung 'phros 'ga' zhig mdzad par gzhan rnams cher ma gsan/
da ni 'gro ba'i dus la bab po gsungs pa de gsal bar gsan pa zhig byung la/ gnas tshul de bzhin rje 'dis zhabs 'bring ba dag la bka' stsal pa na/ thams cad kyis sku tshe
la bar chad yod pa min nam zhes gleng ba byung zhing / gang ltar yang khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyis sngar dngos dang nyams kyi snang bar ji ltar
lung bstan pa bzhin du lo'i mjug tu sde dge bla chen byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan zhi bar gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs sgrub pa dang / rje 'di gdan
'dren zhu bar sde dge'i sku tshab bye tham glo pa shes rab bzang po dang / yon tan phun tshogs dang / bkra shis rgya mtsho sogs dpon 'khor rnams 'byon par/ khong rnams nas
kyang sde dge chos rgyal chen po dam tshig rdo rje tshe ring rnam rgyal pa'i zhu yig 'bul ba dang 'brel bar/ mdo khams kyi bstan 'gro'i mgon du chibs kyi kha lo ma bsgyur
thabs med yin tshul gyis gsol ba phur tshugs su btab pa la brten/ mi 'byon thabs med lta bus rim gyis zhal gyis bzhes te don gnyer 'ga' la chos kyi bdud

rtsi'ang ci rigs par stsal ba dang / mdo khams su phebs rgyu'i nyer bsdogs rnams kyang ji ltar 'os par brtsams te/ dgung grangs nga lngar son pa mdzes byed ces pa chu yos kyi
lo'i hor zla gsum pa'i nang gangs ljongs bsod nams kyi mgron du khugs pa'i chos grwa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs/ der bzhugs pa'i bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku
ngo khag rnams kyi gser zhal rin po che mjal ba dang chabs cig 'bul ba'i dngos po ci rigs par phul ba dang / ye shes pa mngon sum du bzhugs pa'i rten gsum byin rlabs kyi
gzi 'od 'bar ba rnams su mchod 'bul dang / sprus pa'i lha khang chen mor 'dus tshogs su mang jas bsnyen bkur ba bcas mdzad nas e wa~M du phebs/ der yang lha khang khag rnams
su mchod 'bul dang / chos srung rnams la skong ba dang / yul lhar bsang mchod la sogs pa skabs su bab pa'i rim gro'i rigs kyang rgya che bar mdzad de/ lo de'i hor zla
lnga pa'i dkar phyogs kyi rgyal ba dang po'i nyin mchog sprul rin po che 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dang bcas ston 'khor lhan cig tu sngon bcom ldan 'das la 'khor dgra bcom
pa rnams kyis bskor te ljongs rgyu ba bzhin du spyi dang bye brag gi chibs skyel gyi tshogs shin tu rgya che ba dang bcas te e wa~M nas chibs bteg /mar lam chos grwa chen
po bkra shis lhun por phebs/ /paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa rje btsun blo bzang dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi ma gser zhal rin po che mjal ba dang / rten gsum yongs la mchod
'bul sogs mdzad de rim gyis lha ldan du phebs/ 'phags mchog phyag na padmo'i rnam 'phrul rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa mkhas grub rgya mtsho dang / srid skyong tshe smon
gling pa sogs

mjal ba dang / khyad par ston mchog thub pa'i dbang po'i sku brnyan rnam pa gnyis kyi gtso byas pa'i rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul dang thugs smon sogs zhib par mdzad nas chibs
kyi gdong bsgyur te/ ji skad du/ sangs rgyas nyi ma gdul bya yi/ /ri la ji ltar 'os pa 'babs/ /zhes pa ltar/ shin tu bgrod par dka' ba'i la lung mang po rim gyis brgal
zhing / 'os su gyur pa'i gdul bya rnams la chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang ci rigs par stsol bzhin pa'i sgo nas bod chen po'i ljongs su phebs par gyur to/ /de nas mdo smad sde
bzhi dang dge bcu'i dpal gyis mngon par sgeg pa'i rgyal khab nas mi bdag sa'i tshangs pa chen po'i snga phyir chibs bsu'i tshogs dbyar gyi chu 'dzin 'khrigs pa bzhin du lhags
pa rnams dang lhan cig tu byon/ khyad par du dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i ser sbreng gi bkod pa lta bas chog mi shes pa/ ji ltar bye ru'i
'khri shing tshar du dngar ba la/ dbang gzhu'i ri mos mdzes par spud pas kyang dper bya bar mi bzod pa'i ngo mtshar gyi phung po chen po skye bo rnams kyi mig dang yid
kyi brtan pa cig car du 'phrog pa rnams kyis mdun nas bsus te/ khrums zla'i dkar phyogs kyi rgyal ba gsum pa'i nyin mdo khams zal mo sgang gi sa'i thig le sde dge lhun grub
steng gi rgyal khab chen po mi mthun pa'i phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba ga la bar nye 'tshe'i dri ma med pa bde par phebs par gyur to/ /der 'khod pa'i 'gro ba
mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad kyi kyang mtshan dpe'i bkod pa mngon sum du mig gi bdud rtsir gyur cing / legs par gsungs pa'i sgra dbyangs rna ba'i bcud du son pas spro
ba mchog gi shing rta'i rtse mor 'dzegs par gyur to/ /

de nyin chos rgyal mchog nas kyang thog mar 'os pa'i dga' ston gya nom pa bstabs pa dang / rje 'dis kyang chos rgyal chen po'i mdun du thog ma'i zhal mjal la rong gi tshul
du bkra shis pa'i lha gos dang / sku gsung thugs kyi rten khyad par du 'phags pa du mas thog drangs/ legs 'bul gyi dngos po rgya che zhing dpangs mi dman pa phul ba dang
/ de nas rim gyis chos rgyal chen po sku sger dang / de'i sku mched sde dge bla chen byams pa kun dga' 'jam dpal phan bde'i snying po dang / de'i gcung tshe dbang rdo rje
dgra 'dul la sogs pa'i sku ngo khag rnams dang / bka'i blon chen rigs dang / phyag mdzod dang / tshong dpon dang / mdun skor la sogs pa rnams dang / dgon pa'i bla ma dbu
chos la sogs pa rnams la'ang rang rang gi go babs dang bstun pa'i la rong gi 'bul ba dang gnang sbyin sogs zab par mdzad/ khyad par zla ba de'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin mdo
smad kyi bstan 'gro yongs kyi mgon dang skyabs dang dpung gnyen dam par yongs su mnga' gsol ba'i slad du/ rje 'di ston 'khor gyi tshogs dang bcas pa dpal ldan lhun grub
steng gi gtsug lag khang chen por spyan drangs te/ sngon e wa~M pa'i mkhan po rim byon thams cad kyi zhabs kyi chu skyes rnam par bkod pa'i seng ges bteg pa'i rin po che'i
khri 'phang mthon por zhabs mthil 'khor lo'i re khA rnam par bkod de bzhugs su gsol zhing / de nas ji skad du mdo rgya che rol pa las/ khyod kyis sngon chad dge las bsags
pa dang / /yun ring dus kyi dge bas byung ba dang / /khyod kyis chos rnams kun gyi tshul sbyangs pas/ /de ring mchod pa rgya chen byung bar gyur/ /ces 'byung ba ltar bod
chen po'i ljongs kyi skye rgu yongs kyi bdag po chos rgyal byang chub sems

dpa' mchog nas snga na med pa'i dad pa dang spro ba'i 'dzum rlabs khongs nas g.yo bzhin pa'i sgo nas bkra shis pa'i ri mos mngon par 'khyud pa'i lha rdzas kundA ltar dkar ba
dang / sku rten du rgyal ba tshe mtha' yas pa la sogs pa'i sku brnyan du ma dang / gsung rten du 'phags yul gyi mkhas dang grub pa rnams kyi bstan bcos gangs can gyi ljongs
su 'gyur ro 'tshal dang / thugs kyi rten du bka' gdams mchod rten la sogs pa'i mchod rten kha shas dang / bkra shis pa'i rdzas brgyad la sogs pa sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo
nas lha dang mi'i 'jig rten na shin tu rin thang che zhing rnyed par dka' ba'i nor gyi mchog rnam grangs shin tu mang po'i legs 'bul gya nom pa bstabs pa dang / de dag
gi skabs su rdo rje 'dzin pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho pa 'dus tshogs dang bcas pas tshe dpag tu med pa lha dgu'i cho ga dang 'brel ba'i sgo nas zhabs pad brtan pa'i rten 'byung
bsgrigs/ mkhas pa'i dbang po shar bla ma kun dga' dpal ldan pas phun sum tshogs pa lnga dang / maNDal gyi bshad pa rgya cher spros/ gnyer chen rgya mkhar dge legs kyi
tshig don rmad du byung ba'i legs 'bul gyi yi ge brjod ba dag cing gsangs mtho bar bsgrags/ de'i rjes su chos rgyal chen po'i sku'i 'gal rkyen sel ba'i bla ma dang / chos
khrims dang / grwa tshang dang / bka'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i mdun na 'don chen po rnams dang / phyag mdzod dang / mdun skor dang / tshong dpon dang / dpon skya dang / hor
'dra rnams dang / lhun grub steng du gnyug mar bzhugs pa'i bla ma dang / slob dpon dang / chos khrims dang / spyi pa'i dus ja khag rnams dang / gzhan yang dge tshul slong
rab tu mang po dang / rdzong khag chen po rnams kyi mnga' 'og tu gtogs so

'tshal gyi bla ma dang / mi dpon dang / dgon pa dang / khyim bdag 'byor pa dang ldan pa rnams te/ de dag so so nas kyang rmad du byung ba'i dad pa dang spro ba'i chu gter gyen
du 'phyur ba'i stobs kyis legs 'bul gyi dngos po rgya che zhing dpangs mi dman pa sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i dpal dang longs spyod kyi ngo mtshar la'ang co 'dri bar byed pa
dag brtsegs te/ mdo khams kyi bstan 'gro'i mgon du legs par mnga' gsol bas skal ba bzang po'i sprin phung gsar du 'khrigs par gyur to/ /de ltar bgyis pa'i dge ba'i rtsa
ba thams cad kyang bsngo ba'i yon bshad kyi 'bel gtam rgyas par spro bas mtshams sbyar te bar ma dor chud mi za ba'i slad du 'khor gsum rnam par mi rtog pa'i shes rab kyis
bla na med pa'i byang chub chen por yongs su bsngo ba'i rgyas 'debs par mdzad pa dang / der 'dus pa'i skye bo rnams kyang ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i thugs dam
gyi lha khyad par can gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma lha dgu'i 'chi med tshe'i rjes su gnang ba'i chos kyi bdud rtsis yid yongs su tshim par mdzad do/ /de dag gi dus kyi tshe'ang
nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad kha dog sna tshogs pa'i dbang po'i gzhu ris pa tra'i ri mo ltar 'khyil ba dang / ljon shing ltar gyes pa dang / ba dan ltar 'phyang ba
la sogs pa'i ngo mtshar ba'i bkod pa mang po'ang gsar du shar bar gyur to/ /de nas bzung ste dgung grangs drug cu pa sa pho spre'u lo'i bar mdo khams su bzhugs pa'i skabs/
mdo smad kyi phyogs 'ga' dang / chos rgyal chen po'i chab srid la'ang cung zad mtho 'tsham pa rtse ba'i tshos lor grags pa'i khrom pa sde dang bcas la dpung gi sbyor ba
bshams pa tsam gyis dbang du 'dus pas mtshon/ rje nyid kyi

thugs rje'i byin rlabs tshad med pas bdag po chen po sku mched rnams kyang sku la snyun med cing / mnga' ris su gtogs pa mtha' dag 'byor pa/ rgyas pa/ bde ba/ lo legs pa sogs
sde bzhi'i dge mtshan gyi dpal rab tu rgyas shing / me pho rta'i lor sbyin bdag chen po'i lcam snga ma la rigs brgyud med pas/ dar mdo lcags la'i sras mo khab tu bzhes
pa'i tshe'ang legs lam gyi snang ba brgyas par spel ba'i thugs dam skyabs 'jug gi bka' drin bskyangs pa la brten nas sprul pa'i gdung rabs rgyun mi 'chad pa'i dge mtshan
mngon du gyur/ des mtshon te 'bri chu rong 'grim gyi me tog la lan cig dang / rdza khog dang sga stod kyi phyogs su lan cig dang / smad shod phyogs su sbyin bdag dad pa
can rnams kyis gdan drangs pa'i ngor lan bzhi tsam phebs/ de thams cad du'ang 'phral yun gyi 'gal rkyen mtha' dag zhi zhing / mthun rkyen legs tshogs thams cad gong 'phel
du mdzad pa dang / khyad par du'ang gdul bya so so'i blo'i rim pa dang bstun pa'i zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor te/ skye bo phal che ba
ni dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su song zhing bslab pa'i gzhi bzung ba la bkod/ 'ga' zhig ni khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byung ste 'khor ba las mngon par 'phags pa'i gnas
la bkod/ la la ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa stsal te theg pa chen po'i rigs su bkod/ la la ni gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i chos
kyi sgor smin par byas te ring por mi thogs par rnam par grol ba'i skal ba dang ldan par mdzad do/ /mdor na skye bo phal che ba sangs rgyas la gzhol ba dang /

dam pa'i chos la 'babs pa dang / dge 'dun la bzhag par mdzad de ston mchog thub pa'i dbang po'i bstan pa rin po che nyi 'od kyis phyes pa'i padmo bzhin du rnam par rgyas par
mdzad do/ /gzhan yang bdag nyin chen po 'dis ni spangs pa dang rtogs pa'i yon tan thams cad bum nang gi mar me bzhin rnam pa kun tu sba bar mdzad pa ma gtogs/ don la grub
pa'i go 'phang mthon por gshegs shing / stobs dang rdzu 'phrul thams cad kyang 'phags yul gyi grub pa'i slob dpon chen po rnams dang khyad par cung zad kyang med par mngon
te/ rgyu mtshan ci'i phyir zhe na/ rje 'di dgung grangs nga drug tu phebs pa'i shing pho 'brug gi lor smad shod gdong sna bla brang gis gdan drangs te smad shod du tshar
dang po phebs pa'i skabs tshur lam hag la shug rtsibs zer ba der sku bsangs zhig mdzad zhor du/ shin tu sra zhing mkhregs pa'i rdo'i ngos su 'jim pa la bris pa bzhin
du phyag sen gyis ma Ni bri bar mdzad pa'i rjes shin tu gsal ba deng sang thams cad kyis mig gis mngon sum du mjal du yod pa de yin la/ de rjes thams cad kyis 'di lta bu'i
rdzu 'phrul bstan pa ngo mtshar che zhes rje nyid la gsol ba na/ nga la de lta bu nus pa'i stobs dang rdzu 'phrul ci'ang med ces gsungs shing yon tan thams cad sba bar
mdzad par snang na'ang skye bo thams cad la mngon sum tshad mas grub pa yin no/ /gzhan yang sde gzhung dang / go 'jo sogs nas gdan 'dren zhu mi 'byor yang de dag tu ma phebs
par gtso bor sde dge lhun grub steng gi phan bde kun khyab gling gi bla brang rang du bzhugs/ sga stod du phebs skabs ma gtogs lo re bzhin dgon de'i drug cu dang / 'du
ba chen mo zhes

pa ngor lugs dkyil 'khor bdun gyi sgrub mchod tshogs pa'i dbu bzhugs su rtag par phebs/ rgyun tu chos rgyal chen po sku mched rnams kyi thugs bzhed ltar gyi bka' chos rnams
'bul ba dang / sku'i 'ga' rkyen zhi zhing legs tshogs gong 'phel du 'gyur ba'i sku rim gyi rigs sgrub pa dang / dad pa can gzhan dag gis kyang gsol ba btab pa'i ngor gsang
sngags rdo rje theg pa'i bya ba dang / spyod pa dang / rnal 'byor dang / rnal 'byor chen po bla na med pa'i rgyud sde rnams dang rjes su 'brel ba'i dbang bskur ba dang
/ rjes su gnang ba dang / byin gyis brlab pa dang / zab khrid dang / lung 'bogs pa la sogs pa zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor te gdul bya
thams cad rnam par grol ba'i skal ba dang ldan par mdzad pa yin no/ /de dag gi skabs gseng rnams su 'jigs byed kyi sku mtshams zla gcig lhag tsam dang / brag rdzong ma'i
sku mtshams zla ba gcig tsam dang / tshe sgrub zla shas bcas bzhugs pa dang / yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i snang byed khro shul bla ma rin po che ngag dbang smin grol rgya mtsho'i
drung nas/ rgyal mchog lnga pa rin po che ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i ye shes dag pa'i snang ngor rtsa ba gsum gyi lha tshogs rnams kyis dbang bskur zhing byin
gyis brlabs pa'i zab chos dag snang rgya can nyer lnga'i chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa dang / gter ston 'ja' tshon snying po'i zab gter las byung ba'i dkon mchog spyi 'dus
kyi dbang dang / gter ston rkyang mo grags nas brgyud pa'i rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa lha dgu/ tshe dbang gying lnga gza' gdong dang bcas pa'i dbang bskur ba dang /
mnga' ri gter ston paN chen padma dbang rgyal nas brgyud pa'i bsam pa lhun grub ma'i dbang dang /

/gzhan yang snga 'gyur rdo rje theg pa'i gdams ngag zab mo las nyer mkho'i rigs 'ga' zhig gi lung dang / sgrub brgyud karma kaM tshang nas brgyud pa'i gcod nam mkha' sgo 'byed
kyi dbang dang / dpal sa skya pa'i bstan srung mgon po che chung gnyis su grags pa'i nang tshan zhal rnam 'gyur bcu bdun gyi rjes su gnang ba bcas gsan pa dang / yang
nyams dang rtogs pa'i dbang phyug bla ma dpal ldan phrin las kyi drung nas/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po khro bo bcu gcig gi rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i
phyi khrid rdo rje brag rdzong ma dang / nang gi brag rdzong drag po sngags rgod/ gsang ba'i brag rdzong sems nyid ye shes kyi 'khor lo'i rtsal 'don pa bcas kyi nyams khrid
zab mo yongs su rdzogs pa gsan pa dang / rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan bla ma dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i drung nas bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dpag med lha dgu'i
dbang bskur ba legs par gsan par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang yul phyogs so sor bde skyid rgya cher 'byung ba'i slad du lha bum dang / klu bum dang / sa bdag gi bum pa la sogs
pa tshad dang ldan par bsgrubs te sba ba dang / lo re bzhin dbyar gyi dus char 'bebs pa la sogs pa zhi rgyas dbang drag dang rjes su 'brel ba'i mdzad phrin thams cad ni
re re nas smos kyis mi lang ngo / /'phags rnams dag pa rab 'byams las/ /tha mal snang ba ma mchis mod/ /'gro 'di dad phyir mnal lam du/ /'dren pa mchog dang mjal tshul bstan/
/mgon des tshems kyi 'od dkar gyis/ /phyogs su snang ba rab sbyin cing / /lung bstan bdud rtsi'i char 'bebs pa/ /dag pa'i ri bong 'dzin pa bzhin/ /nam zhig sa yi bdag
po yi/ /'phrin yig rin po che yi sgrom/ /gang gi phrag par

nyer bkod pa'i/ /mdo smad ljongs kyi pho nya slebs/ /de tshe mgon po mchog nyid kyi/ /ye shes me long dwangs pa'i mkhar/ /bod chen 'dren par gshegs bzhed pa'i/ /thugs bskyed
gzugs kyi chu 'dzin bkod/ /de nas bcom ldan dgra bcom gyi/ /'khor gyis yongs su bskor ba ltar/ /dbang po gnas pa'i phyogs kyi sgor/ /nyi mas bzhin du mdzes par gshegs/
/bsam yas yon tan phung po yis/ /gser gyi ta la bzhin mtho ba/ /gang de chos kyi khri 'phang du/ /slar yang mtho ba nyid du bsgrubs/ /gang gi grags pa zla 'od ltar/ /dkar
ba yon tan la btags kyang / /sa la pho nya bzhin rgyu ba/ /skye rgu'i bsod nams lags par khums/ /'phags bod mkhas dang grub pa yi/ /mdzad pa gcig tu bsdus pa ltar/ /mkhyen
brtse nus pa'i phrin las kyis/ /thub bstan srid pa'i rtse mor spel/ /rgyal ba rnams kyang btang snyoms su/ /zhi ba'i ngal 'tsho bstan dus 'dir/ /gcig tu 'gro la phan mdzad
pa'i/ /dper 'os rang nyid las gzhan su/ /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten khams/ /brgya phrag spro dang bsdu nus na/ /rdo yi ngos su phyag mdzub kyis/ /yi ge bkod la mtshar
ci zhig /'on te tshur mthong mgu ba'i slad/ /rdzu 'phrul cha tsam bstan pas kyang / /sngon byon grub brnyes brgyad cu bzhi'i/ /grags pa'ang nyams par byas kyis dogs/ /mkhas
dang grub pa'i rtser son kyang / /gsan sgom ngoms pa med 'di mtshar/ /'on te rgya mtshos chu phran kun/ /sdud la tshim pa nam zhig mthong // //gsum pa dbus gtsang dag
pa'i zhing du bsnyen bkur rgya cher bstabs te rang gnas gdan sa chen por zhabs bkod de bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ spyir bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa yon tan ma lus

pa'i phung po chen por gyur pa 'di ni mkhyen brtse nus gsum gyi yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa la dbang 'byor par ma zad/ rtag par chos bzhin spyod pa kho na las/ 'jig rten
chos brgyad la sogs pa dgos med tshe 'di'i bya ba phra zhing phra ba'ang mi mdzad cing / de'i phyir skye bo rtog dpyod dang ldan pa rnams kyis ji tsam brtags kyang yon tan
du snang ba kho na las/ skyon du mngon pa gcig kyang mthong ba med la/ de la brten nas khams bod kyi ljongs su 'khod pa'i skye bo thams cad kyis kyang nges par 'brel tshad
don dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes byed cing / zang zing gi 'bul ba'ang dbyar gyi chu 'dzin bzhin du 'khrigs par gyur mod/ de dag la mngon par zhen pa
cung zad kyang mi mnga'/ 'on kyang skye bo ngan pa'i spyod tshul ltar gyi rang gi 'khor dang nye 'brel la sogs pas sbyin bdag gi dad rdzas la 'bag chol du longs spyod du
'jug pa dang / rang nyid bzang por bsgrub pa'i slad du dgos med kyi thabs skyong dang / rnyed pas rnyed pa 'tshol ba dang / rab tu byung ba'i yo byad kyis khyim pa rnams
kyi sems 'dzin pa la sogs pa log pa'i 'tsho ba dang / ma dag pa'i sbyin pas rang gzhan thams cad nyes dmigs chen po la sbyor ba la sogs pa'i spyod tshul ngan pa mtha' dag
rgyang ring du dor nas/ dad pa can gyi yo byad rnams chud mi za zhing lag len byed pa thams cad la'ang nyes pa mi 'byung ba'i slad du dam gnyer gyi sgo nas yul mchog tu
gyur pa bla ma dang dkon mchog /bstan pa dang sems can gyi ched du bsngo ba'i tshe phangs pa til 'bru tsam yang mi mnga' bar/ de kho na'i ched du lhug par gtong bar mdzad
pa yin te/ de'ang sngar khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi zhal snga nas/

gsar du bzo ba las kyang rnying pa la nyams gso byed pa nyid legs zhes bka' stsal pa thugs la bzhag ste/ sngon bod du bzhugs pa'i dus su'ang sku gsung thugs kyi rten rnying
pa rnams la nyams gso kho na gtso bor mdzad cing / de rjes mdo khams su phebs nas kyang e wa~M bla brang gzhung gi gzim chung g.yabs chen sogs kyi nyams gso'i zhal 'debs
su rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcus gtso byas pa'i yo byad 'ga' zhig bskur bar mdzad pa dang / gling mgo zi dgon du khra leb chos rje rim bzhugs kyi sgar khang rnying pas
g.yos kyis zhig par gyur pa'ang gsar du bzo bar mdzad pa dang / sga stod phyogs kyi chos grwa chen po skye rgu don grub gling pas 'du khang steng du gser zangs kyi rgya
phibs gsar bzhengs byed pa'i tshe'ang rje 'dis zhal 'debs rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu stsal ba sogs de 'dra'i rigs mang zhing / gzhan yang khams phyogs kyi dgon sde
'ga' zhig tu gtan gzhag che chung ci rigs pa stsal ba dang / gsar bzos kyi rigs kyang gser zangs las grub pa'i sku 'dra che chung 'ga' zhig dang / bris thang kha shas dang
/ gsung rten dang / thugs rten kyang ci rigs par bzhengs pa dang / snga phyir mchod pa'i yo byad gsar bzos mdzad pa'ang shin tu mang bar yod la/ dkon mchog gi mchod pa
dang dge 'dun gyi bsnyen bkur yang sngon khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyis spos dang mar me la sogs pa 'di dge ba rjes med lta bu yin pas shin tu legs
zhes gsungs pa la brten nas/ de phyin chad khams bod thams cad du rje rang gi bzhugs gnas gzim chung kun tu mar me nyin mtshan khor yug tu skad cig kyang rgyun ma chad par
mdzad pa dang / khams bod kyi rten gsum khyad par

can rnams mjal ba'i tshe'ang snga phyir mchod 'bul rgya che bar mdzad pa dang / zla ba byung ngo cog gi nya stong tshes brgyad phal che bar yang mchod 'bul zab pa dang bcas
te dge slong 'ga' zhig gis bla ma mchod pa sogs gsung ba dang / khyad par khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid zhi bar gshegs pa'i dus chen cho 'phrul zla ba'i
tshes nyi shu'i nang du nyin lnga drug re la brgya mchod dang bcas te rje rang dang dge slong bzang gras kha shas kyis bla ma mchod pa sogs gsung ba dang / skabs skabs
su dge slong mang rab kyis rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro cog bklag pa dang / sde dge lhun grub steng du lo re bzhin hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i dmar phyogs kyi rdzogs pa gsum pa'i
nyin drug 'du'i dbu bzhugs su yin gyis dgon de'i 'dus tshogs su tshe chog dang / mgon khang khag rnams su skong ba dang / chos sgrogs pa mang pos gsung rab bklag pa dang
/ der 'dus pa'i gsang sngags rnying ma'i bla ma dge slong sngags pa bcas la'ang phyag 'gyed dang rnam gzhag sogs gtong ba'i rgyun mchis pa rnams kyang ma chad par yar ldan
du mdzad pa sogs mdor na dus rtag tu rnam dkar gyi phyogs su gtong ba'i sgo 'phar dbye bzhin pa dang / khyad par sbyin bdag gi dad rdzas mtha' dag chud zos su ma song
bar dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du bsnyen bkur rgya cher stob pa dang / rje rang nyid kyang dus rtag tu tshe 'dir snang gi rnam g.yeng dang 'du 'dzi la gtan nas mi dges shing
/ dben pa kho nar thugs dam la gzhol ba la thugs 'dun rtse gcig tu mdzad pa'i stobs kyis lo snga ma me rta dang / me lug rnams su sde dge chos rgyal chen por bod du 'byon
chog pa'i dgongs khrol yang yang zhu bar mdzad na'ang de

bzhin dgongs pa khrol ba zhig ma byung zhing / slar yang nan tan gyis dgongs zhu mdzad par brten rim gyis sa sprel lor bod du 'byon chog pa'i dgongs khrol byung bar brten/
de skor gyi nyer bsdogs rnams kyang rim gyis brtsams pa dang / don du gnyer ba so sos ji ltar gsol ba btab pa bzhin du nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i khrid dang / kye rdo rje rgyu
lam gyi dbang la sogs pa zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo'ang ci rigs par bskor te re ba'i shing rta yongs su 'gengs par mdzad pa dang / lhun grub steng gi gtsug
lag khang du der bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun gang yod kyis bla ma mchod pa dang / tshe chog nyin kha shas tshogs te/ de dag la'ang bsnyen bkur dang gral 'gyed sogs zab par
mdzad pa dang chabs cig gtsug lag khang der gos chen phul du son pa las grub pa'i bla bre dang / gos yug gi 'phan la sogs pa sbyor 'jags stsal ba dang / phan gling bla brang
rang du'ang chos rgyal dge ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa'i bdag cag gi ston pa thub pa'i dbang po'i skyes rabs dpag bsam 'khri shing las byung ba ltar bris pa'i zhal thang
gras 'grig nyi shu rtsa gcig gong gsham zhal khebs sogs phun sum tshogs pa dang / gser zangs las grub pa'i rgyal ba tshe mtha' yas pa'i sku brnyan mi tshad tsam gcig dang
/ gser zangs las grub pa'i spyan ras gzigs khru gang tsam dang / de bas chung tsam gyi yum chen mo'i gser sku sogs gsar sbyor mang du mdzad pa dang / gzhan chos srung rnams
la skong phrin dang yul lhar bsang mchod la sogs pa skabs su bab pa'i rim gro'i rigs rnams bsgrub pa dang / chos rgyal chen po sku mched rnams kyis dbu byas pa'i sbyi
bdag dad pa can thams cad nas kyang phebs brdzong dang 'bul

ba'i rigs rgyu dpangs mi dman par phul ba dang / phar yang de dag la skabs su bab pa'i chos dang zang zing gis yid kyi dbang po yongs su tshim par mdzad cing / 'phral yun gyi
legs tshogs gong 'phel du 'gyur bar mdzad de/ dgung grangs drug cur phebs pa legs sbyar gyi skad du kI la ka zhes pa phur bu ste rgya rtsis pas sa pho spre'u'i lo'i snron
gyi zla ba'i dmar phyogs kyi gral tshes nyer dgu'i nyin nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di nyid dang / kun gzigs 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po dang
bcas ston 'khor rnams dang / sde dge chos rgyal mchog gi phebs skyel gyi tshogs mtha' yas pa rnams dang / khyad par e wa~M rang du ma phebs bar gyi zhabs 'br-ing bar 'ju
tsha bsod nams stobs rgyal dpon 'khor rnams gtong gnang mdzad pa bzhin/ de rnams dang bcas te dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi rgyal khab chen po nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur
te/ lam bar du 'khod pa'i 'gro ba 'ga' zhig la'ang chos kyi bdud rtsi ci rigs pa stsol bzhin pa'i sgo nas rim gyis shin tu bgrod par dka' ba'i chu bo dang / la lung mang
po brgal te gro bzhin zla ba'i shar phyogs kyi rgyal ba gnyis par bkra shis dbu ma thang du gcung mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang po dpon 'khor gyi chibs bsu dang mjal
'dzom gnang nas sku mched lhan cig tu thog mar byang rwa sgreng gi chos grwa chen por phebs/ der bzhugs pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi rten khyad par du 'phags pa rnams kyi drung

sogs pa'i tshan grangs 'ga' zhig dang / ljon ja 'khor gcig /rta drel

gnyis la sogs pa'i 'bul ba dang / gzhan yang skabs su bab pa'i ja gsar dang / gnang sbyin la sogs pa gang la gang 'os mdzad de dpal stag lung gi dgon par phebs/ stag lung bla
ma rin po cher ljon ja 'khor gcig dang / rta gcig gi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas/ dgon de'i rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul dang / 'dus tshogs su mang jas bsnyen bkur
ba bcas bsgrubs/ de nas rim gyis brag yer pa la sogs pa'i lam bar gyi gnas chen rnams su'ang mchod 'bul rgyas par mdzad de/ khrums kyis nya ba'i hor zla brgyad pa'i dkar
phyogs kyi dga' ba gnyis pa'i nyin chos tshigs kyis phye ba'i yul dbus su gyur pa bsil ldan ljongs kyi lte ba lha ldan du phebs/ de skabs lha ldan du 'brum 'phros thor
tsam yod pa la brten bag sang gi tshul du dbus gtsang kun bde gling du zhag bdun tsam bzhugs te/ skabs su bab pa na pho brang chen po po ta lar 'phags mchog lag na padmo'i
rnam 'phrul rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa mkhas grub rgya mtsho'i gser zhal rin po che mjal ba dang lhan cig /gsol ja bzhes 'bras dang / maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/
dar ras ling la sogs pa'i tshan grangs dang dngos chas rigs rgya che ba dang / ma hA tsi na'i yul gyi bzang ja 'khor drug brgya dang / dngul Tam srang brgya/ rta drel bzhi
la sogs pa phul ba dang / de nas lha ldan rang gi bzhugs mtsher du phebs nas gangs ljongs bsod nams kyi 'gron du khugs pa'i srid skyong rwa sgreng a chi thu ho thog thu

/ dar

ras gos chen la sogs pa'i tshan grangs dang dngos chas kyi rigs mang po/ bzang ja 'khor drug bzhi bcu/ rin chen gnyis pa Tam srang lnga bcu/ rta drel gnyis bcas phul bar/ phyir
