/ kun bde gling gi yongs 'dzin rin po che'i mdun bzang ja 'khor drug gcig dang / chibs pa gcig gi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas phul ba dang / gzhan yang bka' shag dang
/ spyi khyab mkhan po dang / rtse shod kyi gsol gzim mgron gnyer rnams dang / lha sa bla brang gi phyag mdzod pa dang / gnyer tshang pa dang / rtse'i phyag mdzod pa dang
/ gnyer tshang pa dang / mi dpon dang / rtswa gnyer dang / shing gnyen sogs la'ang so so'i go bab dang 'dris zab che chung dang bstun pa'i ja sar gyi sa bcad re dang
/ khyad par du'ang mtshan gyi utpal rna ba'i rgyan du lan cig son pa tsam gyis kyang 'khor ba dang ngan song gi g.yang sa las skyob par nus pa'i bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i

kyi 'dus tshogs rin po cher mang ja'i bsnyen bkur zhu

ba'i dod du bzang ja 'khor drug sum cu so lnga lha sa bla brang gi phyag mdzod par phul ba dang / phyag dang skor ba la sogs pa'ang ci rigs par mdzad de mdor na bsod nams kyi

dngul Tam re bcas re mos kyi tshul du phul ba dang / gtsug lag khang du gos chen mdzod jus mtshal kha'i 'phan gnyis dang / gos chen rgyan bzhi sngo khra'i bla bre shin tu
legs pa dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang brgya dang sum bcu las grub pa'i dngus ltir cha bcas gsar sbyor mdzad pa dang / de lta bu'i dge tshogs rnams bar ma dor chud mi 'dza'
ba'i slad du e wa~M pa'i chos kyi rgyal srid chen por gsar du mnga' gsol ba'i phan khang mkhan rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i blo

gros kyi mdun du ljags bsngo rin po ches rjes 'dzin zhu mtshon gyi 'bul ba shin tu zab pa dang / spyir bla brang gzhung gi 'bul ba khang sar mkhan rnying rin po cher phul zin
rung / phan khang mkhan gsar rin po che'i drung du'ang sa bcad stong min tsam du bzang ja 'khor drug bzhi dang / rgya rol che legs la sogs pa'i dngos po 'ga' zhig kyang
'bul bar mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang zhwa lu ri phug tu rtsod pa'i dus kyi kun mkhyen bu ston gnyis pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong dpal bzang po'i drung
du'ang dngos rdzas 'ga' zhig phul ba dang / zhwa lu chos sde dang / snar thang / srad rgyud pa/ srad dgon khra sogs nye skor gyi dgon khag rnams su'ang mang ja'i bsnyen
bkur stsal ba sogs mdor na rmad du byung ba'i mchod pa'i sprin phung 'dzad pa med par spros pa'i tshul 'di lta bu ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang
po'i rnam par thar pa kho na dang mtshungs par 'gyur gyi/ de las gzhan pa'i so so skye bo gtong phod che bar rlom pa mang po phyogs gcig tu bsdoms kyang gang gi cha shas
re yang bskrun tu yod pa'i re ba ni padma'i rtsa ba ltar shin tu phra ba'o zhes dge ba'i phyogs kyi zla 'od gzhon nus yid kyi ku mu dA yongs su kha phyes pa'i skyes bu gzu
bor gnas pa rnams kyis mgrin gcig tu snyan ngag dam pa'i glu bzhin du len par byed do/ /de nas bzung ste e wa~M rang du bzhugs nas gtso bor thugs dam kho na la gzhol bar
mdzad cing / bka' chos kyi rim pa'ang dgur grangs re gsum du phebs pa lcags mo phag gi lor sde dge bla chen byams pa kun dga' 'jam dpal phan bde'i snying po dpon 'khor
rnams e wa~M du phebs te/ des gsol ba btab pa'i ngor grub chen bi rU pa'i thugs bcud gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa

skya pa rnams kyi thugs dam gyi snying po gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras tshogs bshad kyi smin grol cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa lan cig stsal ba dang / yang bdag gis gsol ba
btab pa'i ngor gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras tshogs bshad kyi smin grol cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa lan cig bka' drin chen po'i sgo nas stsal bas mtshon snga phyir chos
kyi bdud rtsi rigs par stsal ba dang / gzhan yang mang du thos pa la ngoms pa med pa'i bdag nyid chen po 'dis ni gcen mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan
'dzin gyi drung nas dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs dang / Dombi lugs dang / mtsho skyes lugs dang / nag po lugs kyi sku gsung thugs snying po kye rdo rje rnams kyi dkyil
'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / dpal gshin rje'i gshed dmar po lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas shin tu spros pa med pa'i khrid yongs su
rdzogs pa dang / bya rgyud gshegs rigs kyi yum du gtogs pa srung ba lha lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa'i
sngags phyogs kyi skor bka' 'bum pusta ka bzhi dang / tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos bsgrigs pa'i 'dod khams dbang phyug dud sol ma'i dpe bum rnams kyi lung bcas gsan pa
dang / bcu phrag rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta chen po mdo sngags bstan pa'i srog shing 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i drung nas/ bya ba'i rgyud de bzhin gshegs
pa'i rigs kyi nang tshan gtsug tor dri ma med pa lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / rgyal bas lung gis bsngags pa'i ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i bka' 'bum
pusta

ka bzhi dang / zhu chen ma hA paNDi ta tshul khrims rin chen gyi bka' 'bum spyir pusta ka bcu gcig bzhugs kyang / ljangs lung gi rgyun bzhugs pa pusta ka dgu dang bcas pa rnams
kyi lung gsan pa dang / yang gnas lnga rig pa'i mkhas pa chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub pa'i drung nas lce sgom shes rab rdo rjes mdzad pa'i dpe chos
rin chen spungs pa dang / des mdzad pa'i man ngag rin chen spungs pa dang / de la mkho ba'i gtam rgyud rin chen phreng mdzes 'gro mgon dpal ldan ye shes kyis mdzad pa rnams
dang / gangs ljongs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa'i bka' 'bum pusta ka bco lnga dang / der ma 'dus pa dpal brtse ba chen pos mdzad pa'i lam 'bras sras don
ma dang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras glegs bam bcas kyi lung rnams gsan par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang lcags khyi lor thar
rtse rang gi lha khang khag rnams su kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa lan gnyis dang / dgung grangs re drug tu son pa shing pho stag gi lor e wa~M bla brang gzhung
du kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas shin tu rgyas pa lan cig dang / thar rtse rang du rab gnas rgyas pa lan cig bcas stsal te/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten thams cad ye shes
pa'i ngo bor byin gyis brlabs te 'khor ba ji srid gnas pa de srid du skye 'gro'i bsod nams kyi zhing du brtan par bzhugs su gsol lo/ /gzhan yang sku'i 'phrod bzhes kyi
chu tshan du snga phyir tshar kha shas phebs pa dang / de'i nang tshan bzhad glang mar chu tshan du phebs pa'i skabs gangs can chos sde dang / khro phu dang / bo dong e
dang / bya gshong dang / bzhad thub bstan yangs can rnams su mang ja

gral 'gyed dang bcas pa dang / bzhad bkra shis dge 'phel dang / dngul chu chos rdzong dang / gru 'dzin la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang phyogs der btsun ma'i dgon pa mang du mchis
pa de thams cad la'ang mang ja gnyis gsum re ma chad par stsal te dge tshogs gong 'phel du mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang snga phyir bdud rtsi ril bu chig sgrub lan kha shas
mdzad pa dang / khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid gtso bor bzhugs pa'i zhal thang sgros gtsang shin tu che ba zhig bzhengs te rab tu gnas pa'i sgo nas
byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar mdzad cing / e wa~M pa'i gtsug lag khang du sbyor 'jags stsal ba dang lhan cig dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor mang ja gral 'gyed dang bcas pa'i
bsnyen bkur zab par mdzad pa dang / brang ti paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i 'dul ba'i las chog gi yig cha der tshig sbyor bde min phran bu yod pa dang / khyad par yig cha de
spar du ma 'khod pa'i skyon gyis phyis su yig nor gyi skyon mang ba dang / lung rgyun kyang mi bzhugs par brten/ mkhas pa'i dbang po 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub
par rab byung gi gzhi'i cho ga yon tan rin po che'i 'byung gnas su grags pa de thog mar rtsoms par bskul zhing / slad nas kyang yig cha de nyid spar du spel ba sogs mdor
na rnam par dkar ba'i phrin las kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad pas re re nas smos kyis mi lang ba yin no/ /snying pos dben pa'i nor rdzas rnams/ /'dod dang ldan la sdug bsngal
rgyu/ /'di yi ngor ni bla med kyi/ /byang chub thob pa'i rgyu ru mchis/ /gang la dad pa'i lag pa yis/ /rang rang bdog pa'i me tog kun/ /btus nas gus pas gtor ba rnams/
/bsod nams phung por bsgyur ba'i slad/ /sde bzhi dge bcu'i rgyal khab kyi/ /mi bdag tshangs pa'i spun zla der/ /

don mthun tshig gis skabs phyes nas/ /dbus gtsang ljongs su gshegs par brtsams/ /de tshe dad pa'i rtsa brtan zhing / /gtong ba'i yal 'dab ring bskyod pa'i/ /dpag bsam shing
'dra'i skye bo yis/ /slar yang mchod cing smon lam btab/ /de nas bye ru'i 'khri shing tshogs/ /rlung gis dal bur bskyod pa'am/ /'on te thub dbang dgra bcom pa'i/ /'khor
gyis bskor bzhin mdzes par gshegs/ /chos kyi snang bar rab sbyin pa'i/ /nyin mo'i dpal de gzhan gshegs pas/ /phyogs der mun pas bkab pa bzhin/ /blang dor mig ni zum par gyur/
/rim gyis khyod zhabs padma dkar/ /dbus gtsang ljongs su nyer bkod pas/ /phyogs de'i dga' ston rab 'phel ba/ /nyi mas phyes pa'i padmo bzhin/ /de na mchod dang sbyin
pa yi/ /sngon med gter gyi kha phyes pas/ /sngon byon gtong phod can rnams kyi/ /grags pa'ang zil gyis gnon pa bzhin/ /e ma mchod pa'i sprin spro ba'i/ /kun tu bzang de
'di min nam/ /gzhan du mi zad gtong ba'i sgo/ /cig car dbye 'di ga la 'ong / /zab rgyas chos kyis 'gro ba rnams/ /smin grol lam la rab bkod pas/ /snyigs ma lnga bdo'i grags
pa yang / /skyengs te sa la thim mam snyam/ /gzod nas thams cad mkhyen pa yi/ /nor bu'i gling du bgrod zin kyang / /da dung thos bsam sgom pa'i grur/ /'jug 'di gzhan la
slob phyir nges/ /sku gsung thugs kyi rten rnams kyang / /ye shes sems dpar byin brlabs pas/ /longs sku'i zhing dang ljongs 'di zhes/ /'byed la tshangs pa'ang ngal gyis
dogs/ /mdor na rnam dkar phrin las kyi/ /gdugs dkar nyin bzhin bsgreng ba yis/ /grags pa'i ri mo rnam bkra ba/ /phyogs kyi gdong la 'bri ba

bzhin// //spyi don bzhi pa gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang pa chen pos chen por 'os pa'i mtshan dang yo byad kyis chen po'i go sar mnga' gsol nas rnam par dkar ba'i phrin las
ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ zhib par gcen mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar/ spyir thar rtse'i bla ma rim byon thams
cad kyis rgyal bstan spyi dang bye brag rnams dang / khyad par gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang pa bcas su rnam kun phan thogs gang che byung bar ma zad/ lo snga ma shing yos
dang me 'brug gnyis su gor bod dmag 'khrugs rgya chen byung ba'i dus 'byor ldan rnams la dmag phogs kyi yod 'don 'gel skabs kyang / thar rtse nas dngos 'bul phon cher
byung ba bcas kyi gzigs bzos su/ thar rtse rang gi bla rabs rim can la sha 'dzin ni thig thig gu chi mkhan po zhes pa'i cho lo dang / tham kha che chung sogs chen por 'os
pa'i yo byad mang po stsal ba ltar/ spyir don dam pa'i dbang du byas na bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'di dag bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol nas srid pa dang
zhi ba'i mtha' la mi gnas pa'i zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang chen po'i go 'phang dam pa brnyes zin pas tshe 'di snang gi go sa dang / thob thang sogs la ltos dgos pa min na'ang
/ tha snyad kun rdzob tu 'jig rten tshu rol mthong ba rnams kyi snang tshul dang bstun te/ gcen mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dgung grangs gya gnyis su phebs shing / rje 'di
dgung grangs re dgur son pa me mo sbrul gyi lo'i sa ga zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes lnga'i nyin/ dge slong 'ga' zhig gis sku tshe brtan bzhugs cho ga 'bul ba dang
chabs cig /bshad ma thag pa'i chen por 'os pa'i mtshan dang / yo byad rnams dang / gzhan yang legs 'bul

gyi tshogs dang bcas pa'i sgo nas bod gangs can gyi mkhan po che gras su mnga' gsol bar gyur to/ /de nas bzung ste dgung grangs don drug pa shing byi lo'i bar gtso bor thugs
dam kho na la gzhol bar mdzad cing / bka' chos kyang rjes gnang gi skor 'ga' zhig dang / ljags lung gi skor kha yar las rgya che rigs ma stsal/ snga phyir sku'i 'phrod
bzhes kyi chu tshan du tshar gnyis tsam phebs shing / de'i nang tshan lcags bya lor rta nag 'bur chu tshan du phebs skabs rta nag thub bstan dang / 'gos lo tsA ba chen po'i
sgrub gnas zhal gzigs phug tu grags pa sogs de skor gyi gnas chen dang dgon khag rnams su mchod 'bul dang / mang ja gral 'gyed la sogs pa'i bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs
pa stsal ba dang / khyad par nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po gcen mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa de nyid lo snga ma lcags bya hor zla bzhi pa'i mjug nas bzung sku
khams shin tu bsnyel ba'i tshul bzhes rung / gsol sman gyi 'phrod bzhes dang / zhabs brtan gyi rigs rgya gang che mdzad par brten rim gyis sku khams cung zad dwang ba'i
tshul bstan par gyur na'ang / slar yang bstan 'gro'i bsod nams kyis ma 'chun par chu khyi hor zla gsum pa snga ma'i tshes bcu bdun gyi nyi dros tsam la gzugs sku'i bkod pa
chos kyi dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul bstan pas shin tu skal ba dman pa'i dus ngan de lta bu byung bar brten/ de skor gyi dgongs rdzogs rnams kyang gong du mkhan chen rdo
rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar shin tu dpyis phyin par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang snga phyir khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi dus
mchod cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes nyi shu nas brtsams te nyin lnga drug re la nyin re bzhin mchod pa'i phreng ba brgya

phrag mang po dang bcas te/ rje rang nyid sku 'khor gyi tshogs 'ga' zhig dang bcas pas bla ma mchod pa lo re bzhin ma chags par mdzad pa dang / skabs skabs su yid dam gyi lha
'ga' zhig sgrub mchod gsung ba dang / thar rtse rang du'ang lo re bzhin rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che gsung sgrogs ma chad par stsal ba dang / lha ldan gyi jo shAka
rin po che rnam pa gnyis dang / bal yul mchod rten bcas su snga phyir mchod 'bul yang yang bskur bar mdzad pa dang / rje 'di sku mched rnams nas e wa~M pa'i 'dus tshogs
kyi tshogs khro spus ldan gcig gsar bzos mdzad de sbyor 'jags stsal ba dang lhan cig 'dus tshogs su mang ja gral 'gyed dang bcas pa'i bsnyen bkur gya nom pa stsal ba sogs
zhib par gcen mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar dang / khyad par sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa zhes pa'i ming gi gdags gzhi ni lung dang
rtogs pas bsdus pa'i dam pa'i chos kho na yin cing / de nyid yun ring du gnas par byed pa'i thabs kyang dam pa'i chos bshad pa dang / sgrub pa kho na la ltos dgos pa'i phyir
na/ gong du gsal ba ltar rje rang gis kyang gsan bsam sgom gsum ngal med du mdzad pa dang / gdul bya gzhan rnams la'ang zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo ci
rigs par bskor ba dang / der ma zad 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa gong nas gong 'phel du 'gyur ba'i slad du/ rje 'di sku mched rnams nas rtsod
pa'i dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po nyid mdo khams nas e wa~M du spyan 'dren par mdzad pa dang / de'i gsung las skyes pa'i gnas
lnga rig pa'i mkhas pa chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub pa nyid kyi phrin las kyang

gong nas gong 'phel du 'gyur ba mdzad pa dang / mkhas pa chen po de gnyis kyang 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che ni de bzhin gshegs pa
bzhugs pa'i dus la 'gran pa bzhin du rgyas par mdzad pa sogs zhib par gong du gcen mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i rnam thar du gsal ba ltar yin cing / rgyu mtshan de'i
phyir na bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di dag e wa~M pa'i bstan pa rin po che la dngos dang brgyud pa'i sgo nas dka' drin
shin tu che ba yin no/ /chen por 'os pa'i yo byad kyis/ /chen po'i go sar gzengs bstod kyang / /chen po gdod nas brnyes zin pas/ /chen po chung ngus ci zhig bya/ /'on te
tshur mthong 'gro 'di yi/ /yi rang padmo 'dzum pa'i slad/ /mngon mtho'i khri la zhabs bkod pas/ /phan bde'i dga' ston nyin bzhin spel/ /skyabs kun 'dus pa'i bdag nyid cher/
/sri zhu lan cig bgyis pa yang / /'dod rgu ster ba'i nor bu bzhin/ /yang srid mang por rnyed par dka'/ /gang gi rnam dkar phrin las kyis/ /'gro la phan bde rab stsol
zhing / /de kun yid kyi brtan pa yang / /lhag ma med par khyod kyis 'phrogs/ /thub bstan nub kyi ri bo'i rtser/ /thun mtshams gos dmar 'dzin gyur kyang / /khyod kyi rlabs
chen spyod pa yis/ /slar yang 'char ka'i nyi bzhin mdzad/ /'di na srid pa'i gdung 'phrog cing / /rnam grol bdud rtsi sbyin mkhas pa/ /rdo rje 'chang dngos kun dga'i mtshan/
/zhing khams gzhan du gshegs tshul bstan/ /kyi hud 'gro 'di'i bsod nams kyis/ /'dren pa lan cig rnyed pa de/ /rmi lam gyi ni nor bu bzhin/ /skad cig gcig la mi snang
gyur/ /tshul des mgon med bdag cag gi /snying la mya ngan gyis gdungs

pa/ /dgun dang 'phrad pa'i me tog gam/ /chu dang bral ba'i nya bzhin gyur/ /'on kyang de dang mi gnyis pa'i/ /mgon khyod 'tsho gzhes rab brtan pa/ /'di nyid kho nas bdag cag
rnams/ /yid la ngal 'tsho ci yang thob/ /khyod kyi byang chub spyod mchog gis/ /mgon de'i thugs dgongs rab bskangs pa'i/ /ngo mtshar 'byams su klas pa gang / /tshangs pa'i
blos kyang gzhal nus min// //spyi don lnga pa gsung las skyes pa'i bstan 'dzin gyi slob ma ji tsam byon pa'i tshul ni/ bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'dis ni tshe
'di snang gi 'jig rten chos brgyad la sogs pa'i rtog pa mtha' dag rgyang ring du dor nas/ bstan 'gro'i don kho na la dgongs te ji skad du/ blo chen rnams la zab rgya che/
/blo chung gzung bde go sla ba/ /phyi nas tshig don 'brel chags pas/ /don phra 'gal 'brel bcad cing bshad/ /ces pa ltar gdul bya rang rang gi blo dang 'tsham par chos
kyi bdud rtsi ji ltar stsal ba'i tshul yang / gong du bshad pa ltar e wa~M pa'i mkhan sa zhal 'dzin gnang ba'i skabs gsung ngag rin po che tshogs bshad tshar bdun dang /
de rjes tshar gnyis te bsdoms lam 'bras tshar dgu'i gtsos pa'i rje rang gis gsan pa'i chos phal che ba ngal dub la ma gzigs par stsal ba la brtan nas gsung las skyes pa'i
zhal slob kyi rim pa'ang stod mnga' ris/ bar dbus gtsang / smad mdo khams rnams na mtha' yas par bzhugs shing / de rnams re re nas bgrang bar ga la nus/ mdo tsam smos na/
nyi zla ltar grags pa'i mkhas pa chen po 'dzam gling mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan gnyis te/ ris su med pa'i grub mtha' yongs kyi bstan pa'i srog shing gcig pur gyur pa bcu
phrag rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta chen po nges pa don gyi 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen

brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas dang / rab 'byams sde snod rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son zhing 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas kun mkhyen e wa~M pa chen pa'i bstan pa nyin
mo ltar mdzad pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub bam/ mtshan gzhan ngag dbang blo gros snying po gzhan la phan pa mtha' yas pa'i 'od zer du grags pa'i zhas snga
nas dang gnyis so/ /zab rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo rgyun chad med par bskor ba'i e wa~M pa'i bstan 'dzin chen po bcu ni/ gsang chen gdams pa rgya mtshos 'gro ba rnams smin grol
la 'god pa phan khang mkhan rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i blo gros pa dang / mkhyen brtse nus pa'i mnga' bdag khang gsar mkhan rin po che ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal
mtshan pa dang / da lta e wa~M pa'i chos kyi khri la zhabs sen rnam par bkod pa'i rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan khang sar mkhan rin po che 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho
pa dang / rje rang gi sku'i dbon po bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag zhabs drung rin po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa
dang / lung rig smra ba'i dbang phyug klu ldings zhab drung rin po che 'jam dbyangs shes rab chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa dang / gsang chen gdams pa'i gter mdzod klu ldings zhabs
drung rin po che byams pa tshul khrims phun tshogs pa dang / mkhas btsun bzang po'i gter gyur phan khang zhabs drung rin po che dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan pa dang
/ bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa khang gsar zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros snying po pa dang / rje rang gi snag dbon thar rtse zhabs drung ngag gi dbang phyug
'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rje pa dang / chos spyan yangs pa gdong tshang zhabs drung rnams so/ /che rgu mang po'i gtsug tu

zhabs sen rnam par bkod pa'i bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu chen po drug ni/ grub mtha' ris med kyi gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa gnas lnga rig pa'i mkhas pa chen po khro shul
bla ma ngag dbang smin grol rgya mtsho pa dang / mkhas dang grub pa'i gtsug rgyan bla ma ngag dbang chos 'byor pa dang / yi dam gyi lha mang po'i bsnyen sgrub pha mthar son
pa grub mchog dpal ldan phrin las pa dang / mkhas dang grub pa'i dbang phyug bla ma dge 'dun rgya mtsho pa dang / snyan brgyud gdams pa'i gter mdzod bla ma ngag dbang
bzang po dang / nyams dang rtogs pa'i dbang phyug bla ma 'jam dbyangs blo gsal rnams so/ /bstan pa stobs kyis 'dzin pa'i chos skyong ba'i rgyal po ni/ mang du thos pa rgya
mtsho'i pha rol tu son zhing 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum dang / stobs kyi sgo nas bstan pa 'dzin pa sde dge chos rgyal chen po tshe dbang rdo rje rig 'dzin nam/ phyis rab tu
byung ba'i mtshan byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan du grags pa dang / de'i lha sras che ba chos rgyal byang chub sems dpa' dam tshig rdo rje tshe ring
rnam rgyal pa dang / lha sras bar pa lung rtogs bstan pa'i snang byed byams pa kun dga' 'jam dpal phan bde'i snying po pa dang / lha sras chung ba lugs zung mkhyen pa'i
spyan ras bkra ba tshe dbang rdo rje dgra 'dul ba ste bzhi dang / gzhan yang gling tshang la sogs pa rgyal rigs su gtogs pa 'ga' zhig dang / khams phyogs kyi mi chen phal
che ba rje 'di'i zhabs la ma btud pa cher med pa yin no/ /mang du thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa'i lung rig smra ba bdun ni/ rab 'byams sde snod rgya mtsho'i pha
rol tu son zhing lung rig smra ba gzhan gyis 'gran par mi nus pa'i mkhas pa chen po rta nag thub bstan gyi mkhan rin po

che seng ge rab rgyas pa dang / lnga rig smra ba'i dbang po zhu slob kun dga' don grub pa dang / mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i nges gsang thugs su chud cing 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum
la dbang bsgyur ba shar bla ma kun dga' dpal ldan pa dang / mdo sngags smra ba'i dbang po klog pa ba sprul sku shes rab rgya mtsho pa dang / rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan
bla ma bstan pa dar rgyas pa dang / mkhas btsun bzang po'i gter gyur bla ma phan bde bzang po pa dang / lung dang rig pa smra ba bla ma 'jam dbyangs yon tan mtha' yas rnams
so/ /dgon sde so so'i mkhan po dang / slob dpon dang / chos rje dang / sprul sku'i rigs ni/ rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan rgyal rtse gur pa mkhan po byang sems sbyin
pa rin chen pa dang / bzhad thub bstan yangs can gyi slob dpon skal bzang rgya mtsho sogs dbus gtsang phyogs kyi mkhan po dang slob dpon 'ga' zhig dang / khams phyogs kyi
sa dgon rnams kyi sprul sku che phra phal che ba dang / sde dge shar nub kyi bla ma rnams dang / khams phyogs kyi sa dgon phal che ba'i dgon dpon dang / slob dpon la sogs
pa shin tu mang po dang / rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan mnga' ri chos rje kun dga' 'jam dbyangs sogs bla ma chos rje'i rigs shin tu mang po dang / gzhan yang rgyud sde'i
gnad shes pa/ bskyed rim gyi gsal snang thob pa/ rig sngags kyi bden tshig grub pa sogs shin tu mang bar bzhugs mod/ de thams cad la bdag dad cing gus par gyur na'ang
re re nas bgrang bar ga la nus mdor bsdu ba'i dbang du byas na/ rje 'di e wa~M pa'i chos kyi khri la lo bdun bzhugs pa'i skabs/ lo re bzhin sdom pa gsum char gyi bka' drin
rdzogs par nos pa'i slob ma mang dus nyis brgya lhag tsam dang / shin tu nyung ba'i dus kyang phyed nyis brgya skor 'ong bar snang bas/ de ltar na

sdom pa gsum char gyi bka' drin rdzogs par nos pa'i zhal slob ni stong dang sum brgya skor yod par mngon la/ bka' chos kyi 'brel pa tsam thob pa'i slob ma ni bgrang ba las
'das pa yin no/ /gang gi mkhyen brtse nus pa yi/ /yon tan 'dab stong bzhad pa 'dis/ /yid kyi brtan pa ma 'phrogs pa'i/ /'di na thar 'dod skye bo su/ /de slad khyod zhabs
rin chen phreng / /spyi bo'i rgyun du gus len pa'i/ /skal bzang rnams kyis gang gi gsung / /longs spyod bung bas sbrang rtsi bzhin/ /ji ltar mkha' la rgyu skar dang / /dbyar
gyis bskyed pa'i rtswa ljang bzhin/ /khyod gsung bdud rtsis lus rgyas pa'i/ /mkhas dang grub pa bsam mi khyab/ /rgyas par byas so sa mos tshal/ /ri bong 'dzin pa'i 'od
kyis te/ /lung dang rtogs pa'i bstan pa yang / /slob tshogs nying slob bcas pas so/ /de slad dngos dang brgyud pa yi/ /snyigs dus bstan pa spel ba'i drin/ /gal te gzugs
can nyid gyur na/ /'jig rten 'di yang snod du chung // //spyi don drug pa sdom pa gsum la gces spras su mdzad cing nyams su bzhes pa la brten nas nyams rtogs ji ltar 'khrungs
pa'i tshul bye brag tu bshad pa ni/ snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'dzam gling byang phyogs kyi thub dbang gnyis pa lta bur gyur pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rnam thar gsol 'debs las/ tshul khrims phung por nyes pa'i skyon dang bral/ /byang chub sems gnyis bdud rtsis thugs rgyud gtams/
/gsang chen rim gnyis zab mo'i rnal 'byor dang / /nam yang 'bral ba med der gsol ba 'debs/ /zab rgyas gdams pa'i nges gsang khong chud cing / /smin grol 'chad spel phyag

bzhes rnam par dag /rang gis ji ltar gzigs bzhin 'doms mdzad phyir/ /mkhas rnams dgyes pa skyed der gsol ba 'debs/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang rje btsun e wa~M pa'i/ /bshad dang
sgrub pa'i dpal la dbang 'byor bzhin/ /ris med thub pa'i bstan dang de 'dzin la/ /dag pa'i snang ba rgyas der gsol ba 'debs/ /bla ma lhag pa'i lha yis rjes bzung zhing /
/spangs dang rtogs pa'i yon tan mtha' klas kyang / /khengs dang dregs pa mtha' dag ring btang ba'i/ /rnam thar mtshungs pa med der gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ spyir
bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa gangs ri'i khrod kyi sdom brtson sde snod 'dzin pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa 'dis ni/ sde snod gsum gyi nyams su blang
bya bslab pa rin po che rnams la nyams bzhes snying por mdzad pa la brten nas/ spangs pa dang rtogs pa'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa thugs rgyud la 'khrungs par gdon
mi za na'ang / de dag ni sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis kyang brjod par dka' na/ bdag lta bu'i byis pa so so skye bo rnams kyis cha shas tsam
yang shes par ga la nus/ 'on kyang bdag cag tha mal pa rnams kyi ngor ji ltar snang ba'i tshul cha shas tsam bsnyad na/ sku tshe snga ma rnams su legs byas la goms pa brtas
pa'i shugs kyis sku tshe 'dir yang dang po nas rang bzhin gyis zhi zhing dul la bag dang ldan pa'i sgo nas kha na ma tho ba ci'ang mi mdzad cing / de la brten nas khu
bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos kyang byis pa 'di shin tu btsun pa zhig 'dug ces yang yang bka' stsal pa zhig yin na/ sku nar son zhing legs par gsungs pa'i dam pa'i
chos 'dul

ba la rab tu byung ba dang / bsnyen par rdzogs pa mdzad tshun chad de dag gi bslab bya dang 'gal ba lta ga la zhig ste/ dgag sgrub gnang gsum gyi bslab pa'i gzhi mtha' dag
tshul 'chos tsam ma yin par rang gi sku srog las kyang gces par bzung ste blang dor tshul bzhin du mdzad pa la brten nas/ nyes pa phra zhing phra bas kyang ma reg pa yin
te/ tha na sku'i bzhugs tshul dang / na bza' bzhes tshul tshun chad nas mi legs par cung zad kyang mi mnga'/ spyod lam thams cad mdzes shing brjid chags pa dang / gang du
bzhugs pa'i sa phyogs mtha' dag gtsang zhing yid du 'ong ba dang / sku lus las tshul khrims kyi dri bzang khyad par can 'thul ba sogs thams cad la mngon sum du snang ba
'di yin la/ rgyu mtshan de'i phyir na brtan mkhas kyi yon tan gnyis dang ldan pa'i bdag nyid chen po 'di ni sngon gyi 'phags pa dgra bcom pa rnams dang tshul mtshungs par
bzhugs pa yin no/ /der ma zad sku na chung ngu'i dus nas theg chen gyi rigs sad de/ bdag pas gzhan gces kyi snying rje chen po bcos ma ma yin pa thugs rgyud la 'khrungs
shing / de'i stobs kyis gzhan la phan gang thogs mdzad pa las/ gnod par 'gyur ba'i las til 'bru tsam yang mi mdzad la/ khyad par byang chub sems dpa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom
pa gsan phyin chad byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod rnams nas ji ltar bshad pa ltar gyi nyes spyod thams cad sdom pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi sgo nas dge ba'i chos
thams cad yongs su sdud pa dang / bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhis sems can thams cad yongs su smin par mdzad pa sogs byang chub sems dpa'i spyod tshul rgya mtsho lta bu la slob
par mdzad cing / khyad par du'ang mgon

med pa dang / skyabs med pa dang / dbul zhing phongs pa dang / nad dang sdug bsngal drag pos gzir ba rnams la lhag par yang mi bzod pa'i snying rje chen pos zas dang gos la
sogs pa lhug par stsol ba dang / 'dir snang gi bya ba la mngon par zhen pa'i yid dri ma can du gyur pa rnams la'ang lhag par brtse ba'i sgo nas de dag chos la zhugs pa'i
thabs 'ba' zhig mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang rang 'dod kyi 'khri ba gtan nas med cing 'jig rten chos brgyad mgo snyoms pa'i stobs kyis gzhan dag gis 'bul ba dang zhabs tog
shin tu che bar byas kyang de la ha cang thugs dges pa'ang med cing / ma byas kyang mi dges pa gtan nas med pa dang / zang zing gi dngos po rnams kyang gong du bshad pa
ltar bla ma dang dkon mchog mchod pa dang dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur ba dang / ngan slong la sbyin pa rnams su phongs pa med par gtong ba las/ rang don du mngon par zhen pa
cung zad kyang mi mnga' ba dang / 'jig rten gyi sde dpon la sogs pa'i chen po su la'ang ngo srung dang / mthun 'jug rigs gtan nas mi mdzad pa dang / khyad par tshe 'di snang
gi bya gzhag rigs la gting nas mi dges shing / zhal nas kyang / sngon nged kyi khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung las/ tshe 'di snang gi bya byed mang po
'dis bla ma la thugs dam mi yong / bu slob rnams la dpe cha mi yong ba'i gzhi yin pas dgos nges can re re tsam las bya byed mang po mi bya zhes yang yang bka' stsal pa
yin cing / don la'ang tshe 'di snang gi dgos med kyi bya byed mang po 'dis rang gzhan thams cad sdug bsngal la sbyor ba'i rgyu kho na las ma 'das pa yin ces gsungs shing
/ rje rang nyid kyis kyang sku gsung thugs

kyi rten bzhengs pa sogs chos mthun gyi mdzad pa dgos nges kho na las/ don med kyi bya byed mang po gtan nas mi mdzad cing / gzhan dag tshe 'di snang gi bya ba la mngon par
zhen pa rnams la'ang shin tu thugs sun pa'i rnam pa kho na mdzad pa dang / g.yo sgyu zol zog gi rigs ni phra zhing phra ba'ang mi mkhyen pa lta bu yin te/ gsung sgros zhig
mdzad pa'i tshe'ang thugs la gang shar de nyid thal byung du bka' stsal pa las 'khyog bshad kyi rigs gtan nas mi mdzad cing / gzhan dag gis kyang ngag nas brjod pa dang
yid la bsam pa gnyis cung zad mi mthun par byung na'ang de 'dra'i g.yo sgyu gsung zhing shin tu thugs khrel bar 'gyur ba dang / skye bo su la'ang zur gyis 'khu ba dang
/ zhe gcod pa'i tshig ngan la sogs pa tha na pha rol pa'i yid du mi 'ong ba'i rnam 'gyur phra mo tshun chad spangs te/ dus rtag tu 'dzum pa'i bzhin dang / snyan pa'i gsung
gis pha rol po'i yid yongs su tshim par mdzad pa sogs mdor na sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi rnam thar dang khyad par ci'ang med par byang
chub sems dpa'i spyod tshul rgya mtsho lta bu las dus skad cig kyang g.yel ba med pa zhig go /khyad par rig pa 'dzin pa sngags kyi sdom pa'i dbang du byas na bya ba
dang / spyod pa dang / rnal 'byor dang / rnal 'byor chen po bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi dbang bskur ba rnams legs par gsan phyin chad rgyud sde 'og ma so so'i dam tshig rnams
dang / rgyud sde gong ma rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i dbang bzhi so so'i dam tshig mtha' dag srung sdom tshul bzhin du mdzad pa la brten nas/ nyes ltung gi dri ma phra zhing
phra bas kyang ma gos shing / de'i ngang nas dngos grub thams cad kyi rtsa bar gyur pa dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams nges par rdo rje 'chang dngos

yin pa la the tshom cung zad kyang mi mnga' ba'i thugs dad bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgo nas zhal bzhugs pa'i dus su'ang lus ngag yid gsum longs spyod dang bcas pas mnyes par
bya ba kho na las/ mi mnyes pa skad cig kyang mi mdzad cing / zhi bar gshegs nas kyang gong du bshad pa ltar dus dran gyi mchod pa sogs ma chags par mdzad cing rgyun du'ang
gsol 'debs nar mar mdzad pa dang / thugs dam mnyams bzhes kyi rim pa'ang / gong du bshad pa ltar gyi yi dam lha'i ljags bsnyen rnams mdzad pa dang / dus rgyun du'ang
lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi rtsi dang ma bral ba'i sgo nas/ lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang / dpal kye rdo rje phyi nang sbrags ma'i mngon rtogs lam dus kyi dbang
blang ba dang bcas pa shin tu rgyas pa dang / rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi srung ba dang / nA ro mkha' spyod ma ste sa skya pa'i chag med bzhir grags pa rnams dang / 'jam dbyangs
dkar po dang / 'byung po 'dul byed dang / mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu dang / rdo rje brag rdzong ma rnams kyi mngon rtogs bzlas pa dang bcas pa dang / spyan ras gzigs
kyi bdag bskyed sngon du 'gro ba'i dzaM ser nag gi chu sbyin dang / gtor ma brgya rtsa dang / dbyu gu drug cu rtsa bzhi dang / yi dwags la chu sbyin dang bcas pa rnams
dang / gtor bsngo'i rim pa'ang kye rdo rje dang / mkha' spyod ma dang / 'byung po 'dul byed dang / mgon dkar dang / gur zhal gnyis dang / dur bdag dang / las mgon dang /
stag zhon dang / dmag zor ma dang / bektse dang / mkha' 'gro spyi ste de rnams la gtor 'bul gyi cho ga shin tu rgyas pa dang bcas pa rnams ma chag par mdzad cing / skabs
skabs su de'i steng du yi dam gyi lha 'ga' zhig gi bdag bskyed gsung ba

sogs mdor na chos 'chad nyan gyi thugs brel yod pa'i skabs ma gtogs/ rgyun par snga dro nas nyi ma phyed ma zin tsam gyi bar du thugs dam kho na dang / de nas skabs su bab
pa'i thugs brel rnams bcad cing / slar yang dgongs mo'i dus rtsa brgyud kyi bla ma'i sku bstod dang / brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs kha shas gsung bzhin pa'i sgo nas sku 'chags
kyi zhabs skor ci rigs par mdzad cing / de nas sa srib tsam nas bzung ste mtshan phyed ma zin tsam gyis bar du thugs dam kho na la gzhol ba sogs mdor na brtson 'grus drag
pos nyin mtshan khor yug kun tu mnyam par bzhag pa'i rnal 'byor dang / mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i rnal 'byor rnams ltag sprad de nyams su bzhes pa la brten nas tha mal gyi
rnam par rtog pas skad cig kyang brdzi bar mi nus pa yin no/ /de ltar sdom pa gsum la gces spras su mdzad cing nyams su bzhes pa'i stobs kyis spangs pa dang rtogs pa'i yon
tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa thugs rgyud la 'khrungs par gor ma chag na'ang / bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'dis ni rang gi yon tan thams cad bum nang gi mar me bzhin
du sbas te ci'ang mi mkhyen pa'i tshul kho na mdzad cing / de'ang chos dang 'jig rten gyi bya ba che phra thams cad la mkhyen rab kyi klong shin tu che bar snang mod/ tha
na 'jig rten gyi bya ba phra mo tshun chad la nged kyis ci'ang mi shes kho na gsung zhing / dag pa'i gzigs snang dang / nyams rtogs la sogs pa ji 'dra 'khrungs zhes bka'
'dri zhus na'ang / nga lta bu la nyams rtogs ga la 'ong kho na gsung pa dang / bdag cag bu slob rnams kyis bsod nams kyi tshogs rdzogs pa'i slad du rje nyid kyi rnam thar
zhig bri rgyu yin tshul zhus pa'i tshe'ang / nga lta bu'i bla ma'i rnam thar 'bri nyan ga la yod kho na gsung pa sogs mdor na sngon gyi bka' gdams pa'i dge ba'i

bshes gnyen dam pa rnams dang / grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po zhang ston chos 'bar sogs kyi rnam thar dang tshul mtshungs par sbas pa'i brtul zhugs kho na 'dzin par mdzad pas/
dag pa'i gzigs snang dang spangs rtogs kyi yon tan ji ltar 'khrungs su zhig gis rtogs par nus/ 'on kyang sku na chung ngu'i dus su lan re lan gnyis tsam ma yin par dus
rtag tu spyan zur gyis gzigs pa'i tshe/ mdun gyi nam mkhar birWa pa dang sa chen gnyis zhal sprod kyi rnam par bzhugs pa khra lam mer gzigs shing / de la ched du gtad nas
spyan cher gyis gzigs pa'i tshe yal 'gro ba zhig yod ces gsung ba dang / yang lan cig mnal lam du ngor gyi rgyab ri'i ngos su gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras kyi bla ma
brgyud pa rnams tshang bar bzhugs shing / bla ma re re'i mtha' skor du'ang 'ja' kha dog lnga lngas bskor ba zhig shin tu gsal bar byung gsung ba sogs la dpags na dag pa'i
gzigs snang yang mang du byung bar mngon la/ gzhan yang sngar bod du bzhugs pa'i skabs khang gsar mkhan rin po che ngag dbang blo gros bzang pos e wa~M pa'i mkhan sa rtsis
sprod gnang ba'i tshe/ e wa~M pa thams cad kyis da ni mkhan por 'os pa rje 'di kho na las med pas mkhan po mdzad dgos par thag bcad na'ang / rje 'di'i zhal snga nas
nged kyi rmi lam du skas zhig la 'dzegs par brtsams pa'i tshe/ khyi zhig gis bkag pa snyam byed pa'i snang ba zhig byung bas da lan mkhan po byed mi dgos pa 'dra zhes bka'
stsal pa ltar/ de lo gzim phrug khang yongs 'dzin dpal ldan chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis e wa~M pa'i mkhan po zhal 'dzin gnang bar brten rje 'dis mkhan po mdzad dgos ma byung
ba dang / yang mdo khams su lan rjes ma phebs pa'i skabs/ phyogs de'i bla

ma phal che bas sa g.yos kyi 'jigs pa chen po yong bar gsungs kyang / rje 'dis de 'dra'i skyon ci'ang mi 'ong tshul gsungs pa'ang de kho na ltar gyur pa dang / yang rje rang
gi zhabs 'bring bar/ nged tshe 'dir rgyu rkyen rten 'brel legs 'grig ma byung ba'i rkyen gyis slob gnyer cher ma shes pa ma gtogs/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyi
skye mtha' de yin snyam pa sems la shar zhes yang yang bka' stsal 'dug cing / rje sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa ni mgon po 'od dpag tu med pa'i ye shes sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i
rol gar dpal ldan a ti sha'i rnam 'phrul yin par mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong gi rnam thar du gsal ba dang / yang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang pos ngor dbang
khang du rje 'di nyid las lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs thog mar gsan pa'i skabs grub chen bi rU pa'i sku'i rnam par gsal bar gzigs pas rkyen byas te/ de phyin
rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi sprul pa'i sku rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug dang dbyer med pa'i thugs nges brtan por 'khrungs par snang bas sku tshe snga ma'i skye
brgyud kyang des mtshon par nus pa dang / gzhan yang lo snga ma lcags bya lor bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po byams pa kun dga'
bstan 'dzin de nyid sku bsnyun pa'i tshul bstan pa'i tshe'ang / rje 'dis da lan gyi snyun gzhi 'di sel mi thub pa 'dra zhes yang yang bka' stsal kyang / bdag cag rnams
kyis de tsam gyi skyon cher rang e yong snyam mod/ rjes sor de kho na ltar gyur pa sogs de 'dra'i rigs can shin tu mang zhing / tshul de rnams la gzhig na mngon par shes
pa'ang thogs med mnga' bar snang mod/ su zhig gis shes par nus/ grub pa'i mtshan ma ni mdo khams su lan rjes ma phebs pa'i tshe/ gong du bshad pa ltar

shin tu sra shing mkhregs pa'i rdo yi ngos su phyag mdzub kyis ma Ni bris pa dang / yang bzhad thub bstan yangs can gyi grwa sa ba rje 'di'i zhal slob yin pa gcig gis kye rdo
rje'i gzhi bsnyen byed pa'i tshe bar chad kyi rnam pas nad drag po zhig gis btab par brten/ rje 'di la gsol ba phur tshugs su btab pas snga dro'i dus shig la rje 'di seng
ge dkar mo zhig la chibs te phebs byung bas/ khyod kyis nyams len la brtson pa skyed cig /nad las grol bar 'gyur ro zhes bka' stsal byung ba ltar/ de ma thag nas rim
gyis nad las grol ba yin ces kho rang gi ngag las thos shing / de lta bu'i grub pa'i mtshan ma rnams ni sngon gyi rgya gar gyi grub thob chen po rnams kyi rnam par thar pa
dang khyad par ci'ang mi snang bas/ don la grub pa'i go 'phang mthon por gshegs par gdon mi za ba dang / gzhan yang sku dngos kyis dbang bskur ba dang / byin gyis brlabs
pas ni 'gal rkyen bar chad las grol ba lta ci smos/ ljags chab dang / gsang chab tshun chad kyis kyang skye bo mang po nad gdon las grol bar mdzad pa dang / yid dam lha'i
sgrub mchod dang / bka' chos 'chad spel sogs gang dang gang stsal kyang sngon khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi gsung rgyun dang phyag len ji ltar stsal
ba de kho na ltar las sla chos su gtan nas ma song bar mdzad cing / gzhan dag la'ang de ltar dgos pa'i dgag sgrub kyi bca' ba dam po mdzad pa dang / ris su med pa'i
grub mtha' thams cad la dag snang phyogs med du mdzad pa las/ skye bo ngan pa gzhan gyi spyod tshul lta bu'i chags sdang rigs lta ci/ chos par rlom pa dang skyes bu dam par
grags pa kha cig kyang rang gzhan gyi grub mtha'i phyogs bzung nas gzhan la zur gyis smod pas chos la

brten nas sdig pa gsog pa de lta bu'i rigs gtan nas mi mdzad pa thams cad la mngon sum tshad mas grub pa dang / lhag par yon tan gyis khyad par du byas pa'i sde snod 'dzin
pa dang / rgyud sde 'dzin pa rnams la zhe sa dang bkur sti phun sum tshogs pa'i sgo nas gzengs bstod cing / de dag gi yon tan sgrogs pa dang / rang nyid spangs pa dang rtogs
pa'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa la dbang 'byor zhing che rgu thams cad kyi gtsug gi nor bus zhabs kyi padmo la btud par gyur na'ang khengs pa dang dregs pa lta ci/
dman pa'i brtul bzhugs kho na 'dzin pa yin te zhal nas kyang / nga la spangs rtogs kyi yon tan ci'ang med mod/ sngon las kyis e wa~M pa'i mkhan po sogs byed dgos byung ba
yin gsung ba sogs mdor na rnam par thar pa phyogs gang nas gzhig kyang skyon gyi rnam pa cung zad kyang mi mnga'/ rgyu mtshan de'i phyir na sku mthong ba dang / gsung thos
pa dang / mtshan tsam yid la dran pa tshun chad kyang phan pa dang bde ba 'ba' zhig la sbyor bar mdzad pa'i 'brel tshad don ldan chen por bzhugs shing / sangs rgyas dngos
'jig rten du byon pa dang khyad par ci'ang med cing / gdul bya rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mtha' dag kyang mdzad pa'i phyir/ bka' drin gyi ngos nas sangs rgyas
las kyang ches cher lhag par gyur pa yin no/ /lung dang rtogs pas rab bsdus pa'i/ /bstan pa'i rtsa ba so thar te/ /yon tan rin chen thams cad kyi/ /'byung gnas rin chen
'byung gnas bzhin/ /de slad bag yod ra ba yis/ /yongs bskor tshul khrims khang bzang ni/ /dus kun nyes spyod chom po dang / /bral ba'i sdom pa lha yul bzhin/ /bzod nas byang
chub spyod mchog la/ /mdza' ba'i skud pa dkar po yis/ /rtag tu btsems pa'i byang chub sems/ /gzhar yang med pa nyid mi 'gyur/ /khyod kyis

rang bde la chags pa/ /sdig dang sdug bsngal bzhin bcom nas/ /gzhan bde sgrub la yon tan ltar/ /nam yang ngoms pa med 'di ci/ /rtag tu 'gro la sman mdzad pa'i/ /khyod mtshungs
byed po rmongs pa des/ /ci yang byas par ma gyur pas/ /dpe yis kyang ni shin tu dbul/ /dam pa'i don du srid zhi gnyes/ /mnyam pa nyid du rab gzigs pas/ /'dir snang 'jig
rten chos brgyad kyi/ /rdzun ris dbang po'i gzhu bzhin yal/ /bstan pa'i nying khu gsang sngags kyi/ /spyod tshul gser gyi 'khor lo yis/ /cir snang lhan skyes ye shes kyi/
/'khor du sdud pa'i dge mtshan ngoms/ /las dang nyon mongs kyis bskyed pa'i/ /tha mal snang bas rab dbul yang / /dngos kun lha sngags ye shes su/ /'char ba'i 'byor pa
shin tu mtho/ /snying po'i bstan pa rab 'dzin pa/ /khyod 'dra gzhan na ma dmigs pas/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug yab sras kyang / /dgyes pas 'bral med bzhugs sam snyam/ /mgon
khyod gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi/ /bstan pa'i bdag por nges rnyed nas/ /brgyud pa'i bla ma thams cad kyang / /shis pa bsgrub phyir byon min nam/ /ji bzhin gzigs pa'i nyin
byed kyis/ /'gro 'di'i blo mun rab bsal bas/ /phyogs kyi bu mo smin legs mas/ /bsngags pa'i rgyud mangs ci yang bsgrengs/ /ngo mtshar grub pa'i rol rtsed kyis/ /skal bzang
spro ba skyed bsrings pas/ /'brel tshad don dang ldan pa ru/ /nges pa'i ka ba snying la tshugs/ /mgon khyod yon tan gyis 'byor yang / /'khor ba'i skyon gyis shin tu dbul/
/che rgu'i gtsug na rab 'dzegs kyang / /dman pa'i brtul zhugs kho na 'dzin/ /gang gis yon tan skyon bzhin du/ /sbas kyang grags pas mkha' ltar khyab/ /nyin byed

chu 'dzin gyis bsgribs kyang / /'od kyis 'jigs rten gsal bzhin mdzes/ /de slad gang gi yon tan ni/ /rgya mtsho bas kyang shin tu zab/ /ri rab mchog las rnam par mtho/ /lha
yul las kyang ngo mtshar che/ /khyod kyi rnam thar thub dbang ltar/ skyon bral yon tan ldan mthong nas/ /bsam bzhin dad pa'i padmo ni/ /nyin bzhin rgyas pa kho nar gyur//
//spyi don bdun pa mthar gdul bya rtag 'dzin can dang le lo can rnams chos la bskul ba'i slad du gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos kyi dbyings su bsdus kyang sems can gyi don rgyun
mi 'chad pa'i tshul ni/ bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bka' drin 'khor mtha' dang bral ba 'dis ni dgung grangs don drug tu ma phebs kyi bar la bstan pa dang sems
can gyi don rgya chen po mdzad de/ sras kyi thu bo rnams ni yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phung por byin gyis brlabs te mtha' yas pa'i sems can thams cad srid pa'i rgya
mtsho chen po las sgrol ba'i 'dren pa dam par mnga' gsol/ 'ga' zhig ni ma 'ongs pa na 'gro ba 'dren pa'i nus pa dang ldan par mdzad/ gzhan yang sku mthong ba dang / gsung
thos pa dang / mtshan tsam yid la byed pa dang / sku'i grib ma phog pa tshun chad kyi sems can thams cad kyang phan pa dang bde ba 'ba' zhig la 'god par mdzad pa sogs sku
dngos kyis gdul bar 'os pa rnams ni legs par btul/ da ni bdag cag skal dman rnams kyi bsod nams kyi bgo skal re zhig de tsam du zad pa dang / sku'i bkod pa gzhan gyis
sems can gyi don rgya chen po mdzad pa'i dus la bab par gzigs nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul ston par bzhed de/ de'ang sngar dgung grangs lnga bcu dang drug cu'i
nang du phebs pa'i skabs rnams su rje'i zhal nas/ lo bdun cu don grangs tsam thub na mi tshe

mthar phyin pa yin/ de bas lhag bsdad kyang yar langs mi thub/ mar sdod mi thub/ phar 'gro mi thub pa sogs dmigs bsal rang gis rang la sdug gtad pa kho na las med/ ces rgyun
du yang yang bka' stsal bar phal cher ni btang snyoms ngang nas ci'ang mi sems/ la las ni 'di rtag tu rang bka' stsal zhes sun pa'i rnam pa'ang byed/ khyad par dgung grangs
don bzhir phebs pa chu khyi lor/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin zhi bar gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs sgrub pa'i skabs rnams su'ang / da mkhan bgres
rin po che ni zhi bar gshegs song / ban rgan nga yang da lo dang da gzod gnyis bsdad/ sang phod byi lo la ni 'gro ran pa yin ces bdag la'ang yang yang bka' stsal zhing
/ gzhan rnams la'ang yang yang bka' stsal 'dug pas/ phal che bas ni dus rgyun gyi bka' de lta bu yin snyam pa 'dra zhig las ci yang mi sems/ log rtog can la las ni/ 'di
'dra rang gi bka' gsal drags na nam phug mis 'phyas yong zer ba 'dra'ang mchis/ dad pa can bsam yod 'ga' res ni rje 'dis nga la 'di ltar bka' stsal byung bas da legs po
rang 'ong rgyu min pa 'dra zhes blo mi bde ba byed mkhan kyang mchis/ bdag gis rje rang la zhabs brtan 'dra bsgrubs na legs rgyu min nam/ mnal ltas la sogs pa ngan pa 'dra'ang
med dam zhus pas/ da na so rgas drags pas zer ba yin/ gzhan rmi ltas ngan pa sogs ci'ang med/ zhabs brtan ni dge ba 'dra ci 'grub byed pa 'di yin mod/ de las dmigs
bsal gyi zhabs brtan dgos kyang mi dgos/ dus la bab na zhabs brtan gyis kyang phan pa med ces bka' stsal/ sku gzugs ni dgung grangs don bzhi pa dang / don lnga pa'i zla
ba drug pa phan la dus

rgyun las bde ba ltar snang zhing / mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang khu dbon gyi dus chen bla mchod la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang kun rig dang / sgrol ma maNDal bzhi chog sogs mdzad
cing de dag gi tshogs dbur phebs pa dang / khyad par sde dge chos rgyal chen po'i bstan srid la nyag dgras gnod cing 'tshe bar gyur pa la shin tu thugs khral che bar mdzad
cing / de la phan pa'i slad du mgon khang khag rnams su skong ba dang / lha khang khag rnams su yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga la sogs pa mdzad cing / de dag gi tshogs dbur
phebs pa dang / dgung grangs don lngar phebs pa chu mo phag gi lor/ 'di lo dpyid ka mtshar mtshar bgyis te chu tshan zhig la 'gro/ de'ang mang mkhar du phyin na zhor du
phun tshogs gling la sogs pa'i gnas khyad par can 'dra'ang mjal bar 'dug ces bka' phebs na'ang / dbon mdzod mchog nas mang mkhar sa thag ring bas phebs mi nyan tshul zhus
song bas mang mkhar du phebs gru ma song yang / lo de'i hor zla gsum pa'i mjug tsha rong chu tshan du phebs/ de zhor dpal gling du'ang phebs te tshe dbang sogs 'dod chos
rnams stsal/ ri khrus khyim khrus lha bsang sogs mdzad pas dpal gling du 'ja' zug pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas kyang 'ga' zhig byung zhes thams cad kyis gleng / slar hor
zla bzhi pa'i nang ngor du phebs/ de nas bzung zla ba drug pa'i tshes gnam gang bar sku khams dwangs bzhugs yin la/ gnam stong gi nyin snga dro shing tog phran bu zhig
kyang gsol ba dang / phyi dro 'bri zho zhig kyang cung zad gsol song bas rkyen byas pa yin nam/ de'i phyi nyin zla ba bdun pa'i tshes gcig gi snga dro nas bzung glo bur du
sku grang lta bu'i bsnyun tshul tshabs cher bzhes pa dang / de dang lhan cig skyigs bu'ang nyin mtshan bar ma chad par mdzad snang bas/ bdag cag ci

bya gtol med du gyur te gtsug lag khang du 'dus tshogs kyis zhabs brtan tshe chog dang / gzhan yang bdud zlog dang brgya bzhi sogs mang du bgyis pa dang / sman pa so so nas
kyang gsol sman sgo gang zab nas phul bas zhag drug bdun tsam nas phran bu'i sku khams je dwangs su gyur mod/ 'on kyang snyun gzhi gsing dwangs zhig ni gtan nas 'ong rgyu
mi snang bas/ res snyun gzhi cher med kyang gsol chas la dwang ga med pa dang / res mkhal grang gi rnam pa lta bu dang / res zhabs 'bam gyi rnam pa lta bu sogs res 'jog
tu snang zhing / gzhan yang de skabs rnams su dgon pa'i nye skor du wa brgyal ba dang / spyang ki rgyugs pa dang / phyogs gzhan du khang pa yang bsgyel skad kyi dus ma yin
pa'i rlung chen po ldang ba sogs dang / khyad par mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin zhi bar gshegs pa nas bzung / lam 'bras lha khang du bzhugs pa'i
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi 'dra sku rin po che'i zhal mdangs dus rgyun lta bu cung 'ong rgyu mi snang zhes thams cad kyis zer la/ lhag par 'di lo hor zla brgyad pa dang
dgu pa'i nang ngor chen gyi 'dra sku rin po cher spyan chab bsil ba'i rjes lta bu dod pa dang / gzhan yang khams bod kun tu dus kyi 'khrugs rtsod mi bzad pa langs pa
sogs mi dge ba'i ltas mang du byung zhing / de ni 'jig rten gyi phan pa dang bde ba thams cad ni gang zag dam pa 'di dang 'di lta bu'i bsod nams kyi mthu las byung ba yin
la/ de nyid gzhan du bzhud par dgongs pa na 'di lta bu'i snga ltas 'byung ba chos nyid yin te byang chub sems dpa'i skyes rabs dang / sngon gyi gang zag dam pa rnams kyi
rtogs pa brjod pa rnams su'ang de ltar byung ba'i tshul mang du bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /de nas bdag gis zhabs brtan 'dra bsgrubs na zhus kyang /

rje rang gis ni dus la bab zhabs brtan gyis kyang phan pa med tshul bka' phebs pa dang / dbon mdzod mchog nas nad pa shin tu thu ba 'ga' rer rim gro tshabs chen byas pas slar
'chi mgyogs rkyen byed pa 'dra'ang yong 'dug tshul rang bzhin zhus song bas/ rje rang gis kyang rgyab skyor mdzad de/ da rim gro mang po byas kyang 'chi 'gyogs rkyen las
mi yong zhes yang yang bka' stsal rung / bdag gis mchod 'bul zhabs brtan zhig bsgrubs na legs tshul zhus te lha khang khag rnams re mos kyi zla ba gcig dang zhag lnga'i
bar la nyin re bzhin rnam gsum brgya mchod dang bcas te dge slong bzang gras bcu gcig res bla ma mchod pa dang / sman bla'i cho ga dang / tshe lha rnam gsum gyi cho ga
dang / kun rig cho ga dang / gnas brtan cho ga dang / sgrol ma maNDal bzhi chog sogs bgyis pa dang / e wa~M pa'i gtsug lag khang du'ang snga phyir 'dus tshogs kyis tshe chog
lan gsum tsam dang / gzhan yang bdud zlog dang / brgya bzhi la sogs pa zhabs brtan chung chung gi rigs shin tu mang bar bsgrubs rung sku khams la dwangs bskyed du mngon
pa ci'ang mi snang / khyad par dgung grangs don drug tu phebs pa shing byi hor zla gnyis pa'i 'jug nas bzung snyun gzhi cung zad gdangs tshul bzhes shing / 'tsho byed
pa rnams nas kyang de sngon bla rtsar sdod cung zad yod kyang / da sdod cher ma mchis pas lo gcig gnyis zhabs pad brtan pa 'dra zhes zer mod/ rje rang gis ni da lo tshod
sogs gang la gzhig kyang dus la bab pa yin pas zla ba gcig gnyis las e sdod mi shes/ sde dge chos rgyal chen po'i bstan srid la nyag dgras 'tshe ba 'di rang sems khral che/
gzhan da shi rung 'gyod pa til 'bru tsam yang med/ khams bzhugs mchog sprul 'jam dbyangs mkhyen

brtse'i dbang po'ang deng sang sku khams dwangs bzhugs kyi skabs dang / khyod kyang bde ba'i skabs 'dir shi ba'i dus yin/ da nga ni zla ba gcig gnyis kyi mi dang / phyag mdzod
kyang lo gsum bzhi'i mi yin pas nged tsho la blta rgyu ci'ang med/ khams bzhugs mchog sprul rin po che dang / khyod gnyis kyis spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa/ sgos ngor
dgon pa'i bstan pa/ bye brag thar rtse 'di la blta rtog 'dra byed dgos zhes sogs dus tha'i zhal chems mang du bka' stsal bar/ bdag gis da dung lo kha shas zhabs pad brtan
pa'i thugs bskyed bzhes dgos tshul dang / bdag cag rnams kyang thugs rjes rjes su 'dzin dgos tshul zhus pas/ da lo kha shas ga la sdod/ kha'i so/ mgo'i skra gang la bltas
kyang 'gro ran pa yin/ da yun ring bsdad kyang khams pa'i gtam dper mi tshe ring gis than sgugs zer ba lta bu yin ces bka' phebs pa dang / yang nga shi ba'i rjes su
dgongs rdzogs sogs rgya chen gang yang mi dgos/ lam 'bras lha khang du gdan rabs bla brgyud kyi sa bcad stong min tsam du 'dra sku tsam dgos na las/ gzhan dngul gdung sogs
ci'ang mi dgos/ 'on kyang khyod kyis ma shes pa med ces bka' phebs pa dang / zhabs 'bring pa tshor yang khyed tshos nga la zla gcig tsam g.yog gyis/ de nas khyed rang rnams
kyang bsdad pas chog ces yang yang bka' stsal/ sku khams ni zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad bar rim gyis je dngas su gyur/ de skor zhig tu spong ba pa kun dga' bsod nams
kyang mus kyi ri khrod rnams suu mtshams sdod pa'i skabs rje 'di'i zhabs brtan tshe sgrub bgyis pas/ yun ring zhabs pad mi brtan pa'i ltas 'dra shar bas zhal mjal du 'ongs
pa yin ces byon byung ba dang / hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad kyi nyin gsol ba 'dra cung zad ma 'phrod pa dang / de nyin

sku 'chag kyang mang du mdzad song bas/ phran bu'i sku 'khrugs lta bu byung ba yin nam/ gzhan sku khams la gnod rkyen ni ci'ang med mod/ phyi nyin tshes dgu'i nyin gsang chab
kyang 'bab mi thub pa dang / sku gzugs la tsha drod che ba sogs snyun gzhi tsha chu lta bus shin tu sku bsnyel ba'i tshul bstan/ bdag sku mdun du phyin pas/ 'o da ni 'gro
ran song ngo / /de ring nad kyang sdug tu song 'dugs ces bka' stsal bas/ bdag cag ni rtab rtab por gyur te/ de sngon sku khams bde skabs yin gshis 'tsho byed rnams kyang
bsdad med pas gzhis rtser sman pa 'bod du btang ba dang / zhabs brtan 'ga' zhig gi nyer bsdogs 'dra bgyis/ de skabs byams rin sku mdun du zhabs phyir yod pa nyin mo sku
mdun du bsdad/ dgongs mo rang gshag tu 'gro gi yod par/ de nyin nyin phyed tsam nas da khyed rang yang song / nga yang kha ton 'don dgos gsungs thugs brel lta bu mdzad
cing / nyi ma phyed yol tsam nas rje rang gis zhal 'don kho na mdzad/ de rjes nyi ma rgas kha tsam nas dus rgyun dang cung mi 'dra bar thugs 'ur ba'i rnam pa lta bu'i gsung
gsangs mthon pos zhal 'don lam dus rgyas pa tshar gcig /bzlas pa rnams kyang bcu re tsam mdzad song ba dang / mgon dkar dang / bir srung dang / lam zab dang / mkha' spyod
ma rnams kyang bzlas pa nyung shas re dang bcas gsungs song ba dang / gtor bsngo de nged kyis 'don mi thub pa 'dra bas zhabs drung gis 'don rogs gyis gsung ba ltar zhabs
drung nas gtor bsngo rnams 'don pa'i skabs/ rje rang gis kyang gtor bsngo rgyas pa gtor sngags rnams kyang bcu gcig re tsam dang bcas tshar gcig gsungs song / yang de
rjes kyang gtor bsngo rgyas pa tshar gnyis tsam gsungs song ba dang / de rjes gang yin ma 'tshal ba'i sngags mang po zhig bgrang bar mdzad pa sogs mtshan gang zhal 'don
kho na mdzad pa las/

gsung sgros ni tshig re gnyis las mi mdzad/ bdag gis byin rten thams cad bsdus te phul bas legs par gsol song / de nas tho rangs tsam na/ tshe mtshams pa kun bsod da mkha'
spyod ma'i mtshams nam tsam sdod rgyu red ces bka' phebs par/ da lta 'di dus zhes thag chod pa rang mi snang zhus pas/ de'i lan ci'ang mi gsung / de ni bdag cag rnams la
bka' stsal pa'i tha ma yin/ de nas rje rang gis phyag phreng bzhes te/ mkha' spyod ma yin pa 'dra snyam pa'i zhal 'don yun ring po zhig mdzad song / de nas nam langs thag
chod pa tsam na zhal 'don de mtha' bsdus nas phyag phreng yang phar 'jog par mdzad song / de sngon kyang zhabs skyil krung dang sku gzugs drang por bzhugs yod pa yin na'ang
/ slar yang sku gzugs drang por zhog ces pa'i brda lta bu mdzad/ de nas spyan gnyis kyang gyen la bzlog snang / ljags dbugs kyang cung mi 'dra ba zhig tu song / mtshams
pa kun bsod kyang nam langs ma thag ngu bzhin du byon byung bar ci yin dris pas/ da nang tho rangs gnyid du cung zad song ba'i rmi lam du/ lam 'bras lha khang du mchod
mjal la phyin/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i 'dra sku rin po cher byin rlabs zhus te gsol ba btab/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi 'dra
sku'ang de sngon mtshams bsdad pas ma mjal rung / ngor chen gyi sku'i g.yas ngos su bzhugs 'dug pas legs par mjal te gsol ba btab/ sgros cha sogs gang thad nas 'gran bral
byung snang / de'i g.yas ngos su rje 'di sku dngos bzhugs 'dug pas/ 'o da nga ni 'gro ran pa yin/ bu khyod sgrub pa la nan tan snying por gyis shig /ces gsungs nas phyag
gnyis spyi bor bzhag byung bas/ mi phyed pa'i dad pa shugs drag pos mchi ma mang du shor/ gnyid sad nas kyang bsam bzhin

du dad shugs kyi mchi ma rgyun mi 'chad par 'ong ba zhig 'dug /mngon sum las kyang gsal ba'i rmi lam de lta bu zhig byung bas rje 'di sku khams ci 'dra zhes dris byung ba dang
/ gzhis rtse nas 'tsho byed pa dang / de 'bod mi bcas kyang shin tu snga bar yar yong / phyug po gzhung ngos nas yar bltas pas ngor gyi thad kyi nam mkha' thams cad 'ja'
kha dog lnga ldan gyis khrig ger gang 'dug ces gleng / gang ltar yang nyi shar tsam na ljags dbugs kyang mi snang bas/ bdag gis thugs dam gsal 'debs 'dra zhus pas spyan
dmigs lta bu mdzad song ba bcas mdor na dgung grangs don drug tu phebs pa mig dmar zhes pa shing pho byi ba'i lo'i sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcu res gza' zla ba dang / skar
ma rta chung 'dzom pa'i nyi dros sbrul gyi steng du rlung dang byang chub kyi sems thams cad sgra gcan gyi rtsa dbu ma'i nang du zhugs te gzhi la gnas pa'i 'od gsal ma dang
/ bsgom stobs kyis myong ba'i 'od gsal bu gnyis ro gcig tu 'dres nas don gyi 'od gsal zhes bya ba'i 'chi ba chos kyi sku'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs par gyur
to/ /de'i tshe nam mkha'i mtha' skor na sprin mchod pa'i gzugs brnyan 'dra ba cung zad mchis pa dang / nam mkha'i mthongs thams cad kun tu dwangs zhing / nyi ma shin tu
dro ba'i gseb nas gangs lta bu re zung 'babs pa ni bdag cag thams cad kyis mthong bas me tog gi char yin par mngon no/ /de nas nyi ma phyed tsam nas 'ja' sprin gyis nam mkha'
phal cher khyab snang ngo / /bdag cag rnams ni mgon dang skyabs dang dpung gnyen thams cad dang bral bas dang nya bye tshan du dor ba'am/ rgya mtsho'i klong du ded dpon
dang bral ba'i tshong phrug gi tshogs 'khyams pa bzhin du sdug bsngal drag pos non te ci bya gtol med du gyur rung / chos thams cad sems kyi cho 'phrul yin pa dang /

bla ma'i thugs rje dang byin rlabs la nye ring med pa kho na rgyun mtshan du byas nas rang gis rang la sems bso bgyi ba dang / rje rang la gsol ba rtse gcig 'debs pa las gzhan
pa'i thabs zad cing / zhi bar gshegs ma thag nas bzung thugs dam ma grol gyi bar du/ bla ma bstan pa dar rgyas kyi gtsos dge slong bzhis rje nyid kyis dus rgyun du gsungs
pa'i yi dam lha'i mngon rtogs rnams dang / gtor bsngo dang bcas pa nyin re bzhin thun gnyis su bcad nas nyams su blangs pa dang / thugs dam gyi skabs sku'i gzi mdangs
dus rgyun pas legs shing / sku sha dkar ba dang / zhal ras kyi ngos su gnyer ma'ang cher med pa'i gzhon sha chags par mchis/ zla ba de'i tshes bcu gsum gyi nub mo da rang
thugs dam las grol med dam snyam pa 'dra zhig sems la shar te sku gdung rin po che mjal bas de mu ltar mchis/ nam mkha' la yang yang bltas pas 'ja' sprin dkar po shas
che ba'i kha dog lnga ldan gyi 'ja' sprin 'dra mang po shar song / de nub spong ba pa kun bsod lags kyi rmi lam du'ang / lha'i bu dang bu mo mchod rdzas thogs pa bsam gyis
mi khyab pa zhig e wa~M bla brang gzhung gi rgyab nas bskor te phar nub phyogs su song / ci yin dris pas/ mkhan chen rdo rjai 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po dag pa'i
zhing khams su phebs pa yin zer/ 'o na nga'ang bla ma mjal du 'gro snyam phyin pas thar rtse nub sgo dang nye bar slebs/ de na mi nag po 'jigs su rung ba zhig 'gro yin
'dug pa kun bsod la phyi mig cig bltas nas/ khyod da bla ma mjal mos par 'dug te da nangs mkha' spyod la phebs song / de'ang thog mar nub phyogs bde ba can na ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang bzhugs 'dug pas de'i drung du phebs song / nga'ang phebs skyel du phyin pa yin zer thar rtse'i nub sgo'i nang du yar thal gyis

zhugs pa zhig rmis/ gnyid sad nas kyang dga' skyo zung du 'brel ba'i sgo nas mig nas mchi ma mang po shor ces gsungs pa dang / tshes bcu bzhi'i snga dro skya rengs shar ba
tsam na nam mkha' mthing shun ltar sngo zhing shin tu dwangs pa la/ dgon pa'i thad ngos nas nub phyogs su sprin dkar po dar yug brkyangs pa lta bu gnyis 'dug ces gleng ba
dang / de nas nyin phyed tsam na 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan ring thung gsum shar 'dug ces thams cad kyis gleng bas da thugs dam las grol bar gdon mi za snyam nas sku gdung rin
po che'i drung du phyin pas bdag dang lhan cig 'ong ba lta bu'i sbrang bu zhig kyang sku gdung rin po cher 'khor 'dug pa dang / zhal mdangs phran bu nyams pa ltar snang
bas/ slar yang 'od gsal las zung 'jug gi skur bzhengs te/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang lhan cig dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro ma dang chos skyong ba'i srung
ma'i tshogs dang bcas pa rnams kyi bsu ba'i bkod pa so so skye bo'i blo'i spyod yul las 'das pa dang bcas te dag pa'i zhing khams bde ba can la sogs par gshegs par gor
ma chag go /de nas na bza' dang sku gzugs rnams la bltas pas de'i sngon bdag cag rnams kyis ma mthong ba ma gtogs/ shangs bug nas byang sems dkar po mang po mgul gong nang
du babs snang ba thams cad kyang bskams zin 'dug /'di ni ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar sogs nas 'chi kha nyid du phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob nas
rnam shes spyi gtsug tu song ste/ longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i zhing khams su 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i rtags pha'i khu ba'i thig le sna bug g.yon nas mar 'byung ngo /
/zhes bde mchog gi gzhung nas lung 'dren dang bcas te gsungs 'dug pa dang / gsang ba'i gnas kyang sba ba sbubs su nub te gtan nas mi snang /

zhabs 'bring ba tshor dris pas/ /gsang ba'i gnas blta bas mi mngon pa 'di ni sngar nas rang yod pa yin/ phyis dgung grangs bdun cu'i nang du phebs pa'i tshe zhabs pus kyang
mi bde ba dang / sku gsang yang bro ma thag tu stsal dgos pa zhig yod/ de la brten nas thugs brel lta bus gzim tog nang du sku gsang gnang ba'i tshe'ang / res gzim tog gi
nang du gsang chab mi babs par phyi rol tu bo 'ong ba zhig yod pa de'ang sba ba sbubs su nub pa'i rkyen gyis yin ces gleng / 'di lta bu ni sngon gyi dus su rje sa paN dang
/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang dang / chos rje dkon mchog lhun grub sogs la byung zhing / mtshan dpe cha mthun 'di ni ye shes kyi sku mngon du mdzad pa'i rtags yin zhes rnam
thar snga ma rnams su bris 'dug pa ltar ro/ /de nas rin chen 'bar ba las/ bdud rtsi 'khyil ba bzlas pa yi/ /dri zhim chu yis dang por bkru/ /zhes sogs dang / kye rdo
rje'i rgyud rgyas pa las/ sku gsung thugs kyi rigs sngags gdags/ /rang gi lha'am gzhan yang rung / /zhes sogs gsungs pa ltar de sngon mtshams pa so sor yang bum chu bsgrub
rgyu phul yod pa dang / khyad par tshes bcu bzhi'i nub mo dang / bco lnga'i tho rangs bdag cag kha shas kyis dpal kye rdo rje'i bdag gi rnal 'byor sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo
nas las thams cad pa'i bum pa tshul bzhin du bsgrubs shing / de nas tshes bco lnga nyi ma rtse shar tsam na/ sku gdung rin po cher na bza' bzang po dang bcas te bzhugs
khri'i khar bzhugs su gsol nas/ dad pa can thams cad la mjal kha btang ste gsol ba dang smon lam 'debs su gzhug pa dang / de nas grwa pa kha cig gis gzim chung gzhan zhig
tu dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi thig btab cing / bdag cag kha shas kyis nyi dros phyi ma tsam na

'jig rten kun gyi mchod sdong bla na med pa'i sku gdung rin po cher gong du bshad pa ltar gyi bum pa'i chus sku khrus legs par gsol zhing / sku'i gnas gsum du sku gsung thugs
kyi sa bon dang / dpal kye rdo rje'i rtsa sngags dang / snying po dang / nye snying rnams shog bu la bris shing dri bzang pos byug pa rnams sbyar ba dang / bsil ba'i sman
dri bzang po dang ldan pa thams cad lhan cig tu sbyar ba'i lde gus yongs su byugs shing / ras ser po mang pos legs par dkris pa dang / dbu rgyan dang / stod g.yog dang
/ smad g.yogs la sogs pa'i lha rdzas kyi na bzas mdzes par spras te/ dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gang du bzhengs pa'i gnas kyi gzim chung du spyan drangs te/ spos mar
me zhal zas rnams re re nas brgya phrag lnga tsam dang bcas pa'i mchod pa'i bye brag mtha' yas pa'i dbus su gdung sgrom gyi steng du bzhugs su gsol/ de nas bdag cag dge
slong bcus sku gdung rin po che rnam snang dges pa rdo rjer yan lag bzhi rdzogs su bskyed de bzlas pa bya ba sogs rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i kye rdor dus tha'i cho
ga sogs nas ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bgyis so/ /de nub bdag cag dge slong bcus dpal dges pa rdo rje'i sta gon gyi cho ga bgyis pa nas bzung / zhag zhe dgu'i bar du dge slong
bcus dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub cing mchod pa dang / bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba la sogs pa nyin rer cho ga tshar re ma chag
par bgyis pa dang / de thams cad la nyin re bzhin grwa pa re la phyag 'gyed dngul zho re dang / skabs 'gar de'i steng tshab ra la sogs pa'i bsnyen bkur zhabs tog phun sum
tshogs pa bsgrubs pa dang / de'ang bdun phrag re re rdzogs pa'i mthar rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gshegs su gsol zhing / slar yang thig

btab ste sta gon bya ba sogs rje btsun rin po ches dus tha'i cho ga las ji ltar bshad pa bzhin bgyis pa dang / dus tha'i cho ga dngos kyang gang zag mchog la bya ba'i tshul
ji ltar bshad pa ltar thog mar bdun phrag gnyis kyi bar la sku gdung rin po che rnam par snang mdzad kye rdo rjer bskyed cing / ye shes pa gzhug pa sogs bgyis pa dang /
dbang bskur ba ni rje btsun rin po ches gzhan phan bdud rtsi las/ bla ma'am gang zag mchog la byed na/ dbang la sogs pa len mkhan ni gang zag mchog de yin la/ dbang skur
mkhan de ni dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo la sogs pa sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs rnams yin zhing / bdag gis bla ma'i zhabs tog byed par dmigs na bsod nams
mchog tu 'gyur gyi/ gzhan du na bdag slob dpon lta bur bsgoms na ni bdag nyid la nyes par 'gyur ro/ /des na bdag g.yog gam/ zhabs tog byed par bsam pa gal che'o/ /zhes bka'
stsal pa ltar dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bos dbang rnams phul bar bsams te/ dbang tshig rnams bdag gis brjod pa dang / maNDal 'bul ba dang / dbang rdzas 'bul ba sogs las kyi
rdo rje'i bya ba thams cad bdag gis bgyis te/ mdor na bdun phrag gnyis kyi bar la dus tha'i cho ga dbang dang bcas pa'i zhabs tog bgyis pa dang / bdun gsum pa man chad la
dus tha'i cho ga dang / dbang sogs kyi spros pa ci'ang ma byas par bla ma dang dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo dbyer med du dmigs te bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba kho na bgyis
pa yin la/ bdun phrag bdun pa'i dkyil 'khor gshegs gsol gyi nyin dpal bo'i ston mo'am tshogs 'khor du grags pa dang / rdul tshon chu bor spyan 'dren pa dang / gtor 'bul
la sogs pa cho ga mtha' rgyas kyi tshul du bgyis pa dang / de'ang

thog mar thugs dam grol ba nas bzung / sku gdung rin po cher zhugs ma phul gyi bar du nyin re bzhin spos mar me zhal zas rnams re re nas brgya phrag gnyis gsum re ma chag par
phul ba dang / de nas kyang dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la nyin re bzhin rnam gsum brgya mchod re ma chad par phul ba dang / yang sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcu nas bzung
dgung zhag zhe dgu ma rdzogs kyi bar zhag lnga bcu nga bzhi la nyin re bzhin dge slong bcus snga dro bdag bskyed bsnyen rgyas dang 'brel ba'i dpal kun tu rig pa'i ras bris
la brten pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / phyi dro bdag bskyed rdo rje sems dpa' dang 'brel ba'i kun rig gi cho ga re ste tshar gnyis ma chad par bgyis pa dang / de'ang
bla ma dang dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo dbyer med du dmigs te bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba kho na bgyis pa yin la/ khyad par bdun tshigs re rdzogs nyin dge tshogs byang
chub tu bsngo ba'i phyir tshogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon du bla ma re re gdan zhus dang 'brel bar dge slong nyi shu res kun rig gi cho ga tshar gnyis re bgyis pa dang /
de thams cad la'ang nyin re bzhin mchod pa shin tu rgyas pa dang / grwa pa re la nyin re bzhin phyag 'gyed dngul zho re phul ba sogs bsnyen bkur zab pa dang / yang bdun
tshig re re'i mtshams su dge slong bzhi res rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub cing mchod pa dang / bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang
ba sogs bgyis pa dang / yang e wa~M pa'i lam 'bras lha khang sogs dang / rje rang gi gzim chung bcas re mos kyis nyin re bzhin brgya mchod re dang bcas te dge slong bcu
skor res snga phyir bla ma mchod pa nyin nyi shu skor bgyis pa dang / de dag so sor grwa pa rer yon 'bul dngul zho re dang bcas pa'i bsnyen bkur zab pa dang / thugs dam
grol ba nas bzung rim gyis e wa~M bla brang

gzhung du mkhan rin po che khri thog pa ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi mdun du skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi dgongs pa chos dbyings su rdzogs pa'i ljags bsngo
thugs smon zhu mtshon lha gos dang / rdor dril/ gos chen gyi stod rtse spus legs/ chung ja 'khor drug gcig bcas phul ba dang / de bzhin du klu ldings zhabs drung rin po
che byams pa tshul khrims phun tshogs pa dang / khang gsar mchog sprul rin po che 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho pa dang / khang gsar zhabs drung chung ba ngag dbang
blo gros snying po bcas so so'i mdun du'ang ljags bsngo zhu mtshon gyi 'bul ba gong mtshungs re phul/ bla brang phan bde khang gsar du de skabs mkhan po zhabs drung gnyis
ka khams su phebs nas bzhugs med na'ang / de dag gi 'bul skal lam mchod thebs kyi zhal 'debs su gser zangs kyi mar me mdzad dang / rdor dril/ ljon ja 'khor drug gnyis/ 'bras
dkar ltang sogs phul ba dang / bdun tshigs dang po rdzogs nyin kun rig gi rdo rje slob dpon du klu ldings zhabs drung rin po che byams pa tshul khrims phun tshogs gdan
zhus kyi 'bul bar gser zangs kyi thang stong rgyal po'i sku dang / gser Dar dngul shan ma 'phan dang bcas pa/ phyag ting dngul thag dang bcas pa/ dngul gyi 'gu tshe theb
lnga tshar dang bcas pa/ rgya rol che legs cha/ mdzod gos Tam ris dmar ser gyi shan ldan sku sbyar me long ma/ mdzod gos mtshal kha'i stod 'bogs sram rgyan ma/ sbu har
gyi zhabs lhwam 'ja' chen/ phying dmar/ ljon ja brgyad pa 'khor drug gnyis/ 'bras dos sogs phul ba dang / sku tshigs gnyis par khang sar mchog sprul rin po che 'jam dbyangs
shes rab rgya mtsho gdan zhus kyi 'bul bar gser zangs kyi slob dpon za hor ma dang / dngul

gyi maNDal/ dngul ting bdun tshar/ gser Dar dngul shan ma 'phan dang bcas pa/ rgya rol spus legs cha/ srab ther gyi sku sham spus legs/ gos chen sman sham gyis mtha' lcags
byas pa'i sku sbyar/ gos chen rgya smug gi stod 'bogs sram rgyan ma/ spu har gyi zhabs lhwam 'ja' chen/ phying khra/ ja brgyad pa 'khor gnyis/ 'bras ltang sogs phul ba dang
/ bdun tshigs gsum pa rdzogs nyin khang gsar zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros snying po gdan zhus kyi 'bul bar gser zangs kyi don yod grub pa dang / dngul gyi
'bru par shubs ldan/ zangs bum kha mchu zhabs gsum dngul las grub pa/ thod DAr dngul shan ma 'phan bcas shubs ldan/ gos chen rgyan bzhi'i shan ldan gyi na bza' 'gan sbyar/
srab ther gyi sku sham/ ras lhwam/ li ldir/ ras khra'i mnam yol/ ljon ja brgyad pa 'khor gcig /'bras dos sogs dang / sku tshigs bzhi par thar rtse rang gi zhabs drung
'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rjer dngul kyi bkra shis rdzas brgyad sogs 'bul ba 'os 'tsham dang / bdun tshigs lnga par dpon slob las thog pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan par rdor
dril dang / gos chen gyi stod rtse/ ras lhwam/ ja brgyad pa 'khor gcig sogs dang / bdun tshigs drug par bla ma bstan pa dar rgyas la gos chen gyi tshar stod/ rgya ther gyi
gzan/ dngul gyi chab blugs/ ras lhwam/ ja sbag gnyis bcas dang / bdun tshig bdun par sprul sku shes rab rgya mtsho par gos chen gyi stod rtse dang / srab gzan/ phrug gzan/
ja sbag gnyis bcas phul ba dang / gzhan yang khang ser dpon slob 'jam dbyangs grags pa cho ga'i dbu bzhugs sogs su phebs ma thub stabs mchod bsngo zhu mtshon gyi 'bul
bar rdor dril dang /

ljon 'dab 'khor gcig sogs phul ba dang / hor nyag brag sprul skur cho ga gsung rten phar phul bar gos chen gyi stod rtse dang / ljon 'dab 'khor gcig dang / sga stod chos rje
spang shar bla ma dang / 'dzi phu bla ma bcas so sor cho ga gsung rten phar phul bar rdor dril re re dang / mgo snam kha/ ras lhwam/ dkar yug sogs phul ba dang / tshe mtshams
pa bsod nams bzang po dang / tshe mtshams pa kun dga' bsod nams dang / tshe mtshams pa ngag dbang chos 'phel dang / bka' 'gyur bla ma bcas so sor mtshams zla re bzhugs
rgyu'i rten du dngul srang gsum re phul ba dang / dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi gtsug lag khang du nyin re bzhin rnam gsum brgya mchod dang bcas te dge 'dun gang yod kyi
dpal kun tu rig pa'i cho ga nyin bdun dang / bla mchod nyin gnyis te nyin tshogs dgu bgyis pa'i thog mar nyin gcig la dge slong re rer phyag 'gyed dngul zho re phul ba dang
/ de rjes nyin drug la nyin re bzhin grwa pa re la phyag 'gyed dngul Tam phyed re phul ba dang / de rjes nyin gnyis la nyin re bzhin grwa pa nyi shu re la phyag 'gyed
ljon 'dab sbag re phul ba dang / de dag gi dge tshogs byang chub snying por bsngo ba'i slad du mkhan rin po che khri thog par tshogs bsngo lan gnyis zhus pa'i 'bul bar ljon
'dab 'khor gnyis sogs phul ba dang / dpon slob la'ang tshogs bsngo zhu mtshon ljon ja sbag gnyis bcas dang / yang sa ga zla ba'i nang e wa~M pa'i gtsug lag khang du dge
'dun gang yod kyis ngor lugs dkyil 'khor lnga'i sgrub mchod tshogs pa'i skabs kyang 'phar ma nyin gcig btsugs te/ de'ang rten gyi drung du rnam gsum brgya mchod gnyis
dang / dkyil 'khor so sor mchod pa dang / dge 'dun rnams la mang jas bsnyen bkur ba sogs zab pa dang / snga tshogs su grwa pa bcu re la phyag 'gyed ljon ja sbag re dang /
phyi tshogs su grwa pa re la phyag 'gyed dngul Tam re dang /

de'i steng dar kha bsod kyi tshab ra bcas phul ba dang / las tshan so sor yang snga tshogs dang phyi tshogs bcas su rnam gzhag gang zab dang / de nyin mkhan rin po che khri
thog pa tshogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon du phebs pa'i 'bul bar gser zangs las grub pa'i ston pa dang / rdor dril la sogs pa sku gsung thugs kyi rten/ dar ras ling gos chen
mgo snam la sogs pa tshan grangs kyi rigs shin tu mang po/ ja 'khor drug gnyis/ shing thog dang 'bras dos la sogs pa zab par phul ba dang / gzhan chos grwa chen po bkra shis
lhun por paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i mchog sprul rin po che'i mdun ljags bsngo zhu mtshon ston pa'i gser sku dang / rdor dril theg chen/ mgo snam gyon 'dang / ljon
ja 'khor gnyis/ rta pho gcig /'bras ltang sogs phul ba dang / yongs 'dzin dang / sngags chen dang / zur bzhi bcas kyi bla ma so sor ljags bsngo zhu mtshon gyi 'bul ba dang
/ dgon de'i 'du khang dang lha khang gtso che gras rnams su rnam lnga brgya mchod dang / de bying gi lha khang rnams su'ang mchod 'bul cung zad dang bcas pa/ tshogs chen
la mang ja dang / de'i nang tshan khron sbug mi tshan la mang ja bcas zab pa dang / khyad par bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por khri chen thams
cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang bkra shis rin chen gyi spyan sngar ljags bsngo zhu mtshon ston pa'i gser sku dang / rdor dril/ dar gos la sogs pa'i tshan grangs dang / dngul
Tam srang lnga/ ja 'khor gnyis sogs dang / skyabs mgon dngos grub dpal 'bar dang / ngag dbang rdo rje rin chen dang / 'jam mgon kun dga' bsod nams bcas so so'i mdun du rdor
dril/ dngul Tam srang gsum re/ ja 'khor drug re re bcas phul ba dang / gdung sras chung ba gnyis so sor rdor dril dang / bzang ja sbag gnyis re/ dngul Tam srang do re
bcas phul ba dang / rje btsun ma mgres gzhon bcu

gnyis dang / lha khang mkhan po bcas su bsngo zhus ljon 'dab sbag re re dang / chos grwa chen po der bzhugs pa'i rten gsum ngo mtshar can so so'i mdun du brgya mchod dang /
mgon khang khag rnams su sa lam gyi bar chad zhi zhing thugs bzhed lhun gyis grub pa'i phyir chos srung rnams la skong ba dang / sgrol ma lha khang du sgrol chog dang /
lha khang chen mor rnam lnga brgya mchod dang / dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor mang ja'i bsnyen bkur bcas bsgrubs pa dang / zhwa lu ri sbug mchog sprul rdo rje 'chang chen
po'i spyan sngar ljags bsngo zhu mtshon dngul Tam srang lnga dang / ljon ja 'khor drug gcig /zhwa lu ri mthil gyi slob dpon so sor bsngo zhus dang / dgon de'i rten gsum gyi
drung du brgya mchod dang / dgon par mang ja gsum gyis bsnyen bkur ba dang / tshar chen rin po che'i gdan sa mdar grong mo cher rnam lnga brgya mchod dang / mkhan por
bsngo rten/ 'dus tshogs su kun rig nyin btsugs kyi grwa pa rer phyag 'gyed dngul skar lnga re dang / mang mkhar thub bstan dge 'phel dang / mang mkhar dar rgyas dgon/ mang
mkhar dgon pa shar/ mang mkhar bsam grub dgon/ mang mkhar gnas gsang sngags sde/ lha rtse chos sde/ rtag brtan phun tshogs gling / ri khrod jo nang / bzhad bkra shis dge
'phel/ bzhad padma chos sdings/ bzhad grwa tshang chen mo/ bzhad dngul chu/ bzhad gru 'dzin/ bzhad ltang dgon/ bzhad dpal ldan sdings/ bzhad dgon gsar/ bzhad dgon sbug
/bzhad chos sgo/ bzhad 'bru dgon/ bzhad dgon pa byang bcas kyi dgon pa so sor mang jas bsnyen bkur ba dang / bla ma rnams su bsngo zhus dang rten gsum phal cher ba'i mdun
brgya mchod dang bcas pa dang / rgyang 'bum mo che dang / mang mkhar mu gu lung du rnam gsum brgya mchod dang / mus rab 'byams pa'i gdan sa bzhad thub bstan yangs pa

can du brgya mchod dang / mkhan po gsar rnying dang slob dpon so sor bsngo zhus dang / dgon par mang ja dang / grwa pa re la phyag 'gyed dngul skar lnga re dang / kun mkhyen
bsod nams seng ge'i gdan sa rta nag thub bstan du rnam lnga brgya mchod/ mkhan po dang slob dpon so sor bsngo zhus dang / 'dus tshogs su mang ja dang / grwa pa re la phyag
'gyed dngul skar lnga re phul ba dang / rta nag sgrol sbug tu brgya mchod dang dgon par mang ja/ byang chub gling dgon stod smad gnyis su brgya mchod dang / bla mar bsngo
rten dang / grwa btsun re rer 'gyed skar lnga re dang / rab brtan chos lung du'ang mang ja 'gyed bcas dang / paN chen shAkya mchog ldan pa'i gdan sa thub bstan gser
mdog can du brgya mchod dang / dgon par mang ja 'gyed skar lnga re dang / dpal ldan sa skya'i gdan sa rtse gdong chos sder rnam gsum brgya mchod dang / 'dus tshogs su mang
jas bsnyen bkur ba dang / 'gyed grwa pa rer dngul skar lnga re dang / dpyal lo sogs kyi gdan sa thar pa dgon dang / pa rnam dga' ba gdong / nyang stod spyid sbug bcas su
brgya mchod dang / bla ma so sor bsngo zhus/ 'dus tshogs su mang ja gnyis re dang / rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sder rnam lnga brgya mchod dang / 'dus tshogs su mang ja
dang / mkhan por bsngo zhus dang / de'i nang gses gur pa grwa tshang du rnam lnga brgya mchod dang / bla mar bsngo rten/ 'dus tshogs su mang ja gsum dang phyag 'gyed grwa
rer dngul zho re/ mus gle lung chos sder brgya mchod dang mang ja 'gyed bcas/ mus kyi spru byang chub gling du mang ja 'gyed bcas/ gtum ston blo gros grags kyis btab pa'i
dpal snar thang gi chos sde dang / dgon pa byang / lhun po rtse/ gangs can chos sde/ khro phu/ gnas chos sde/ bo dong chos sde/ bya gshong / snying ri'i sgrub sde khag
/gnas phur mo chos rdzong

gi sgrub sde khag /dben sgang ri khrod pa/ srad chos 'khor gling rnams su mang ja dang bla ma so sor bsngo zhus/ rten gsum so sor brgya mchod bcas dang / srad rgyud pa dang
/ srad dgon khra/ shangs rgya mtsho dgon/ 'bras yul skyed mos tshal rnams kyi rten gsum so sor brgya mchod dang / bla ma so sor bsngo zhus/ 'dus tshogs so sor mang ja dang
/ 'gyed grwa pa re rer dngul skar lnga re bcas phul ba dang / dbus phyogs su jo shAka rnam gnyis kyi gtsos rten gsum khyad par du 'phags pa rnams kyi spyan sngar mchod
'bul gyi rten du bod dngul rdo tshad gcig bskur ba dang / gzhan yang bdun tshigs gnyis pa rdzogs pa'i rjes su/ spyir khang steng la sogs par sa chog ma byas kyang chog mod/
byas kyang 'gal ba med par sems nas sa chog mdor bsdus sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas gdung khang myang 'das mchod rten gyi dbyibs su brtsigs pa dang / sbyin sreg kyang 'byor
pas lcogs na gsum bzhi sogs byas kyang 'gal ba med par sems nas/ 'og tu kun rig dang / de steng rgya lcog gi steng du dpal kye rdo rje'i sbyin sreg gi dkyil 'khor bris
pa dang / sngar kye rdo rje'i sgo nas sku gdung rin po cher gnas yig gdags pa dang / rnam snang dges pa rdo rjer bskyed pa sogs grub zin pa yin na'ang / kun rig gi sngon
'gro'i rdo rje sems dpar bskyed pa dang / gnas yig gdags pa sogs bgyis pa dang / de nub mchod pa'i bye brag 'ga' zhig dang bcas te sku gdung rin po che gdung khang du
spyan drangs pa dang / de'i phyi nyin hor zla lnga pa'i tshes gnyis kyi tho rangs tsam nas lung rig smra ba'i dbang phyug khang gsar mkhan rin po che ngag dbang bsod nams
rgyal mtshan tshogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon chen por spyan drangs te/ bsnyen pa song ba'i dge slong bcu phrag gcig dang bcas pas dpal dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgo

nas sku gdung rin po cher zhugs 'bul ba dang / bstan pa'i snang byed bla ma bstan pa dar rgyas kyi dbu byas pa'i dge slong brgyad kyis bcom ldan 'das kun tu rig pa'i sgo nas
sku gdung rin po cher zhugs 'bul ba'i zhabs tog rgyud sde nas ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin du bsgrubs shing / de nyin tho rangs nas bzung nam mkha' thams cad kha dog sna tshogs
pa'i sprin gyis gang ba zhig ni nges par 'dug cing / dgon pa'i grwa pa phal cher zhig gis ni da nangs tho rangs 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan rtsa ba gcig pa shar ngos su bstan
cing rtse mo mang por gyes pa nub phyogs su zug pa zhig shar song ba de lta bu ni sngar mkhan chen rdo rjai 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi gdung bzhu'i skabs
kyi 'ja' yis kyang cha shas tsam yang 'gran par mi gzod ces gleng 'dug pa dang / thog mar zhugs 'bul ba'i tshe me rang 'bar lta bu'i shin tu 'bar sla ba dang / de dus kyi
dud pa ni/ thog mar gdung khang gi steng du 'khyil ba snyam byed cing / de nas dud pa rnams dgon pa'i nub ngos kyi nam mkhar song zhing / de nas dgon pa la g.yon skor
lan cig byas nas/ mthar nam mkha'i 'ja' sprin rnams dang dbyer med du 'dres pa'i tshul gyis yal bar gyur ces zer ba dang / me lce rnams kyang kha dog dkar gsal 'od dang ldan
zhing / gzhan du 'khyag 'khyog med par rtse mo rnams rtswa ljang gshibs pa ltar gyen kho nar 'bar ba'i ya mtshan pa dang / skabs skabs su bkra shis pa'i ri mo'i dbyibs
