lta bur 'bar ba dang / bsreg rdzas rnams 'bul ma tshar gong nas sku gdung rin po cher me bzhes grub pa'i shin tu sla ba dang / khyad par dri zhim pos dgon pa'i gling thams
cad la khyab pa ni skye bo mtha' dag la mngon sum tshad mas grub pa nyid do/ /de nyin mkhan rin po che khri thog pa'i mdun gser zangs las grub pa'i gong ma dbang sdud
snying po'i snang brnyan dang / dngul gyi 'bru par/ zangs bum kha mchu zhabs gsum dngul las grub pa/ phyag ting

dngul thag can dang / gser Dar dngul shan ma/ rol mo cha/ mdzod gos dmar ser gyis shan pa'i sku sbyar me long ma/ srab ther gyi chos gos/ le na'i sku gzan/ zhabs lhwam 'ja'
chen/ nam thong phyar ba/ ja 'khor drug gnyis/ 'bras do sogs phul ba dang / bla ma bstan par nang gos kyi stod rtse dang / ja sbag gnyis sogs phul ba dang / de bying thams
cad la'ang rnam gzhag dang yon 'bul la sogs pa shin tu zab par bgyis so/ /de nas mchod pa dang bcas te zhag bdun song ba'i mthar gdung khang zhal phye ba na/ gdung rus
ni mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi skabs ltar nyung tsam zhig las ma mchis so/ /de'i rjes su rgyud sde rnams nas ji ltar bshad pa bzhin gyis
gdung rus rnams btus te dpal kye rdo rje'i sgo nas bsgrubs pa'i bum chus sku khrus gsol ba dang / dpal kun rig gi rtsa rig 'bum phrag 'gro nges bgyis pa'i bum chus yang yang
sku khrus gsol zhing / slar gdung rus rnams zhib par btags te rin po che'i phye ma dang / dri zhim po'i chus sprus pa'i 'jim pa gtsang ma dang lhan cig tu bsres te/ 'jim
pa byin rlabs sngon du 'gro bas bla ma yi dam sangs rgyas byang sems chos srung nor lha dang bcas pa'i sku 'dra mang du spar btab cing de rnams la'ang rab tu gnas pa
brgya tshar 'gro nges bgyis pa dang / yang gdung thal rnams la'ang gdung rus shin tu zhib pa phran bu 'dres snang bas de dag kyang shin tu zhib par btags shing dri zhim po'i
chus sprus pa'i 'jim pa dang bsres te/ 'jim pa byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas rigs lnga'i sa bon dang / gtsug tor dri med kyi gzungs dang / rten 'brel snying po
bcas kyi gzungs gzhug dang ldan pa'i sAtstsha khri phrag brgyad lhag tsam bzhengs shing / de thams cad la'ang rab tu gnas pa bgyis pa

dang / khyad par lo de'i hor zla brgyad pa'i nang phyi rten khang bu brtsegs pa'i mchon rten bzhengs par/ thog mar sa chog mdor bsdus dang / sa bdag lto 'phye'i thig dang /
gter bum gzhug pa sogs sngon du 'gro bas mchod rten gyi phyags tshad rnams ngor chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras kyi bzhed pa ji lta ba bzhin du bgyis pa dang / de'i nang du'ang
mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i srog shing la ji skad bshad pa ltar gyi gzungs gzhug pa dang / 'bri ba sogs dang / khyad par bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan 'bum nas bzung / chos
srung nor lha dang bkra shis kyi bar thams cad kyi go rim ma 'phyugs pa gong ma'i phyag len ji lta ba bzhin dang / 'og tu gnod sbyin 'khor lo dang nor lha'i gter bum bcas
dang / khyad par sAtstsha rnams kyang yongs su rdzogs pa bzhugs su gsol zhing / de dag kyang sa rdo spungs pa lta bu ma yin par re re nas pad spungs mchod rten shar du
bstan te bsgrigs pa dang / star re bsgrigs tshar ba'i rjes su sAtstsha rab gnas mdor bsdus re'ang bgyis pa dang / de dag gi bar thams cad kyang gsang dang shug phye kho
nas bkang ba sogs mdor na tshul bzhin du bzhengs pa'i mchod rten la dge slong bcus tshe dpag tu med pa la brten pa'i rab tu gnas pa bgyis pa dang / yang hor zla lnga pa'i
mjug nas bzung ste rta nag lha bris pas gtsug lag khang du bsham rgyu'i dus thang rin po che che legs shin tu sgros gtsang ba zla ba gsum dang zhag lnga'i bar du bzhengs
te/ gong gsham zhal khebs sogs kyang phun sum tshogs par bgyis pa dang / yang rtse gdong nas bzo rig mkhas pa mi bzhi bos te hor zla dgu pa'i tshes brgyad nas bzung / nang
rten 'dra sku rin po che gser zangs las grub pa sku dngos mda' tshad tsam khri rgyab dang bcas pa dang / rin chen gnyis pa 'degs srang brgyad cu las grub pa'i padma spungs
pa'i mchod rten mda' tshad tsam pa la rin po che du ma'i phras

mdzes par spud pa bcas kyang zla ba gsum gyi khongs su shin tu sgros gtsang bar bzhengs grub pa la yungs 'bru lta bu'i ring bsrel dang / sku 'dra li ma dang / byin rten khyad
par du 'phags pa 'ga' zhig dang / srog shing mtshan nyid dang ldan pa dang / bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan nyid 'bum nas bzung ste bkra shis kyi bar rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel
ba'i gzungs bsam las 'das pa dang / sku gdung yid bzhin nor bu'i cha shas las grub pa'i sku 'dra rnams kyis phyur bur bkang ste/ tshul bzhin du bsgrubs pa'i nor lha'i
gter bum dang / gnod sbyin 'khor los zhabs bsdams pa'i bar rje btsun gong ma'i phyag len ji lta ba bzhin bgyis pa yin no/ /de dag gi tshe bzo bo thams cad la'ang 'dzugs
ston dang / bar ston dang / gser ston dang / grol ston sogs shin tu zab pa dang / rgyun gyi bza' btung phun sum tshogs pa dang / yon dang gnang sbyin la sogs pas shin tu
yid tshim par bgyis so/ /de dag gi skabs su'ang bar chad kyi rnam pa cung zad tsam yang med cing / mthun rkyen rnams kyang 'bad rtsol cher mi dgos par shugs kyis 'grig pa
sogs mdor na tshegs chung ngus bde blag tu grub pa ni rje nyid kyi thugs rje kho na yin par gdon mi za'o/ /gzhan yang zhi bar gshegs pa nas bzung / deng sang gi bar phal
che bar zla re bzhin dus chen dang bstun te dge slong kha shas kyis bla ma mchod pa ma chag par bgyis pa dang / khyad par bshad ma thag pa'i dus thang dang / 'dra sku dang
/ dngul gdung rnams la thog mar bdag cag dge slong bcus tshe dpag tu med pa la brten pa'i rab tu gnas pa nyin gang ma zhig bgyis pa dang / de rjes shing glang sa ga zla
ba'i tshes gcig nas bzung / bdag cag dge slong bcu gcig gis dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub mchod dang 'brel bar bzang po drug ldan gyi rab
tu gnas pa shin tu rgyas pa nyin bdun pa

zhig bgyis pa dang / de dag gi tshe'ang nyin re bzhin rnam gsum brgya mchod dang bcas pa'i mchod pa shin tu rgyas pa dang / dge 'dun rnams la'ang bsnyen bkur phul du phyin
pa bsgrubs pa dang / khyad par zla ba de'i tshes bcu'i nyin dge slong rags bsdus kyi ser sbreng dang bcas te 'dra sku rin po che dang / dus thang gnyis lam 'bras lha khang
dang / gtsug lag khang du gdan drangs te/ de'ang 'dra sku rin po cher nang gos dmar ser las grub pa'i snam sbyar la sogs pa'i na bzas bklubs te lam 'bras lha khang du bzhugs
su gsol zhing / de'i sku mdun rin chen gnyis pa 'degs srang bzhi dang zho brgyad las grub pa'i phud kong dang / dngul srang lnga dang zho brgyad las grub pa'i spyi
blugs dang / dngul srang lnga dang zho gsum las grub pa'i 'bru bar dang / dngul srang bcu gcig dang zho lnga las grub pa'i dkar 'dzin gyi steng zhal dkar yu ring zas snas
bkang ba dang / dngul srang bdun dang zho do las grub pa'i bzed zhal dang / dngul srang bco brgyad las grub pa'i bum pa cha la kha rgyan bum gos dang bcas pa dang / rdol
dril gser mgo can dang / Da ma ru dngul dkris can dang / phyag ting dngul thag can dang / dngul thod khebs stegs gser zangs las grub pa rnams sbyor 'jags zhus pa dang /
de nyin nas bzung nyin lnga la nyin re bzhin rnam lnga brgya mchod dang bcas te lam 'bras lha khang du dge slong bcu res bla ma mchod pa bgyis par bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs
pa bsgrubs pa dang / yang tshes bcu nas bzung nyin gsum la e wa~M pa'i gtsug lag khang du nyin re bzhin rnam gsum brgya mchod dang bcas te dge 'dun gang yod kyis bla
ma mchod pa tshogs par nyin gnyis la grwa pa rer phyag 'gyed dngul Tam phyed re phul ba dang / nyin gcig la grwa pa rer dngul Tam re phul ba sogs bsnyen bkur shin tu bzang
bar bgyis pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i dus kyi

tshe'ang / thog mar dgung zhag skabs kyi bdun re re rdzogs mtshams su res nyi gur phub pa dang / res 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan shar ba sogs ma chad par byung zhing / rab gnas
kyi skabs kyang 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan 'dra shar ba dang / 'dra sku rin po che dang dus thang bcas bla brang gzhung du gdan drangs pa'i skabs kyang glo bur du 'ja' kha dog
lnga ldan shar ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas kyang 'ga' re byung ngo / /gzhan yang snga phyir e wa~M pa'i bla brang khag rnams dang / thar rtse rang gi grwa tshang dang
ltos rigs rnams nas gdung 'bul byung ba thams cad kyang gong gi dge tshogs rnams su smin nges zhus pa yin cing / gzhan phyogs tha dad pa nas mgon po gang gi thugs sras su
gyur pa rnams kyis zab dgongs dbyings su rdzogs pa'i slad du legs byas kyi sgo 'phar yangs por phyes pa'i tshul rnams ni re re nas smos kyis mi lang ngo / /mdor na bdag
cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa mkhas dang grub pa yongs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba 'di'i phyogs su bdag cag rnams kyi lus longs spyod dus gsum bsags pa'i dge tshogs dang bcas
pa thams cad bskal pa brgya phrag mang por nyin re bzhin bye ba phrag mang po btang yang bka' drin gyi cha shas tsam yang 'tsho bar mi nus mod/ 'on kyang re zhig bdag cag
rnams kyi nus pa ni de tsam du zad do/ /de ltar kun rdzob tu gdul bya tshu rol mthong ba rnams kyi snang ngor yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po'i tshul bstan par gyur
mod/ mgon po gang gi thugs rje la skyo ba dang dub pa mi mnga' shing / gdul bar bya ba'i sems can la'ang mu dang mtha' med pa'i phyi dus 'khor ba ji srid gnas pa de srid
kyi bar du gdul bya rnams kyi khams dang bsam pa dang bag la nyal dang rjes su mthun par sprul pa sna tshogs pa'i sgo nas sems can gyi don rgyun mi 'chad par 'bad med
lhun grub tu 'byung

ba yin te chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po ches/ 'khor ba ji srid gnas kyi bar/ /rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyis/ /de srid de yi don mdzad pa/ /phrin las dbang phyug la
phyag 'tshal/ /ces gsungs pa ltar dang / rgyud bla ma las kyang / gdul bya'i khams dang 'dul ba'i thabs dang ni/ /gdul bya'i khams kyi 'dul ba'i bya ba dang / /de yi yul
dang dus su gshegs pa la/ /khyab bdag rtag tu lhun gyis grub par 'jug /ces gsungs pa ltar ro/ /kye ma skye rgu'i bsod nams ni/ /'bab chu zad pa'i rdzing bzhin te/ /'dren
pa lan cig rnyed pa yang / /gzigs pa gzhan du phyogs par gyur/ /ji bzhin gzigs pa'i chu gter ni/ /snying rje'i dri bzhon gyis bsrubs te/ /tshad mar gyur pa'i tshig gi zla/
/'gro 'di'i blo mun sel phyir spros/ /bden pa'i gsung gi bsil zer gyis/ /'gro 'di'i rab rib kun bsal yang / /slar yang som nyi'i mun spro ba'i/ /kye ma 'gro ba'i las
'di ci/ /gzod nas skye rga na 'chi bzhi'i/ /rba klong 'khrugs pa'i chu gter las/ /brgal yang 'gro 'di 'khor ba las/ /yid 'byung slad du bsnyun tshul bstan/ /dkar phyogs bdud
rtsi ltar bgyid pa'i/ /lha rnams mya ngan khur 'dzin cing / /rgyal kun mgon med la gzigs pa'i/ /spyan ni snying rje'i chu yis brlan/ /de mthong bdag cag rnams kyi snying
/ /dum bur mi 'gas rdo rje'am ci/ /'on te yid srubs dpung tshogs kyis/ /rig sngags byin pa yong mi shes/ /rgyal gsung thabs tshul sna tshogs kyis/ /rtsa gsum lha yi byin
bskul yang / /lung bstan bden pa'i ri mo ni/ /nam yang zub pa nyid ma gyur/ /nam zhig 'gro 'di'i bden 'dzin gyi/ /'khri shing drung nas 'byin pa'i slad/ /bde stong zung

'jug ting 'dzin ro/ /zhag gsum bar du rnam par myangs/ /de nas mtha' gnyis spangs pa yi/ /grub pa'i dge mtshan brnyes bzhin du/ /rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa dang / /lhan cig
mchog gi grong du gshegs/ /kye ma blang dor ston byed pa'i/ /smra ba'i nyi ma nub gyur pas/ /gangs ljongs 'gro 'di gling bar gyi/ /mun pa'i nang du lhung ba bzhin/ /kyi
hud 'khor ba'i nad 'phrog pa'i/ /chos kyi sman pa de bshegs pas/ /srid pa'i zug rngus mnar ba yi/ /gangs can 'gro 'di mgon med gyur/ /ma la rin chen snang ba dang / /nyi
zla'i 'od kyis mi sel ba'i/ /bzod du med pa'i mya ngan gyi/ /mun pa che 'di su yis byas / /kyi hud glang pos chu skyes rnams/ /bcom pa'i padmo'i rdzing bzhin du/ /mya ngan
me lces yid bsregs pa'i/ /bdag cag gdung ba ngan song bzhin/ /mgon khyod gzod nas 'gro ba la/ /phan pa sgrub par dam bcas rdzun/ /gzhan du khyod la brten pa yi/ /mya ngan
khur 'di ga las 'ong / /ngo mtshar sgyu ma'i tshon ris kyis/ /skal bzang spro ba skyed bsrings kyang / /mgon bral bdag cag rnams kyi snying / /lhag par mya ngan tsher
mas gdungs/ /'on kyang 'khor 'das chos thams cad/ /sems kyi cho 'phrul yin zhes gsungs/ /de phyir dam pa'i don nyid du/ /gshegs bzhugs 'du 'bral yod ma yin/ /don 'di bdag
cag rnams kyi yid/ /dbugs 'byin stsol ba'i sman gyi mchog /'khrul pa gcod pa'i stwa re dang / /byin rlabs 'gugs pa'i pho nya'ang yin/ /yid bzhin nor dang dpag bsam gyi/
/khengs pa'i ri bo snyil byed pa'i/ /'gro 'di'i bsod nams zhing mchog tu/ /bzhag pa'i sku gdung rin po cher/ /rgyal ba 'gro la phan mdzad kyis/ /rgyud du ji skad gsungs pa

ltar/ /sri zhu'i bya ba thams cad kyang / /tshogs gnyis rdzogs pa'i slad du bsgrubs/ /gangs can skye rgu'i bsod nams kyis/ /mgron du nye bar khug pa yi/ /dbus gtsang ljongs
kyi rten gsum dang / /bla ma dge 'dun bcas rnams la/ /mchod dang bsnyen bkur bstabs pa yi/ /bsod nams zla shes gzhon nu'i 'od/ /sngon bsags sdig pa'i mun pa rnams/ /zil
gyis gnon la chas pa bzhin/ /dad pa'i nor gyis rgyud phyug pa'i/ /skal bzang thar par chas rnams kyis/ /bsod nams gsog pa'i zhing mchog tu/ /ngo mtshar 'bar ba'i rten rnams
bzhengs/ /'bad rtsol med par yid bzhin du/ /rjes kyi bya ba kun 'grub pa/ /mgon khyod byin rlabs mthu kho nar/ /nges pa'i ka ba snying la tshugs/ /tshur mthong gdul bya
'dul ba'i slad/ /mdzad pa'i tha ma 'di bstan yang / /don dam 'khor ba ma stong bar/ /de srid 'gro don rgyun mi 'chad/ /phyogs 'di'i mgon med gdul bya la/ /rjes brtse'i
shing rtas nyer drangs te/ /sprul pa'i zla gzhon myur shar nas/ /phan bde'i ku mud rgyas par mdzod/ /sngon byon rgyal ba thams cad kyis/ /bsgral bar ma nus bdag lta bu'i/
/'gro rnams deng nas byang chub bar/ /khyod kyis rjes su 'dzin gyur cig /de mthus tshe rabs thams cad du/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i sgor zhugs shing / /byang chub spyod mchog
rgya mtsho yis/ /don gnyis myur du 'grub par shog/ //de ltar dzam bu'i rkang 'thung gis nye bar mtshan pa'i ljongs 'dir phan bde'i nyi ma gsar du 'char ba'i slad du
bsam bzhin du sku'i skye ba bzhes pa bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po'i zhal snga
nas kyi rtogs pa brjod pa so so skye bo'i blo yi spyod yul du gyur pa rnams re zhig

bkod zin to// //slar smras pa/ ngo mtshar mkhyen brtse nus pa'i chu klung ji snyed gcig tu 'khyil ba las/ /ngo mtshar bshad sgrub dpag bsam ljon pa sngon med gsar du skyed
bsrings pas/ /ngo mtshar phan bde'i 'dod rgu sbyin la tsintA ma Nis mtshon min pa/ /ngo mtshar mi zad du ma'i gter gyur dpal ldan bla mar phyag bgyi'o/ /gang gi rnam thar
yon tan rin chen gter/ /yid 'phrog don gyi ltad mo 'bum 'byin pa/ /de kun tshig gi srad bur brgyu ba la/ /rgyal ba rnams kyang ngal ba'i rnam pa 'dzin/ /'on kyang bdag blo'i
khab kyi bu ga ru/ /chud pa'i rtogs brjod phra rab rdul lta bu/ /'di gtan phongs pa'i gdung ba sel ba gang / /sdeb legs tshig gi rgyal mtshan rtse la bkod/ /'di na gang
mtshan rna bar lhung ba yang / /skye ba brgya phrag mang por rnyed dka' na/ /rnam thar dran bzhin gsol ba btab pa'i mod/ /rnam grol 'dod rgu sbyin la som nyi ci/ /de
slad 'khor bas byas pa'i dpal 'byor rnams/ /skad cig mi gnas klog gi thag pa ltar/ /mthong na zhi ba'i nags klung bsten byed pa'i/ /thar 'dod dad pa'i gsos su 'di longs shig
/'dir 'bad dge tshogs spos kyi glang po yis/ /ma rungs 'khor ba'i g.yul ngo rab bcom nas/ /drin gyis lci ba'i yid can kun khyer te/ /byang chub snying po'i grong du 'jug
gyur cig /dpal ldan bla ma dam pa gsum gyi rtogs pa brjod pa ngo mtshar me tog g.yo ba'i 'khri shing byin rlabs 'dod rgu'i 'byung gnas las/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang
rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyi rtogs pa brjaud pa'i yal 'dab ste gsum pa'o//

//da ni rtsom pa mthar phyin te 'jug gi bya ba tshigs su bcad pa 'ga' zhig slob dpon daNDI'i zhabs kyi gzhung lugs kyi tambu ra'i rgyud las drangs te smras pas/ oM swa sti
siddhaM/ rgyal ba las kyang drin gyis lhag pa'i skyabs kun 'dus zhal bla ma dang / /gzhan yang yi dam rgyal ba sras dang slob mar bcas pa'i tshogs mtha' dag /mi phyed dad
gsum gser las grub pa'i gzhal med khang chen 'dir spyon la/ /ji ltar smon pa'i don rnams 'grub pa'i dge mtshan me tog bsnyil bar gsol/ 1 /bgrang du med pa'i bskal pa rgya
mtshor tshogs gnyis them skas la 'dzegs te/ /mi gnas myang 'das nor bu'i khri la zhabs kyi padmo rnam bkod kyang / /namaX mkhaX' dang mnyam yid can ma lus 'chi med grong
du bkri ba'i slad/ /ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i rnam par rol der slar yang dad pas phyag bgyi'o/ 2 /khyad par byams brtse dri yi gzhon paXs rgyal rnams ye shes chu yi gter/ /yang
yang bsrubs las 'di na kunaX dgaX'i mtshan dpe'i cha shas rab rdzogs shing / /zab rgyas chos kyi snang ba 'bum sdes bstan 'gro'i ku mud bzhad mdzad pa'i/ /yongs 'dzin
smra ba'i zla ba gang der dad pas gus phyag nyin bzhin brtsegs/ 3 /mkhyen pa'i ye shes lha lam ngogs su snying rje'i sprin dkar rab bkod de/ /gsang ba sngags kyi rnalaX
'byoraX zab mo'i bdud rtsi'i gru char phab pa las/ /rnam par grol ba'i lo tog skyed la 'jaXm dpaXl dbyangs dang dbyer med cing / /mkhas btsun bzaXng po'i gtsug gi rgyan
gyur gang der slar yang phyag bgyi'o/ 4 /gzhan yang zab rgyas chos tshul rgya mtsho'i rin chen do shal g.yo ba yis/ /bdag blo phongs pa'i gdung ba sel mdzad dpal ldan bla
ma'i tshogs rnams dang / /rab 'byams skyabs yul rgya mtsho'i 'dun sar zhing gi rdul rnyed lus sprul te/ /

gsol 'debs ngag gi rol mo 'khrol bzhin dad pas gus phyag nyin bzhin stob/ 5 /'di na bdag blo dad pa'i gru bo brtson 'grus rlung gis bskyod pa las/ /rnam thar mi zad nor bu'i
gling nas thun mong dag tu rab grags pa'i/ /rtogs brjod rin chen nyung shas blangs gang thar 'dod dad pa'i gsos nyid du / sdeb legs tshig gi phreng bar spel ba'i legs byas
rmad byung 'dis mtshon te/ 6 /rang lus longs spyod dus gsum bsags pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ji snyed pa/ /rnam par ri gling nyi zla dang bcas bye phrag bsam gyis mi khyab
par/ /sprul pa'i ltad mo gsar du ngoms 'dis tshangs pa'i khegs pa snyil byed cing / /kun bzang mchod pa'i spun zlar gyur gang dgyes pa'i spyan zur lhung phyir 'bul/ 7 /gang
gi rnam thar sgro skur spangs te rang bzhin brjod pa'i rgyan nyid du/ /spel ba'i legs bshad bdud rtsi'i rdzing 'dir blo ngan rdul gyis bslad pa yi/ /nongs pa gang mchis
'phags rnams 'dun sar stobs bzhi nor bu ke ta kas/ /yang yang yid kyi rnyog ma bgrungs na dwang ba'i dga' ston ci yang stsol/ 8 /zho 'thung rus pas bdar du med cing chu
bo'i rgyun gyis mi 'dag pa'i/ /thog ma med pa'i dus nas bsags pa'i sdig ltung dri ma stug po yis/ /rang sems bde gshegs snying po'i khams kyi mdzes pa rab tu sma phab pa/
/slar la stobs bzhi'i chu yis bkrus las dag pa'i dge mtshan lhag par ngoms/ 9 /'phags bod mkhas dang grub pa yongs kyi phrin las gcig tu bsdus 'dra ba'i/ /dpal ldan bla
ma dam pa gsum gy-i rnam thar rmad du byung bas mtshon/ /srid dang zhi ba'i legs spyad ji snyed nyin mor byed pa'i gzi 'od la/ /rjes su yi rangs padmo'i 'dab rgya rnam
par grol ba'i mtshar sdug g.yo/ 10 /phyogs bcu rab 'byams mu med zhing na chos ston ji snyed bzhugs kun gyi/ /

phul byung byams dang snying rje'i phyag ni ring por rkyong pa'i rol rtsed kyis/ /theg gsum dam pa'i chos kyi rnga chen rgyun chad med par brdungs pa'i sgras/ /'gro kun ma
rig gnyid las bslangs te thar pa'i grong du bkri bar gsol/ 11 /gang na dam chos snang ba gsar pas 'khor ba'i mun pa snyil byed cing / /dge legs mtha' dag cig car sbyin pa'i
rnam 'dren da lta bzhugs pa kun/ /slar yang gsang gsum tshe dpag med ltar bskal pa zhing gi rdul rnyed par/ /'tsho gzhes cho ga rab tu brtan pa'i dga' ston ches cher dar
bar shog 12 /dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams kyi mtshan tsam zhig kyang thos dka' na/ /phyogs re'i rnam thar cung zad brjod pa'ang sngon bsags mthu las rnyed pa ste/ /de
slad dad dang spro ba mchog gis legs spyad don ldan 'di spel ba'i/ /dge tshogs dri med kha ba dung dang ku mu dA ltar dkar bas mtshon/ 13 /'khor dang myang 'das gnyis kyis
bsdus shing dus gsum kun tu bsags pa yi/ /lus ngag yid dang rjes su 'brel ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ji snyed pa/ /gzhan phan sems dang 'khor gsum mi rtog shes rab zab mo'i
thabs mkhas kyis/ /bla na med pa'i byang chub snying por yongs su bsngo ba'i g.yar dam len/ 14 /de mthus phan dang bde ba'i rtsa lag lung dang rtogs pas bsdus pa yi/ /thub
pa'i dbang po'i bstan pa spyi dang bye brag rje btsun sa skya pa'i/ /ring lugs 'khrul pa'i dri ma kun zad 'khor ba ma stongs de srid du/ /dbyar gyi mtshos kyang 'gran
du med par phyogs dus kun tu rgyas par shog 15 /de 'dzin sngon byon dam par rnams kyi zab dgongs dbyings su rdzogs gyur cing / /da lta bzhugs pa'i skyes chen kun kyang nam
mkha' ji srid gnas kyi bar/ /gsang gsum 'tsho gzhes rab tu brtan cing mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam gsum gyis/ /sa gsum kun dga'i

dpal la sbyor ba'i dge mtshan snang bar 'bar gyur cig 16 /bla gos dmar po'i 'od rdul stug pos thun mtshams chu 'dzin zil gnon pa'i/ /'dus pa rnams kyang tshul khrims phung
po rang gi srog las gces par lta/ /thos bsam bsgom pa'i lang tsho rab rdzogs 'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i gzi 'od kyis/ /nyes pa'i ra ri yongs su 'phrog bzhin gong nas gong du
'phel bar shog 17 /bde gshegs bstan pa'i gdugs dkar rab g.yo phan bde'i grib bsil 'jo ba gang / /snying stobs dpung pas srid rtser 'degs la gsang bdag rjes su rkang 'jog
pa'i/ /bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chen po kun gyi tshe bsod dpal 'byor snyan grags sogs/ /legs pa'i yon tan yar ngo'i zla bzhin gong nas gong du 'phel bar shog 18 /chos ldan rgyal
po'i bka' yi spring yig phyogs kyi rgyal phran mgo bo la/ /rnam par 'god pa'i ngo mtshar rab g.yo dge bcu'i khrims kyi ra ba na/ /skye rgu mtha' dag bde bar tshud cing
kun kyang rdzogs ldan dus bzhin du/ /sde bzhi'i dpal la ci dgar spyod pa'i dge mtshan dar la babs gyur cig 19 /sdug bsngal brgya phrag du mas rab gtses khams gsum sems
can thams cad kyang / 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rgyu dang bcas pa dug can zas bzhin rab spangs nas/ /phar phyin drug dang bsdu dngos bzhi sogs byang chub spyod mchog la zhugs
te/ /sku bzhi ye shes lnga dang ldan pa'i go 'phang myur du thob gyur cig 20 /bdag kyang deng nas tshe rabs kun tu mtshungs med dge ba'i bshes rnams kyis/ /rjes bzung
yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i sgor zhugs thos bsam sgom pa mthar phyin zhing / /'chad rtsod rtsom pas bstan dang 'gro la phan pa rgya chen rab bsgrubs nas/ /ring min thams cad
mkhyen pa'i go 'phang bde blag nyid du thob par shog 21 /de ltar lhag

bsam skyed mos tshal las mngon par 'dod pa'i me tog rnams/ /spro ba mchog gis legs par btus nas sdeb legs tshig gi srad bu la/ /mdzes par brgyus pa'i thar 'dod rgyan 'di skyabs
yul rgya mtsho'i byin mthu yis/ /gegs kyi sbyor bas nam yang rnying min 'dod don 'bras bu g.yur za shog 22 /bkra shis gang zhig bskal mang rnyed dka'i bde stong gnyis
su med pa yi/ /lhan skyes ye shes nor bu'i snye ma skad cig nyid la lag pa'i rtser/ /sbyin mkhas skyabs kun 'dus pa'i ngo bo dpal ldan bla ma'i tshogs rnams kyi/ /bkra
shis byin rlabs snang ba gsar pas srid zhi'i khams kun khyab gyur cig 23 /de ltar dpal ldan bla ma dam pa gsum gyi rtogs pa brjod pa ngo mtshar me tog g.yo ba'i 'khri shing
byin rlabs 'dod rgu'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba 'di 'ang / snga mo nas snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas rje bla
ma dam pa 'di gsum gyi rtogs brjod cig nges par ma byung thabs med du dgongs nas rnam thar zhig ljags rtsom stsal rgyu'i thugs bzhed yod pa'i khar/ bdag gis kyang gsol
ba btab pas khyod kyis rgyus yod kyi tho dzar zhig byung tshe de bzhin bya'o zhes zhal bzhes thob par gyur na'ang / de rjes gus phran rang le lo dang snyom las kho na'i
gzhan dbang du song nas tho dzar de bri ma thub par yun ring por song ba'i mthar/ slar yang snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa mchog gi zhal nas/ kho bo'ang 'chad rtsod rtsom
gsum dang / skabs skabs su yi dam lha'i bsnyen pa 'dra bya dgos pa bcas kyi brel g.yeng kho nas re zhig rnam thar 'bri ba'i long med pa lta bur gyur pas/ da ni rnam
par thar pa de khyod kyis bris shig ces bka' stsal rin po che gser gyi con pan lta bu spyi bor stsal ba la brten gyen ldog ma spobs par rigs dang dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i

khyab bdag bka' drin mtshungs zla ma mchis pa mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang /
mkhas dang grub pa yongs kyi gtsug rgyan bka' drin gzhal bar dka' ba mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / kun mkhyen bu ston gnyis
pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / nyams dang rtogs pa'i mthar son zhabs drung rin po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal
mtshan la sogs pa yongs 'dzin dam pa bka' drin can rnams kyi zhabs rdul spyi bos blangs te gsung gi bdud rtsis 'tsho zhing / khyad par du'ang rtsod dus kyi thams cad
mkhyen pa 'dzam gling byang phyogs kyi thub dbang gnyis pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po dang / gnas lnga rig pa'i mkhas pa chen po mdo sngags bstan pa'i srog
shing 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub pa gnyis kyi bka' drin la brten nas phyi nang rig pa'i gnas la blo gros kyi padmo cung zad kha bye ba shAkya'i dge slong byams
pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan nam/ ming gzhan 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i seng ge mtsho byung dga' ba'i bshes gnyen du bod pa'am/ 'jam dpal dgyes pa'i bshes gnyen gtsug
lag smra ba'i nyi ma phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba'i sde zhes kyang bgyi bas rnam g.yeng dang le lo'i gseb tshags rnams su rim gyis bris te/ rab byung bcu bzhi
pa'i nang gses lcags mo bya'i lor thams cad bris zin pa yin na'ang / slar yang mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnam gnyis dgongs pa zhi dbyings su gzigs pa'i tshul rnams kyang
kha bskangs te yongs su rdzogs par rab byung bco lnga pa'i thog ma legs sbyar gyi skad du pra bha wa zhes pa bod skad du rab byung ste rgya rtsis pas me mo yos kyi

lo/ nag pa zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi rgyal ba dang po'i nyin yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi bla brang thar pa rtser grub par bgyis pa 'dis
kyang bdag sogs sems can thams cad kyi rgyud la dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams kyi byin rlabs myur du 'jug pa'i rgyur gyur cig/ //shu bha mastu sarba dza ga tAM// //
